anurudhyeta karmaṇi etān vegān vinayet vai tapasvī nindā ca asya hṛdayam na upahanyāt madhyasthaḥ eva tiṣṭheta praśaṃsā nindayoḥ samaḥ mahātmā su vrataḥ dāntaḥ sarvatra eva anapāśritaḥ apūrva cārakaḥ saumyaḥ aniketaḥ samāhitaḥ vānaprastha gṛhasthābhyām na saṃsṛjyeta karhi cit ajñāta lipsām lipseta na ca enam harṣaḥ āviśet vijānatām mokṣaḥ eṣa śramaḥ syāt a vijānatām mokṣayānam idam kṛtsnam viduṣām hāritaḥ abravīt yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca prāpya jātim manuṣyeṣu devaiḥ api pitāmaha kadā vayam kariṣyāmaḥ saṃnyāsam duḥkha saṃjñakam duḥkham etat śarīrāṇām dhāraṇam kurusattama vimuktāḥ saptadaśabhiḥ hetu bhūtaiḥ ca pañcabhiḥ indriya arthaiḥ guṇaiḥ ca eva aṣṭābhiḥ prapitāmaha na gacchanti punarbhāvam munayaḥ saṃśita vratāḥ kadā vayam bhaviṣyāmaḥ rājyam hitvā paraṃtapa bhīṣmaḥ uvāca na asti anantam mahā rāja sarvam saṃkhyāna gocaram punarbhāvaḥ api saṃkhyātaḥ na asti kim cit iha acalam na ca api gamyate rājan na eṣa doṣaḥ prasaṅgataḥ īśaḥ ayam satatam dehī nṛpate puṇya pāpayoḥ yathā añjana mayaḥ vāyuḥ punar mānaḥśilam rajaḥ anupraviśya tad varṇaḥ dṛśyate rañjayan diśaḥ tathā karma phalaiḥ dehī rañjitaḥ tamasā āvṛtaḥ jñānena hi yadā jantuḥ ajñāna prabhavam tamaḥ tvayā ca lokena ca sa amareṇa tasmāt na śāmyanti mahā ṛṣi saṃghāḥ asmin arthe purā gītam śṛṇuṣva ekamanāḥ nṛpa yathā daityena vṛtreṇa bhraṣṭa aiśvaryeṇa ceṣṭitam a śocatā śatru madhye buddhim āsthāya kevalām bhraṣṭa aiśvaryam purā vṛtram uśanāḥ vākyam abravīt vṛtraḥ uvāca na śocāmi na hṛṣyāmi bhūtānām āgatim gatim kāla saṃcoditāḥ jīvāḥ majjanti narake avaśāḥ paridṛṣṭāni sarvāṇi divyāni āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ kṣapayitvā tu tam kālam gaṇitam kāla coditāḥ sa avaśeṣeṇa kālena saṃbhavanti punar punar nirgacchanti avaśāḥ jīvāḥ kāla bandhana bandhanāḥ evam saṃsaramāṇāni jīvāni aham adṛṣṭavān yathā karma tathā lābhaḥ iti śāstra nidarśanam gatam gacchanti ca adhvānam sarva bhūtāni sarvadā bhīṣmaḥ uvāca kāla saṃkhyāna saṃkhyātam sṛṣṭi sthiti parāyaṇam tam bhāṣamāṇam bhagavān uśanā pratyabhāṣata bhīmān duṣṭa pralāpān tvam tāta kasmāt prabhāṣase vṛtraḥ uvāca pratyakṣam etat bhavataḥ tathā anyeṣām manīṣiṇām gandhān ādāya bhūtānām rasān ca vividhān api jvālā mālā parikṣiptaḥ vaihāyasa caraḥ tathā ajeyaḥ sarva bhūtānām āsam nityam apeta bhīḥ aiśvaryam tapasā prāptam bhraṣṭam tat ca sva karmabhiḥ yuyutsatā mahā indreṇa purā sārdham mahātmanā tatas me bhagavān dṛṣṭaḥ hariḥ nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ vaikuṇṭhaḥ puruṣaḥ viṣṇuḥ śuklaḥ anantaḥ sanātanaḥ nūnam tu tasya tapasaḥ sa avaśeṣam mama asti vai yat aham praṣṭum icchāmi bhavantam karmaṇaḥ phalam kim vā phalam param prāpya jīvaḥ tiṣṭhati śāśvataḥ kena vā karmaṇā śakyam atha jñānena kena vā iti idam uktaḥ sa muniḥ tadānīm pratyāha yat tat śṛṇu rāja siṃha uśanāḥ uvāca yasya pṛthvī talam tāta sa ākāśam bāhu gocaram tasya aham te pravakṣyāmi viṣṇoḥ māhātmyam uttamam bhīṣmaḥ uvāca tayoḥ saṃvadatoḥ evam ājagāma mahā muniḥ sanatkumāraḥ dharma ātmā saṃśaya chedanāya vai niṣasāda āsane rājan mahārhe muni puṃgavaḥ tam āsīnam mahā prājñam uśanāḥ vākyam abravīt brūhi asmai dānava indrāya viṣṇoḥ māhātmyam uttamam viṣṇoḥ māhātmya saṃyuktam dānava indrāya dhīmate śṛṇu sarvam idam daitya viṣṇoḥ māhātmyam uttamam sṛjati eṣa mahā bāho bhūta grāmam carācaram eṣa ca ākṣipate kāle kāle visṛjate punar na eṣa dānavatā śakyaḥ tapasā nā eva ca ijyayā saṃprāptum indriyāṇām tu saṃyamena eva śakyate tadvat jāti śataiḥ jīvaḥ śudhyate alpena karmaṇā līlayā alpam yathā gātrāt pramṛjyāt ātmanaḥ rajaḥ yathā ca alpena mālyena vāsitam tila sarṣapam evam jāti śataiḥ yuktaḥ guṇaiḥ eva prasaṅgiṣu yathā karma viśeṣān ca prāpnuvanti tathā śṛṇu tat te anupūrvyā vyākhyāsye tat iha ekamanāḥ śṛṇu an ādi nidhanaḥ śrīmān hariḥ nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ sa vai sṛjati bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca eṣa sarveṣu bhūteṣu kṣaraḥ ca akṣaraḥ eva ca ekādaśa vikāra ātmā jagat pibati raśmibhiḥ pādau tasya mahīm viddhi mūrdhānam divam eva ca bāhavaḥ tu diśaḥ daitya śrotram ākāśam eva ca nakṣatra cakram netrābhyām pādayoḥ bhūḥ ca dānava saḥ mukham tāta karmaṇaḥ tat phalam viduḥ chandāṃsi tasya romāṇi akṣaram ca sarasvatī bahu āśrayaḥ bahu mukhaḥ dharmaḥ hṛdi samāśritaḥ śruti śāstra graha upetaḥ ṣoḍaśartvikkratuḥ ca saḥ pitāmahaḥ ca viṣṇuḥ ca saḥ aśvinau sa puraṃdaraḥ jantuḥ paśyati jñānena tatas sattvam prakāśate saṃhāra vikṣepa sahasra koṭīḥ tiṣṭhanti jīvāḥ pracaranti ca anye prajā visargasya ca pārimāṇyam vāpī sahasrāṇi bahūni daitya vāpyaḥ punar yojana vistṛtāḥ tāḥ krośam ca gambhīra tayā avagāḍhāḥ āyāmataḥ pañcaśatāḥ ca sarvāḥ pratyekaśaḥ yojanataḥ pravṛddhāḥ vāpyāḥ jalam kṣipyati vāla koṭyā tu ahnā sakṛt ca api atha na dvitīyam tāsām kṣaye viddhi kṛtam visargam saṃhāram ekam ca tathā prajānām ṣaṭ jīva varṇāḥ paramam pramāṇam kṛṣṇaḥ dhūmraḥ nīlam atha asya madhyam raktam punar sahyataram sukham tu hāridra varṇam su sukham ca śuklam gatim ca yām darśanam āha devaḥ gatvā śubham darśanam eva ca āha gatiḥ punar varṇa kṛtā prajānām varṇaḥ tathā kāla kṛtaḥ asura indra śatam sahasrāṇi caturdaśa iha parā gatiḥ jīva guṇasya daitya ārohaṇam tat kṛtam eva viddhi sthānam tathā niḥsaraṇam ca teṣām kṛṣṇasya varṇasya gatiḥ nikṛṣṭā sa majjate narake pacyamānaḥ śatam sahasrāṇi tatas caritvā prāpnoti varṇam haritam tu paścāt sa ca eva tasmin nivasati anīśaḥ yuga kṣaye tamasā saṃvṛta ātmā tatas sa hāridram upaiti varṇam saṃhāra vikṣepa śate vyatīte gatīḥ sahasrāṇi ca pañca tasya catvāri saṃvarta kṛtāni ca eva sa deva loke viharati abhīkṣṇam tatas cyutaḥ mānuṣa tām upaiti saṃhāra vikṣepa śatāni ca aṣṭau martyeṣu tiṣṭhan amṛta tvam eti saḥ asmāt atha bhraśyati kāla yogāt kṛṣṇe tale tiṣṭhati sarva kaṣṭe saṃśritya saṃdhāvati śuklam etam aṣṭā aparān arcyatamān sa lokān aṣṭau ca ṣaṣṭim ca śatāni yāni manaḥ viruddhāni mahā dyutīnām śuklasya varṇasya parā gatiḥ yā trīṇi eva ruddhāni mahā anubhāva saṃhāra vikṣepam aniṣṭam ekam catvāri ca anyāni vasati anīśaḥ ṣaṣṭhasya varṇasya parā gatiḥ yā siddhā viśiṣṭasya gata klamasya sapta uttaram teṣu vasati anīśaḥ saṃhāra vikṣepa śatam sa śeṣam tasmāt upāvṛtya manuṣya loke tatas mahān mānuṣa tām upaiti tasmāt upāvṛtya tatas krameṇa saḥ agre sma saṃtiṣṭhati bhūta sargam sa sapta kṛtvas ca paraiti lokān saṃhāra vikṣepa kṛta pravāsaḥ saṃhāra kāle paridagdha kāyāḥ brahmāṇam āyānti sadā prajāḥ hi ceṣṭā ātmanaḥ deva gaṇāḥ ca sarve ye brahma lokāt amarāḥ sma te api prajā visargam tu sa śeṣa kālam sthānāni svāni eva saranti jīvāḥ niḥśeṣāṇām tat padam yānti ca ante sarva āpadā ye sadṛśāḥ manuṣyāḥ ye tu cyutāḥ siddha lokāt krameṇa teṣām gatim yānti tathā ānupūrvyā jīvāḥ pare tad bala veṣa rūpāḥ vidhim svakam yānti viparyayeṇa tāvat tadā teṣu viśuddha bhāvaḥ saṃyamya pañca indriya rūpam etat śuddhām gatim tām paramām paraiti śuddhena nityam manasā vicinvan iti etat ākhyātam ahīna sattva nārāyaṇasya iha balam mayā te vṛtraḥ uvāca viṣṇoḥ anantasya sanātanam tat sthānam sargāḥ yatra sarve pravṛttāḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca evam uktvā sa kaunteya vṛtraḥ prāṇān avāsṛjat yojayitvā tathā ātmānam param sthānam avāptavān yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca ayam sa bhagavān devaḥ pitāmaha janārdanaḥ sanatkumāraḥ vṛtrāya yat tat ākhyātavān purā bhīṣmaḥ uvāca mūla sthāyī sa bhagavān svena anantena tejasā tad sthaḥ sṛjati tān bhāvān nānā rūpān mahā tapāḥ turīyārdhena lokān trīn bhāvayati eṣa buddhimān tān vidhātā prasanna ātmā lokān carati śāśvatān sarvāṇi a śūnyāni karoti anantaḥ sanatkumāraḥ saṃcarate ca lokān yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca vṛtreṇa parama artha jña dṛṣṭā manye gatiḥ śuklaḥ śukla abhijātīyaḥ sādhyaḥ na āvartate anagha vayam tu bhṛśam āpannāḥ raktāḥ kaṣṭa mukhe asukhe kām gatim pratipatsyāmaḥ nīlām kṛṣṇa adhamām atha bhīṣmaḥ uvāca śuddha abhijana saṃpannāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ saṃśita vratāḥ sukhena saṃyāsyatha siddha saṃkhyām mā vaḥ bhayam bhūt vimalāḥ stha sarve yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca aho dharmiṣṭha tā tāta vṛtrasya amita tejasaḥ yasya vijñānam atulam viṣṇoḥ bhaktiḥ ca tādṛśī durvijñeyam idam tāta viṣṇoḥ amita tejasaḥ katham vā rāja śārdūla padam tat jñātavān asau katham vinihataḥ vṛtraḥ śakreṇa bharata ṛṣabha dharmiṣṭhaḥ viṣṇu bhaktaḥ ca tattva jñaḥ ca pada anvaye etat me saṃśayam brūhi pṛcchataḥ bharata ṛṣabha vṛtraḥ tu rāja śārdūla yathā śakreṇa nirjitaḥ vistareṇa mahā bāho param kautūhalam hi me bhīṣmaḥ uvāca rathena indraḥ prayātaḥ vai sārdham sura gaṇaiḥ purā dadarśa atha agratas vṛtram viṣṭhitam parvata upamam yojanānām śatāni ūrdhvam pañca ucchritam ariṃdama śatāni vistareṇa atha trīṇi eva abhyadhikāni tu tat prekṣya tādṛśam rūpam trailokyena api durjayam vṛtrasya devāḥ saṃtrastāḥ na śāntim upalebhire bhayāt vṛtrasya sahasā dṛṣṭvā tat rūpam uttamam tatas nādaḥ samabhavat vāditrāṇām ca nisvanaḥ deva asurāṇām sarveṣām tasmin yuddhe upasthite na saṃbhramaḥ na bhīḥ kā cit āsthā vā samajāyata asibhiḥ paṭṭiśaiḥ śūlaiḥ śakti tomara mudgaraiḥ śilābhiḥ vividhābhiḥ ca kārmukaiḥ ca mahā svanaiḥ pitāmaha purogāḥ ca sarve deva gaṇāḥ tathā ṛṣayaḥ ca mahābhāgāḥ tat yuddham draṣṭum āgaman vimāna agryaiḥ mahā rāja siddhāḥ ca bharata ṛṣabha tatas antarikṣam āvṛtya vṛtraḥ dharma bhṛtām varaḥ aśma varṣeṇa deva indram parvatāt samavākirat tatas deva gaṇāḥ kruddhāḥ sarvatas śastra vṛṣṭibhiḥ vṛtraḥ ca kuru śārdūla mahā māyaḥ mahā balaḥ mohayām āsa deva indram māyā yuddhena sarvatas tasya vṛtra arditasya atha mohaḥ āsīt śatakratoḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ uvāca eṣa brahmā ca viṣṇuḥ ca śivaḥ ca eva jagatprabhuḥ mā kārṣīḥ kaśmalam śakra kaḥ cit eva itaraḥ yathā āryām yuddhe matim kṛtvā jahi śatrum sureśvara nirīkṣate tvām bhagavān tyaja moham sureśvara bhīṣmaḥ uvāca evam saṃbodhyamānasya vasiṣṭhena mahātmanā tatas buddhim upāgamya bhagavān pākaśāsanaḥ yogena mahatā yuktaḥ tām māyām vyapakarṣata tatas aṅgiraḥ sutaḥ śrīmān te ca eva parama ṛṣayaḥ dṛṣṭvā vṛtrasya vikrāntam upagamya maheśvaram ūcuḥ vṛtra vināśa artham lokānām hita kāmyayā samāviśat mahā raudram vṛtram daitya varam tadā viṣṇuḥ ca bhagavān devaḥ sarva loka abhipūjitaḥ aindram samāviśat vajram loka saṃrakṣaṇe rataḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ ca mahā tejāḥ sarve ca parama ṛṣayaḥ te samāsādya vara dam vāsavam loka pūjitam eṣa vṛtraḥ mahān śakra balena mahatā vṛtaḥ viśva ātmā sarva gaḥ ca eva bahu māyaḥ ca viśrutaḥ jahi tvam yogam āsthāya mā avamaṃsthāḥ sureśvara ṣaṣṭim varṣa sahasrāṇi brahmā ca asmai varam dadau mahā bala tvam ca tathā tejaḥ ca agryam sureśvara etat vai māmakam tejaḥ samāviśati vāsava śakraḥ uvāca bhīṣmaḥ uvāca āviśyamāne daitye tu jvareṇa atha mahā asure devatānām ṛṣīṇām ca harṣāt nādaḥ mahān abhūt tatas dundubhayaḥ ca eva śaṅkhāḥ ca su mahā svanāḥ murajāḥ ḍiṇḍimāḥ ca eva prāvādyanta sahasraśas asurāṇām tu sarveṣām smṛti lopaḥ abhavat mahān prajñā nāśaḥ ca balavān kṣaṇena samapadyata tam āviṣṭam atho jñātvā ṛṣayaḥ devatāḥ tathā stuvantaḥ śakram īśānam tathā prācodayan api ṛṣibhiḥ stūyamānasya rūpam āsīt su durdṛśam bhīṣmaḥ uvāca vṛtrasya tu mahā rāja jvara āviṣṭasya sarvaśas abhavan yāni liṅgāni śarīre tāni me śṛṇu gātra kampaḥ ca su mahān śvāsaḥ ca api abhavat mahān romaharṣaḥ ca tīvraḥ abhūt niḥśvāsaḥ ca mahān nṛpa śivā ca aśiva saṃkāśā tasya vaktrāt su dāruṇā niṣpapāta mahā ghorā smṛtiḥ sā tasya bhārata ulkāḥ ca jvalitāḥ tasya dīptāḥ pārśve prapedire gṛdhra kaṅka vaḍāḥ ca eva vācaḥ amuñcan su dāruṇāḥ vṛtrasya upari saṃhṛṣṭāḥ cakra vat paribabhramuḥ tatas tam ratham āsthāya deva āpyāyitam āhave amānuṣam atho nādam sa mumoca mahā asuraḥ atha asya jṛmbhataḥ śakraḥ tatas vajram avāsṛjat sa vajraḥ su mahā tejāḥ kālāgni sadṛśa upamaḥ kṣipram eva mahā kāyam vṛtram daityam apātayat vṛtram vinihatam dṛṣṭvā devānām bharata ṛṣabha vṛtram tu hatvā bhagavān dānavāriḥ mahā yaśāḥ atha vṛtrasya kauravya śarīrāt abhiniḥsṛtā brahmahatyā mahā ghorā raudrā loka bhaya āvahā karāla daśanā bhīmā vikṛtā kṛṣṇa piṅgalā prakīrṇa mūrdhajā ca eva ghora netrā ca bhārata kapāla mālinī ca eva kṛśā ca bharata ṛṣabha rudhira ārdrā ca dharma jña cīra vastra nivāsinī sā abhiniṣkramya rāja indra tādṛś rūpā bhaya āvahā vajriṇam mṛgayām āsa tadā bharata sattama svargāya abhimukhaḥ prāyāt lokānām hita kāmyayā bisāt niḥsaramāṇam tu dṛṣṭvā śakram mahā ojasam kaṇṭhe jagrāha devendram su lagnā ca abhavat tadā nalinyām bisa madhya sthaḥ babhūva abda gaṇān bahūn tadā gṛhītaḥ kauravya niśceṣṭaḥ samapadyata tasyāḥ vyapohane śakraḥ param yatnam cakāra ha jñātvā gṛhītam śakram tu dvija pravara hatyayā tām uvāca mahā bāho brahma hatyām pitāmahaḥ tvayā kṛtā iyam maryādā loka saṃrakṣaṇa arthinā śakrāt apagamiṣyāmi nivāsam tu vidhatsva me bhīṣmaḥ uvāca tathā iti tām prāha tadā brahmahatyām pitāmahaḥ śakrasya adya vimokṣa artham catur bhāgam pratīccha me yaḥ tvām jvalantam āsādya svayam vai mānavaḥ kva cit bhīṣmaḥ uvāca tatas vṛkṣa oṣadhi tṛṇam samāhūya pitāmahaḥ tatas vṛkṣa oṣadhi tṛṇam tathā evā uktam yathātatham vayam agnim tathā śītam varṣam ca pavana īritam brahmahatyām imām adya bhavataḥ śāsanāt vayam grahīṣyāmaḥ triloka īśa mokṣam cintayatām bhavān bhīṣmaḥ uvāca tatas vṛkṣa oṣadhi tṛṇam evam uktam mahātmanā brahmāṇam abhisaṃpūjya jagāma āśu yathāgatam vācā madhurayā prāha sāntvayan iva bhārata iyam indrāt anuprāptā brahmahatyā vara aṅganāḥ caturtham asyāḥ bhāgam hi mayā uktāḥ saṃpratīcchata apsarasaḥ ūcuḥ grahaṇe kṛtabuddhīnām deveśa tava śāsanāt tam eṣā yāsyati kṣipram vyetu vaḥ mānasaḥ jvaraḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca tathā iti hṛṣṭa manasaḥ uktvā atha apsarasām gaṇāḥ apaḥ saṃcintayām āsa dhyātāḥ tāḥ ca api atha agaman tāḥ tu sarvāḥ samāgamya brahmāṇam amita ojasam imāḥ sma deva saṃprāptāḥ tvad sakāśam ariṃdama śāsanāt tava deveśa samājñāpaya naḥ vibho iyam vṛtrāt anuprāptā puruhūtam mahā bhayā brahmahatyā caturtha aṃśam asyāḥ yūyam pratīcchata āpaḥ ūcuḥ śleṣma mūtra purīṣāṇi yuṣmāsu pratimokṣyati tathā vaḥ bhavitā mokṣaḥ iti satyam bravīmi vaḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca yathā nisṛṣṭam tam deśam agacchat deva śāsanāt evam śakreṇa saṃprāptā brahmahatyā janādhipa śrūyate hi mahā rāja saṃprāptā vāsavena vai samavāpya śriyam devaḥ hatvā arīn ca sahasraśas praharṣam atulam lebhe vāsavaḥ pṛthivīpate vṛtrasya rudhirāt ca eva khukhuṇḍāḥ pārtha jajñire dvijātibhiḥ abhakṣyāḥ te dīkṣitaiḥ ca tapodhanaiḥ sarva avastham tvam api eṣām dvijātīnām priyam kuru evam śakreṇa kauravya buddhi saukṣmyāt mahā asuraḥ upāya pūrvam nihataḥ vṛtraḥ atha amita tejasā ye tu śakra kathām divyām imām parvasu parvasu yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca pitāmaha mahā prājña sarva śāstra viśārada katham eṣa mahā prājña jvaraḥ prādurabhūt kutas bhīṣmaḥ uvāca śṛṇu rājan jvarasya iha saṃbhavam loka viśrutam vistaram ca asya vakṣyāmi yādṛśam ca eva bhārata purā meroḥ mahā rāja śṛṅgam trailokya viśrutam jyotiṣkam nāma sāvitram sarva ratna vibhūṣitam aprameyam anādhṛṣyam sarva lokeṣu bhārata śailarājasutā ca asya nityam pārśve sthitā babhau tathā devāḥ mahātmānaḥ vasavaḥ ca mahā ojasaḥ tathā eva ca mahātmānau aśvinau bhiṣajām varau tathā vaiśravaṇaḥ rājā guhyakaiḥ abhisaṃvṛtaḥ yakṣāṇām adhipaḥ śrīmān kailāsa nilayaḥ prabhuḥ aṅgiraḥ pramukhāḥ ca eva tathā devarṣayaḥ apare apsaraḥ gaṇa saṃghāḥ ca samājagmuḥ anekaśas vavau śivaḥ sukhaḥ vāyuḥ nānā gandha vahaḥ śuciḥ sarva ṛtu kusuma upetāḥ puṣpavantaḥ mahā drumāḥ tathā vidyādharāḥ ca eva siddhāḥ ca eva tapodhanāḥ mahādevam paśupatim paryupāsanta bhārata bhūtāni ca mahā rāja nānā rūpa dharāṇi atha rākṣasāḥ ca mahā raudrāḥ piśācāḥ ca mahā balāḥ bahu rūpa dharāḥ hṛṣṭāḥ nānā praharaṇa udyatāḥ pragṛhya jvalitam śūlam dīpyamānam sva tejasā gaṅgā ca saritām śreṣṭhā sarva tīrtha jala udbhavā paryupāsata tam devam rūpiṇī kuru nandana evam sa bhagavān tatra pūjyamānaḥ sura ṛṣibhiḥ devaiḥ ca su mahābhāgaiḥ mahādevaḥ vyatiṣṭhata tatas tasya makham devāḥ sarve śakra purogamāḥ devasya anumate agacchan gaṅgādvāram iti śrutiḥ prasthitāḥ devatāḥ dṛṣṭvā śailarājasutā tadā uvāca vacanam sādhvī devam paśupatim patim bhagavan kva nu yānti ete devāḥ śakra purogamāḥ dakṣaḥ nāma mahābhāge prajānām patiḥ uttamaḥ umā uvāca umā uvāca ajeyaḥ ca apradhṛṣyaḥ ca tejasā yaśasā śriyā bhīṣmaḥ uvāca evam uktvā tu sā devī devam paśupatim patim tūṣṇīṃbhūtā bhavat rājan dahyamānena cetasā atha devyāḥ matam jñātvā hṛd gatam yat cikīrṣitam sa samājñāpayām āsa tiṣṭha tvam iti nandinam tatas yoga balam kṛtvā sarva yoga īśvara īśvaraḥ tam yajñam su mahā tejāḥ bhīmaiḥ anucaraiḥ tadā sahasā ghātayām āsa devadevaḥ pinākadhṛk ke cit nādān amuñcanta ke cit hāsān ca cakrire rudhireṇa apare rājan tatra agnim samavākiran ke cit yūpān samutpāṭya babhramuḥ vikṛta ānanāḥ tatas sa yajñaḥ nṛpate vadhyamānaḥ samantataḥ āsthāya mṛga rūpam vai kham eva abhyapatat tadā tam tu yajñam tathārūpam gacchantam upalabhya saḥ dhanuḥ ādāya bāṇam ca tadā anvasarata prabhuḥ lalāṭāt prasṛtaḥ ghoraḥ sveda binduḥ babhūva ha prādurbabhūva su mahān agniḥ kāla anala upamaḥ tatra ca ajāyata tadā puruṣaḥ puruṣa ṛṣabha hrasvaḥ atimātra rakta akṣaḥ hari śmaśruḥ vibhīṣaṇaḥ ūrdhva keśaḥ atiloma aṅgaḥ śyena ulūkaḥ tathā eva ca karālaḥ kṛṣṇa varṇaḥ ca rakta vāsāḥ tathā eva ca tam yajñam sa mahā sattvaḥ adahat kakṣam iva analaḥ devāḥ ca api adravan sarve tatas bhītāḥ diśaḥ daśa tena tasmin vicaratā puruṣeṇa viśām pate hāhā bhūte pravṛtte tu nāde loka bhayaṃkare pitāmahaḥ mahādevam darśayan pratyabhāṣata kriyatām pratisaṃhāraḥ sarva deva īśvara tvayā imāḥ hi devatāḥ sarvāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca paraṃtapa yaḥ ca eṣa puruṣaḥ jātaḥ svedāt te vibudha uttama samarthā sakalā pṛthvī bahudhā sṛjyatām ayam parām ca prītim agamat utsmayan ca pinākadhṛk avāpa ca tadā bhāgam yathoktam brahmaṇā bhavaḥ śānti artham sarva bhūtānām śṛṇu tat ca api putraka śīrṣa abhitāpaḥ nāgānām parvatānām śilājatuḥ apām tu nīlikām vidyāt nirmokam bhujageṣu ca khorakaḥ saurabheyāṇām ūṣaram pṛthivī tale paśūnām api dharma jña dṛṣṭi pratyavarodhanam randhrāgatam atha aśvānām śikhā udbhedaḥ ca barhiṇām netra rogaḥ kokilānām jvaraḥ proktaḥ mahātmanā ap jānām pitta bhedaḥ ca sarveṣām iti naḥ śrutam śukānām api sarveṣām hikkikā procyate jvaraḥ śārdūleṣu atha dharma jña śramaḥ jvaraḥ iha ucyate mānuṣeṣu tu dharma jña jvaraḥ nāma eṣa viśrutaḥ etat māheśvaram tejaḥ jvaraḥ nāma su dāruṇaḥ namasyaḥ ca eva mānyaḥ ca sarva prāṇibhiḥ īśvaraḥ anena hi samāviṣṭaḥ vṛtraḥ dharma bhṛtām varaḥ praviśya vajraḥ vṛtram tu dārayām āsa bhārata dāritaḥ ca sa vajreṇa mahā yogī mahā asuraḥ jagāma paramam sthānam viṣṇoḥ amita tejasaḥ viṣṇu bhaktyā hi tena idam jagat vyāptam abhūt purā tasmāt ca nihataḥ yuddhe viṣṇoḥ sthānam avāptavān imām jvara utpattim adīna mānasaḥ paṭhet sadā yaḥ su samāhitaḥ naraḥ vimukta rogaḥ sa sukhī mudā yutaḥ labheta kāmān sa yathā manīṣitān yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca śokāt duḥkhāt ca mṛtyoḥ ca trasyanti prāṇinaḥ sadā bhīṣmaḥ uvāca nāradasya ca saṃvādam samaṅgasya ca bhārata nāradaḥ uvāca saṃprahṛṣṭa manāḥ nityam viśokaḥ iva lakṣyase samaṅgaḥ uvāca bhūtam bhavyam bhaviṣyat ca sarvam sattveṣu mānada teṣām tattvāni jānāmi tatas na vimanāḥ hi aham agādhāḥ ca apratiṣṭhāḥ ca gatimantaḥ ca nārada andhāḥ jaḍāḥ ca jīvanti paśya asmān api jīvataḥ sahasriṇaḥ ca jīvanti jīvanti śatinaḥ tathā śākena ca anye jīvanti paśya asmān api jīvataḥ yadā na śocemahi kim nu na syāt dharmeṇa vā nārada karmaṇā vā kṛtānta vaśyāni yadā sukhāni duḥkhāni vā yat na vidharṣayanti yasmai prajñām kathayante manuṣyāḥ prajñā mūlaḥ hi indriyāṇām prasādaḥ muhyanti śocanti yadā indriyāṇi prajñā lābhaḥ na asti mūḍha indriyasya bhāva ātmakam saṃparivartamānam na mādṛśaḥ saṃjvaram jātu kuryāt iṣṭān bhogān na anurudhyet sukham vā na cintayet duḥkham abhyāgatam vā samāhitaḥ na spṛhayet pareṣām na anāgatam na abhinandeta lābham na ca api hṛṣyet vipule artha lābhe tathā artha nāśe ca na vai viṣīdet duḥkhāt trātum sarve eva utsahante paratra śīle na tu yānti śāntim dhṛtiḥ ca duḥkha tyāgaḥ ca api ubhayam naḥ sukha udayam etān śoka bhaya utsekān mohanān sukha duḥkhayoḥ paśyāmi sākṣi vat loke dehasya asya viceṣṭanāt tṛṣṇā mohau tu saṃtyajya carāmi pṛthivīm imām pīta amṛtasya iva atyantam iha ca amutra vā bhayam tena nārada saṃprāptaḥ na mām śokaḥ prabādhate yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca a tattva jñasya śāstrāṇām satatam saṃśaya ātmanaḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca guru pūjā ca satatam vṛddhānām paryupāsanam śravaṇam ca eva vidyānām kūṭastham śreyaḥ ucyate atrā api udāharanti imam itihāsam purātanam gālavasya ca saṃvādam deva ṛṣeḥ nāradasya ca vīta moha klamam vipram jñāna tṛptam jita indriyam śreyaskāmam jita ātmānam nāradam gālavaḥ abravīt yaiḥ kaiḥ cit saṃmataḥ loke guṇaiḥ tu puruṣaḥ nṛṣu bhavati anapagān sarvān tān guṇān lakṣayāmi aham bhavān evaṃvidhaḥ asmākam saṃśayam chettum arhati amūḍhaḥ cira mūḍhānām loka tattvam a jānatām jñāne hi evam pravṛttiḥ syāt kārya akārye vijānataḥ bhagavan āśramāḥ sarve pṛthak ācāra darśinaḥ idam śreyaḥ idam śreyaḥ iti nānā pradhāvitāḥ tān tu viprasthitān dṛṣṭvā śāstraiḥ śāstra abhinandinaḥ sva śāstraiḥ parituṣṭān ca śreyaḥ na upalabhāmahe śāstram yadi bhavet ekam vyaktam śreyaḥ bhavet tadā śāstraiḥ ca bahubhiḥ bhūyas śreyaḥ guhyam praveśitam etasmāt kāraṇāt śreyaḥ kalilam pratibhāti mām nāradaḥ uvāca āśramāḥ tāta catvāraḥ yathā saṃkalpitāḥ pṛthak tān sarvān anupaśya tvam samāśritya eva gālava teṣām teṣām tathā hi tvam āśramāṇām tatas tatas nānā rūpa guṇa uddeśam paśya viprasthitam pṛthak ṛju paśyan tathā samyak āśramāṇām parām gatim yat tu niḥśreyasam samyak tat ca eva asaṃśaya ātmakam anugraham ca mitrāṇām amitrāṇām ca nigraham saṃgraham ca trivargasya śreyaḥ āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ nivṛttiḥ karmaṇaḥ pāpāt satatam puṇya śīla tā sadbhiḥ ca samudācāraḥ śreyaḥ etat asaṃśayam mārdavam sarva bhūteṣu vyavahāreṣu ca ārjavam vāc ca eva madhurā proktā śreyaḥ etat asaṃśayam devatābhyaḥ pitṛbhyaḥ ca saṃvibhāgaḥ atithiṣu api asaṃtyāgaḥ ca bhṛtyānām śreyaḥ etat asaṃśayam satyasya vacanam śreyaḥ satya jñānam tu duṣkaram ahaṃkārasya ca tyāgaḥ praṇayasya ca nigrahaḥ saṃtoṣaḥ ca eka caryā ca kūṭastham śreyaḥ ucyate dharmeṇa veda adhyayanam vedāṅgānām tathā eva ca vidyā arthānām ca jijñāsā śreyaḥ etat asaṃśayam naktaṃcaryā divāsvapnam ālasyam paiśunam madam karma utkarṣam na mārgeta pareṣām parinindayā nirguṇāḥ tu eva bhūyiṣṭham ātma saṃbhāvinaḥ narāḥ doṣaiḥ anyān guṇavataḥ kṣipanti ātma guṇa kṣayāt guṇavattaram ātmānam svena mānena darpitāḥ vipaścit guṇa saṃpannaḥ prāpnoti eva mahat yaśaḥ abruvan vāti surabhiḥ gandhaḥ sumanasām śuciḥ evamādīni ca anyāni parityaktāni medhayā na loke dīpyate mūrkhaḥ kevala ātma praśaṃsayā api ca apihitaḥ śvabhre kṛta vidyaḥ prakāśate mūḍhānām avaliptānām asāram bhāṣitam bahu darśayati antarātmānam divā rūpam iva aṃśumān etasmāt kāraṇāt prajñām mṛgayante pṛthagvidhām prajñā lābhaḥ hi bhūtānām uttamaḥ pratibhāti mām na apṛṣṭaḥ kasya cit brūyāt na ca anyāyena pṛcchataḥ jñānavān api medhāvī jaḍa vat lokam ācaret tatas vāsam parīkṣeta dharma nityeṣu sādhuṣu caturṇām yatra varṇānām dharma vyatikaraḥ bhavet puṇyam puṇyeṣu vimalam pāpam pāpeṣu ca āpnuyāt tathā paśyāmahe sparśam ubhayoḥ pāpa puṇyayoḥ a paśyantaḥ anna viṣayam bhuñjate vighasa āśinaḥ bhuñjānam ca anna viṣayān viṣayam viddhi karmaṇām yatra āgamayamānānām asatkāreṇa pṛcchatām prabrūyāt brahmaṇaḥ dharmam tyajet tam deśam ātmavān śiṣya upādhyāyikāḥ vṛttiḥ yatra syāt su samāhitā yathāvat śāstra saṃpannā kaḥ tam deśam parityajet ākāśa sthāḥ dhruvam yatra doṣam brūyuḥ vipaścitām ātma pūjā abhikāmāḥ vai kaḥ vaset tatra paṇḍitaḥ yatra saṃloḍitāḥ lubdhaiḥ prāyaśas dharma setavaḥ pradīptam iva śaila antam kaḥ tam deśam na saṃtyajet yatra dharmam anāśaṅkāḥ careyuḥ vīta matsarāḥ caret tatra vaset ca eva puṇya śīleṣu sādhuṣu na tān anuvaset jātu te hi pāpa kṛtaḥ janāḥ vyavadhāvet tatas tūrṇam sa sarpāt śaraṇāt iva yena khaṭvām samārūḍhaḥ karmaṇā anuśayī bhavet yatra rājā ca rājñaḥ ca puruṣāḥ pratyanantarāḥ kuṭumbinām agra bhujaḥ tyajet tat rāṣṭram ātmavān śrotriyāḥ tu agra bhoktāraḥ dharma nityāḥ sanātanāḥ yājana adhyāpane yuktāḥ yatra tat rāṣṭram āvaset svāhā svadhā vaṣaṭkārāḥ yatra samyak anuṣṭhitāḥ aśucīni atra paśyeta brāhmaṇān vṛtti karśitān tyajet tat rāṣṭram āsannam upasṛṣṭam iva āmiṣam prīyamāṇāḥ narāḥ yatra prayaccheyuḥ a yācitāḥ daṇḍaḥ yatra avinīteṣu satkāraḥ ca kṛtātmasu caret tatra vaset ca eva puṇya śīleṣu sādhuṣu upasṛṣṭeṣu a dānteṣu durācāreṣu a sādhuṣu avinīteṣu lubdheṣu su mahat daṇḍadhāraṇam yatra rājā dharma nityaḥ rājyam vai paryupāsitā apāsya kāmān kāma īśaḥ vaset tatra a vicārayan tathāśīlāḥ hi rājānaḥ sarvān viṣaya vāsinaḥ pṛcchataḥ te mayā tāta śreyaḥ etat udāhṛtam na hi śakyam pradhānena śreyaḥ saṃkhyātum ātmanaḥ evam pravartamānasya vṛttim praṇihita ātmanaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca katham nu muktaḥ pṛthivīm caret asmadvidhaḥ nṛpaḥ nityam kaiḥ ca guṇaiḥ yuktaḥ saṅga pāśāt vimucyate bhīṣmaḥ uvāca ariṣṭaneminā proktam sagarāya anupṛcchate bhīṣmaḥ uvāca evam uktaḥ tadā tārkṣyaḥ sarva śāstra viśāradaḥ vibudhya saṃpadam ca agryām sat vākyam idam abravīt prasaktaḥ putra paśuṣu dhana dhānya samākulaḥ sneha pāśa sitaḥ mūḍhaḥ na sa mokṣāya kalpate sneha jān iha te pāśān vakṣyāmi śṛṇu tān mama sa karṇakena śirasā śakyāḥ chettum vijānatā samarthān jīvane jñātvā muktaḥ cara yathāsukham bhāryām putravatīm vṛddhām lālitām putra vatsalām jñātvā prajahi kāle tvam para artham anudṛśya ca eṣa tāvat samāsena tava saṃkīrtitaḥ mayā mokṣa arthaḥ vistareṇa api bhūyas vakṣyāmi tat śṛṇu sakta bhāvāḥ vinaśyanti narāḥ tatra na saṃśayaḥ āhāra saṃcayāḥ ca eva tathā kīṭa pipīlikāḥ asaktāḥ sukhinaḥ loke saktāḥ ca eva vināśinaḥ ime mayā vinābhūtāḥ bhaviṣyanti katham tu iti sva kṛtena adhigacchanti loke na asti a kṛtam purā dhātrā vihita bhakṣyāṇi sarva bhūtāni medinīm kaḥ hetuḥ sva janam poṣṭum rakṣitum vā a dṛḍha ātmanaḥ jīvantam api ca eva enam bharaṇe rakṣaṇe tathā yadā mṛtaḥ ca sva janam na jñāsyasi katham cana mṛte vā tvayi jīve vā yadi bhokṣyati vai janaḥ mokṣe niveśaya manaḥ bhūyas ca api upadhāraya kṣudh pipāsā ādayaḥ bhāvāḥ jitāḥ yasya iha dehinaḥ dyūte pāne tathā strīṣu mṛgayāyām ca yaḥ naraḥ ātma bhāvam tathā strīṣu muktam eva punar punar saṃbhavam ca vināśam ca bhūtānām ceṣṭitam tathā prastham vāha sahasreṣu yātrā artham ca eva koṭiṣu prāsāde mañcaka sthānam yaḥ paśyati sa mucyate mṛtyunā abhyāhatam lokam vyādhibhiḥ ca upapīḍitam yaḥ paśyati sukhī tuṣṭaḥ na paśyan ca vihanyate yaḥ ca api alpena saṃtuṣṭaḥ loke asmin muktaḥ eva saḥ agnīṣomau idam sarvam iti yaḥ ca anupaśyati paryaṅka śayyā bhūmiḥ ca samāne yasya dehinaḥ śālayaḥ ca kadannam ca yasya syāt muktaḥ eva saḥ kṣaumam ca kuśa cīram ca kauśeyam valkalāni ca pañcabhūta samudbhūtam lokam yaḥ ca anupaśyati tathā ca vartate dṛṣṭvā loke asmin muktaḥ eva saḥ rakta mūtra purīṣāṇām doṣāṇām saṃcayam tathā śarīram doṣa bahulam dṛṣṭvā ca idam vimucyate valī palita saṃyogam kārśyam vaivarṇyam eva ca puṃstva upaghātam kālena darśana uparamam tathā bādhiryam prāṇa manda tvam yaḥ paśyati sa mucyate gatān ṛṣīn tathā devān asurān ca tathā gatān lokāt asmāt param lokam yaḥ paśyati sa mucyate prabhāvaiḥ anvitāḥ taiḥ taiḥ pārthiva indrāḥ sahasraśas ye gatāḥ pṛthivīm tyaktvā iti jñātvā vimucyate arthān ca durlabhān loke kleśān ca sulabhān tathā apatyānām ca vaiguṇyam janam viguṇam eva ca paśyan bhūyiṣṭhaśas loke kaḥ mokṣam na abhipūjayet śāstrāt lokāt ca yaḥ buddhaḥ sarvam paśyati mānavaḥ asāram iva mānuṣyam sarvathā muktaḥ eva saḥ mokṣa jaiḥ ca guṇaiḥ yuktaḥ pālayām āsa ca prajāḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca tiṣṭhate me sadā tāta kautūhalam idam hṛdi katham deva ṛṣiḥ uśanā sadā kāvyaḥ mahāmatiḥ asurāṇām priya karaḥ surāṇām apriye rataḥ nityam vaira nibaddhāḥ ca dānavāḥ sura sattamaiḥ katham ca api uśanāḥ prāpa śukra tvam amara dyutiḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca śṛṇu rājan avahitaḥ sarvam etat yathātatham eṣa bhārgava dāyādaḥ muniḥ satyaḥ dṛḍha vrataḥ asurāṇām priya karaḥ nimitte karuṇā ātmake prabhaviṣṇuḥ ca kośasya jagataḥ ca tathā prabhuḥ tasya ātmānam atha āviśya yoga siddhaḥ mahā muniḥ nivedayām āsa tadā śivāya amita tejase deva śreṣṭhāya rudrāya saumyāya bahu rūpiṇe yoga ātmakena uśanasā ruddhvā mama hṛtam vasu yogena ātma gatim kṛtvā niḥsṛtaḥ ca mahā tapāḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca saṃrakta nayanaḥ rājan śūlam ādāya tasthivān kva asvau kva asau iti prāha gṛhītvā parama āyudham uśanāḥ dūratas tasya babhau jñātvā cikīrṣitam sa mahā yoginaḥ buddhvā tam roṣam vai mahātmanaḥ saṃcintya ugreṇa tapasā mahātmānam maheśvaram uśanāḥ yoga siddha ātmā śūla agre pratyadṛśyata vijñāta rūpaḥ sa tadā tapaḥ siddhena dhanvinā jñātvā śūlam ca deveśaḥ pāṇinā samanāmayat ānatena atha śūlena pāṇinā amita tejasā pinākam iti ca uvāca śūlam ugra āyudhaḥ prabhuḥ pāṇi madhya gatam dṛṣṭvā bhārgavam tam umāpatiḥ āsyam vivṛtya pāṇim saṃprākṣipat śanais sa tu praviṣṭaḥ uśanāḥ koṣṭham māheśvaram prabhuḥ vyacarat ca api tatra asau mahātmā bhṛgu nandanaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca jaṭhare devadevasya kim ca akārṣīt mahā dyutiḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca purā saḥ antar jala gataḥ sthāṇu bhūtaḥ mahā vrataḥ varṣāṇām abhavat rājan prayutāni arbudāni ca udatiṣṭhat tapaḥ taptvā duścaram sa mahā hradāt tapaḥ su cīrṇam iti ca provāca vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ tad saṃyogena vṛddhim ca api apaśyat sa tu śaṃkaraḥ vyarājata mahā rāja triṣu lokeṣu vīryavān tatas pinākī yoga ātmā dhyāna yogam samāviśat tuṣṭāva ca mahā yogī devam tatrasthaḥ eva ca niḥsāram kāṅkṣamāṇaḥ tu tejasā pratyahanyata uśanā tu tadā uvāca jaṭhara sthaḥ mahā muniḥ tam uvāca mahādevaḥ gaccha śiśnena mokṣaṇam iti srotāṃsi sarvāṇi ruddhvā tridaśa puṃgavaḥ apaśyamānaḥ sa dvāram sarvatas pihitaḥ muniḥ niṣkrāntam atha tam dṛṣṭvā jvalantam iva tejasā bhavaḥ roṣa samāviṣṭaḥ śūla udyata karaḥ sthitaḥ nyavārayata tam devī kruddham paśupatim patim hiṃsanīyaḥ tvayā na eṣa mama putra tvam āgataḥ na hi deva udarāt kaḥ cit niḥsṛtaḥ nāśam archati bhīṣmaḥ uvāca tatas prītaḥ abhavat devyāḥ prahasan ca idam abravīt gacchatu eṣa yathākāmam iti rājan punar punar tatas praṇamya vara dam devam devīm umām tathā uśanā prāpa tat dhīmān gatim iṣṭām mahā muniḥ caritam bharata śreṣṭha yat mām tvam paripṛcchasi yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca kim karma puruṣaḥ kṛtvā śubham puruṣa sattama bhīṣmaḥ uvāca atra te vartayiṣyāmi yathā pūrvam mahā yaśāḥ parāśaram mahātmānam papraccha janakaḥ nṛpaḥ kim śreyaḥ sarva bhūtānām asmin loke paratra ca nṛpāya anugraha manāḥ muniḥ vākyam atha abravīt tasmāt hi paramam na asti yathā prāhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ tasmin āśramiṇaḥ santaḥ sva karmāṇi iha kurvate martyāḥ yatra avatiṣṭhante sā ca kāmāt pravartate su kṛta a su kṛtam karma niṣevya vividhaiḥ kramaiḥ daśārdha pravibhaktānām bhūtānām bahudhā gatiḥ sauvarṇam rājatam vā api yathā bhāṇḍam niṣicyate tathā niṣicyate jantuḥ pūrva karma vaśa anugaḥ na a bījāt jāyate kim cit na a kṛtvā sukham edhate sukṛtī vindati sukham prāpya deha kṣayam naraḥ daivam tāta na paśyāmi na asti daivasya sādhanam pretya jāti kṛtam karma na smaranti sadā janāḥ lokayātrā āśrayaḥ ca eva śabdaḥ veda āśrayaḥ kṛtaḥ śānti artham manasaḥ tāta na etat vṛddha anuśāsanam cakṣuṣā manasā vācā karmaṇā ca caturvidham kurute yādṛśam karma tādṛśam pratipadyate kalyāṇam yadi vā pāpam na tu nāśaḥ asya vidyate kadā cit sukṛtam tāta kūṭastham iva tiṣṭhati majjamānasya saṃsāre yāvat duḥkhāt vimucyate tatas duḥkha kṣayam kṛtvā su kṛtam karma sevate sukṛta kṣayāt duṣkṛtam ca tat viddhi manuja adhipa damaḥ kṣamā dhṛtiḥ tejaḥ saṃtoṣaḥ satya vādi tā hrīḥ ahiṃsā avyasani tā dākṣyam ca iti sukha āvahāḥ nityam manaḥ samādhāne prayateta vicakṣaṇaḥ na ayam parasya sukṛtam duṣkṛtam vā api sevate karoti yādṛśam karma tādṛśam pratipadyate pareṣām yat asūyeta na tat kuryāt svayam naraḥ bhīruḥ rājanyaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ sarva bhakṣaḥ vaiśyaḥ anīhāvān hīna varṇaḥ alasaḥ ca vidvān ca aśīlaḥ vṛtta hīnaḥ kulīnaḥ satyāt bhraṣṭaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ strī ca duṣṭā rāgī muktaḥ pacamānaḥ mūrkhaḥ vaktā nṛpa hīnam ca rāṣṭram ete sarve śocya tām yānti rājan yaḥ ca ayuktaḥ sneha hīnaḥ prajāsu parāśaraḥ uvāca sevā āśritena manasā vṛtti hīnasya śasyate āyuḥ na sulabham labdhvā na avakarṣet viśām pate utkarṣa artham prayatate naraḥ puṇyena karmaṇā na tu yaḥ satkriyām prāpya rājasam karma sevate varṇa utkarṣam avāpnoti naraḥ puṇyena karmaṇā durlabham tam alabdhā hi hanyāt pāpena karmaṇā ajñānāt hi kṛtam pāpam tapasā eva abhinirṇudet na tat seveta medhāvī śuciḥ ku salilam yathā kiṃkaṣṭam anupaśyāmi phalam pāpasya karmaṇaḥ tasya api su mahān tāpaḥ prasthitasya upajāyate viraktam śodhyate vastram na tu kṛṣṇa upasaṃhitam svayam kṛtvā tu yaḥ pāpam śubham eva anutiṣṭhati prāyaścittam naraḥ kartum ubhayam saḥ aśnute pṛthak ajñānāt tu kṛtām hiṃsām ahiṃsā vyapakarṣati brāhmaṇāḥ śāstra nirdeśāt iti āhuḥ brahma vādinaḥ tathā kāma kṛtam ca asya vihiṃsā eva apakarṣati iti āhuḥ dharma śāstra jñāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ vedapāragāḥ guṇa yuktam prakāśam ca pāpena anupasaṃhitam yathā sūkṣmāṇi karmāṇi phalanti iha yathātatham buddhi yuktāni tāni iha kṛtāni manasā saha a buddhi pūrvam dharma jña kṛtam ugreṇa karmaṇā kṛtāni yāni karmāṇi daivataiḥ munibhiḥ tathā na ācaret tāni dharma ātmā śrutvā ca api na kutsayet saṃcintya manasā rājan viditvā śaktim ātmanaḥ karoti yaḥ śubham karma sa vai bhadrāṇi paśyati nave kapāle salilam saṃnyastam hīyate yathā evam karmāṇi yāni iha buddhi yuktāni bhūpate na samāni iha hīnāni tāni puṇyatamāni api rājñā jetavyāḥ sa āyudhāḥ ca unnatāḥ ca dama anvitaḥ puruṣaḥ dharma śīlaḥ bhūtāni ca ātmānam iva anupaśyet garīyasaḥ pūjayet ātma śaktyā parāśaraḥ uvāca prāṇī karoti ayam karma sarvam ātma artham ātmanā viśiṣṭasya viśiṣṭāt ca tulyau dāna pratigrahau saṃrakṣyam yatnam āsthāya dharma artham iti niścayaḥ na dharma arthī nṛśaṃsena karmaṇā dhanam arjayet apaḥ hi prayataḥ śītāḥ tāpitāḥ jvalanena vā śaktitas atithaye dattvā kṣudhā ārtāya aśnute phalam rantidevena loka iṣṭā siddhiḥ prāptā mahātmanā tasmāt lebhe param sthānam śaibyaḥ api pṛthivīpatiḥ ṛṇavān jāyate martyaḥ tasmāt anṛṇa tām vrajet pitṛbhyaḥ śrāddha dānena nṛṇām abhyarcanena ca vācaḥ śeṣa avahāryeṇa pālanena ātmanaḥ api ca ṛgbhiḥ stutvā mahābhāgaḥ devān vai yajña bhāginaḥ gataḥ śukra tvam uśanāḥ devadeva prasādanāt devīm stutvā tu gagane modate tejasā vṛtaḥ kakṣīvān jāmadagnyaḥ ca rāmaḥ tāṇḍyaḥ tathā aṃśumān bharadvājaḥ hariśmaśruḥ kuṇḍadhāraḥ śrutaśravāḥ ete mahā ṛṣayaḥ stutvā viṣṇum ṛgbhiḥ samāhitāḥ anarhāḥ ca arha tām prāptāḥ santaḥ stutvā tam eva ha dharmam vai śāśvatam loke na jahyāt dhana kāṅkṣayā āhitāgniḥ hi dharma ātmā yaḥ sa puṇya kṛt uttamaḥ agniḥ ātmā ca mātā ca pitā janayitā tathā guruḥ ca nara śārdūla paricaryāḥ yathātatham mānam tyaktvā yaḥ naraḥ vṛddha sevī vidvān klībaḥ paśyati prīti yogāt dākṣyeṇa ahīnaḥ dharma yuktaḥ na dāntaḥ parāśaraḥ uvāca vṛttiḥ sakāśāt varṇebhyaḥ tribhyaḥ hīnasya śobhanā prītyā upanītā nirdiṣṭā dharmiṣṭhān kurute sadā vṛttiḥ ced nā asti śūdrasya pitṛpaitāmahī dhruvā na vṛttim paratas mārget śuśrūṣām tu prayojayet tathā sat saṃnikarṣeṇa hīna varṇaḥ api dīpyate yādṛśena hi varṇena bhāvyate śuklam ambaram tasmāt guṇeṣu rajyethāḥ mā doṣeṣu kadā cana anityam iha martyānām jīvitam hi calācalam sukhe vā yadi vā duḥkhe vartamānaḥ vicakṣaṇaḥ yaḥ cinoti śubhāni eva sa bhadrāṇi iha paśyati yaḥ hṛtvā go sahasrāṇi nṛpaḥ dadyāt arakṣitā sa śabda mātra phala bhāj rājā bhavati taskaraḥ svayaṃbhūḥ asṛjat ca agre dhātāram loka pūjitam dhātā asṛjat putram ekam prajānām dhāraṇe ratam śūdraiḥ nirmārjanam kāryam evam dharmaḥ na naśyati sukhena tāsām rāja indra modante divi devatāḥ tasmāt yaḥ rakṣati nṛpaḥ sa dharmeṇa abhipūjyate adhīte ca api yaḥ vipraḥ vaiśyaḥ yaḥ ca arjane rataḥ yaḥ ca śuśrūṣate śūdraḥ satatam niyata indriyaḥ prāṇa saṃtāpa nirdiṣṭāḥ kākiṇyaḥ api mahā phalāḥ nyāyena upārjitāḥ dattāḥ kim uta anyāḥ sahasraśas yādṛśam tādṛśam nityam aśnāti phalam ūrjitam abhigamya dattam tuṣṭyā yat dhanyam āhuḥ abhiṣṭutam avajñayā dīyate yat tathā evā aśraddhayā api ca tat āhuḥ adhamam dānam munayaḥ satya vādinaḥ tathā prayatnam kurvīta yathā mucyeta saṃśayāt dhanena vaiśyaḥ śūdraḥ tu nityam dākṣyeṇa śobhate parāśaraḥ uvāca vaiśye nyāya arjitāḥ ca eva śūdre śuśrūṣayā arjitāḥ arthāḥ praśasyante dharmasya arthe mahā phalāḥ nityam trayāṇām varṇānām śūdraḥ śuśrūṣuḥ ucyate kṣatra dharmāḥ vaiśya dharmāḥ na āvṛttiḥ patati dvijaḥ śūdra karmā yadā tu syāt tadā patati vai dvijaḥ vāṇijyam pāśupālyam ca tathā śilpa upajīvanam śūdrasya api vidhīyante yadā vṛttiḥ na jāyate raṅga avataraṇam ca eva tathā rūpa upajīvanam madya māṃsa upajīvyam ca vikrayaḥ loha carmaṇoḥ śrūyante hi purāṇe vai prajāḥ dhigdaṇḍa śāsanāḥ dāntāḥ dharma pradhānāḥ ca nyāya dharma anuvartakāḥ dharmaḥ eva sadā nṝṇām iha rājan praśasyate tam dharmam asurāḥ tāta na amṛṣyanta janādhipa vivardhamānāḥ kramaśas tatra te anvāviśan prajāḥ teṣām darpaḥ samabhavat prajānām dharma nāśanaḥ darpa ātmanām tatas krodhaḥ punar teṣām ajāyata tatas krodha abhibhūtānām vṛttam lajjā samanvitam hrīḥ ca eva api anaśat rājan tatas mohaḥ vyajāyata tatas moha parītāḥ te na apaśyanta yathā purā tān prāpya tu sa dhik daṇḍaḥ na kāraṇam atas abhavat tatas abhyagacchan devān ca brāhmaṇān ca avamanya ha agacchan śaraṇam vīram bahu rūpam gaṇādhipam tena sma te gagana gāḥ sa purāḥ pātitāḥ kṣitau teṣām adhipatiḥ tu āsīt bhīmaḥ bhīma parākramaḥ devatānām bhaya karaḥ sa hataḥ śūlapāṇinā prāvartanta ca vedāḥ vai śāstrāṇi ca yathā purā tatas abhyaṣiñcan rājyena devānām divi vāsavam saptarṣayaḥ ca anvayuñjan narāṇām daṇḍa dhāraṇe saptarṣīṇām atha ūrdhvam ca vipṛthuḥ nāma pārthivaḥ rājānaḥ kṣatriyāḥ ca eva maṇḍaleṣu pṛthak pṛthak mahā kuleṣu ye jātāḥ vṛttāḥ pūrvatarāḥ ca ye teṣām atha asuraḥ bhāvaḥ hṛdayāt na apasarpati tasmāt tena eva bhāvena sa anuṣaṅgena pārthivāḥ āsurāṇi eva karmāṇi nyaṣevan bhīma vikramāḥ pratyatiṣṭhan ca teṣu eva tāni eva sthāpayanti ca bhajante tāni ca adya api ye bāliśatamāḥ narāḥ tasmāt aham bravīmi tvām rājan saṃcintya śāstrataḥ saṃsiddha adhigamam kuryāt karma hiṃsā ātmakam tyajet na saṃkareṇa draviṇam vicinvīta vicakṣaṇaḥ sa tvam evaṃvidhaḥ dāntaḥ kṣatriyaḥ priya bāndhavaḥ prajāḥ bhṛtyān ca putrān ca svadharmeṇa anupālaya iṣṭa aniṣṭa samāyogaḥ vairam sauhārdam eva ca tasmāt guṇeṣu rajyethāḥ mā doṣeṣu kadā cana mānuṣeṣu mahā rāja dharma adharmau pravartataḥ na tathā anyeṣu bhūteṣu manuṣya rahiteṣu iha dharma śīlaḥ naraḥ vidvān īhakaḥ anīhakaḥ api vā ātma bhūtaḥ sadā loke caret bhūtāni a hiṃsayan na anṛtam ca eva bhavati tadā kalyāṇam ṛcchati parāśaraḥ uvāca tapaḥ vidhim tu vakṣyāmi tat me nigadataḥ śṛṇu prāyeṇa hi gṛhasthasya mamatvam nāma jāyate saṅga āgatam nara śreṣṭha bhāvaiḥ tāmasa rājasaiḥ gṛhāṇi āśritya gāvaḥ ca kṣetrāṇi ca dhanāni ca dārāḥ putrāḥ ca bhṛtyāḥ ca bhavanti iha narasya vai rāga dveṣa abhibhūtam ca naram dravya vaśa anugam kṛtārthaḥ bhogataḥ bhūtvā sa vai rati parāyaṇaḥ lābham grāmya sukhāt anyam ratitaḥ na anupaśyati puṣṭi artham ca eva tasya iha janasya artham cikīrṣati sa jānan api ca akāryam artha artham sevate naraḥ bāla sneha parīta ātmā tad kṣayāt ca anutapyate tapaḥ hi buddhi yuktānām śāśvatam brahma darśanam anvicchatām śubham karma narāṇām tyajatām sukham sneha āyatana nāśāt ca dhana nāśāt ca pārthiva nirvedāt ātma saṃbodhaḥ saṃbodhāt śāstra darśanam śāstra artha darśanāt rājan tapaḥ eva anupaśyati tapaḥ sarva gatam tāta hīnasya api vidhīyate prajāpatiḥ prajāḥ pūrvam asṛjat tapasā vibhuḥ ādityāḥ vasavaḥ rudrāḥ tathā eva agni aśvi mārutāḥ viśvedevāḥ tathā sādhyāḥ pitaraḥ atha marut gaṇāḥ yakṣa rākṣasa gandharvāḥ siddhāḥ ca anye divaukasaḥ saṃsiddhāḥ tapasā tāta ye ca anye svarga vāsinaḥ ye ca ādau brahmaṇā sṛṣṭāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ tapasā purā te bhāvayantaḥ pṛthivīm vicaranti divam tathā mahā kuleṣu dṛśyante tat sarvam tapasaḥ phalam kauśikāni ca vastrāṇi śubhāni ābharaṇāni ca vāhana āsana yānāni sarvam tat tapasaḥ phalam manonukūlāḥ pramadāḥ rūpavatyaḥ sahasraśas vāsaḥ prāsāda pṛṣṭhe ca tat sarvam tapasaḥ phalam abhipretāni sarvāṇi bhavanti kṛta karmaṇām upabhoga parityāgaḥ phalāni akṛta karmaṇām avekṣya manasā śāstram buddhyā ca nṛpa sattama tatas asya naśyati prajñā vidyā iva abhyāsa varjitā naṣṭa prajñaḥ yadā bhavati tadā nyāyam na paśyati yat iṣṭam tat sukham prāhuḥ dveṣyam duḥkham iha ucyate kṛta akṛtasya tapasaḥ phalam paśyasva yādṛśam nityam bhadrāṇi paśyanti viṣayān ca upabhuñjate prākāśyam ca eva gacchanti kṛtvā niṣkalmaṣam tapaḥ apriyāṇi avamānān ca duḥkham bahuvidha ātmakam sva vṛttāt yaḥ na calati śāstra cakṣuḥ sa mānavaḥ iṣu prapāta mātram hi sparśa yoge ratiḥ smṛtā rasane darśane ghrāṇe śravaṇe ca viśām pate tatas asya jāyate tīvrā vedanā tad kṣayāt punar tatas phala artham carati bhavanti jyāyasaḥ guṇāḥ dharma vṛttyā ca satatam kāma arthābhyām na hīyate aprayatna āgatāḥ sevyāḥ gṛhasthaiḥ viṣayāḥ sadā māninām kula jātānām nityam śāstra artha cakṣuṣām dharma kriyā viyuktānām aśaktyā saṃvṛta ātmanām kriyamāṇam yadā karma nāśam gacchati mānuṣam teṣām na anyat ṛte loke tapasaḥ karma vidyate dākṣyeṇa havya kavya artham svadharmam vicaret nṛpa yathā nadīnadāḥ sarve sāgare yānti saṃsthitim evam āśramiṇaḥ sarve gṛhasthe yānti saṃsthitim varṇaḥ viśeṣa varṇānām mahā ṛṣe kena jāyate etat icchāmi aham śrotum tat brūhi vadatām vara katham brāhmaṇataḥ jātaḥ viśeṣa grahaṇam gataḥ parāśaraḥ uvāca evam etat mahā rāja yena jātaḥ saḥ eva saḥ tapasaḥ tu apakarṣeṇa jāti grahaṇa tām gataḥ su kṣetrāt ca su bījāt ca puṇyaḥ bhavati saṃbhavaḥ vaktrāt bhujābhyām ūrubhyām padbhyām ca eva atha jajñire mukha jāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ tāta bāhu jāḥ kṣatra bandhavaḥ ūru jāḥ dhaninaḥ rājan pāda jāḥ paricārakāḥ caturṇām eva varṇānām āgamaḥ puruṣa ṛṣabha atas anye tu atiriktāḥ ye te vai saṃkara jāḥ smṛtāḥ kṣatra jātiḥ atha ambaṣṭhāḥ ugrāḥ vaidehakāḥ tathā śvapākāḥ pulkasāḥ stenāḥ niṣādāḥ sūta māgadhāḥ āyogāḥ karaṇāḥ vrātyāḥ caṇḍālāḥ ca narādhipa brahmaṇā ekena jātānām nānātvam gotrataḥ katham yatra tatra katham jātāḥ sva yonim munayaḥ gatāḥ parāśaraḥ uvāca mahātmanām samutpattiḥ tapasā bhāvitātmanām svena eva tapasā teṣām ṛṣi tvam vidadhuḥ punar pitāmahaḥ ca me pūrvam ṛśyaśṛṅgaḥ ca kāśyapaḥ vaṭaḥ tāṇḍyaḥ kṛpaḥ ca eva kakṣīvān kamaṭha ādayaḥ yavakrītaḥ ca nṛpate droṇaḥ ca vadatām varaḥ ete svām prakṛtim prāptāḥ vaideha tapasaḥ mūla gotrāṇi catvāri samutpannāni pārthiva aṅgirāḥ kaśyapaḥ ca eva vasiṣṭhaḥ bhṛguḥ eva ca nāmadheyāni tapasā tāni ca grahaṇam satām viśeṣa dharmān varṇānām prabrūhi bhagavat mama tathā sāmānya dharmān ca sarvatra kuśalaḥ hi asi parāśaraḥ uvāca pratigrahaḥ yājanam ca tathā eva adhyāpanam nṛpa viśeṣa dharmaḥ viprāṇām rakṣā kṣatrasya śobhanā kṛṣiḥ ca pāśupālyam ca vāṇijyam ca viśām api dvijānām paricaryā ca śūdra karma narādhipa viśeṣa dharmāḥ nṛpate varṇānām parikīrtitāḥ dharmān sādhāraṇān tāta vistareṇa śṛṇuṣva me ānṛśaṃsyam ahiṃsā ca apramādaḥ saṃvibhāgi tā sveṣu dāreṣu saṃtoṣaḥ śaucam nitya anasūya tā ātma jñānam titikṣā ca dharmāḥ sādhāraṇāḥ nṛpa brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ trayaḥ varṇāḥ dvijātayaḥ atra teṣām adhīkāraḥ dharmeṣu dvipadām vara vikarma avasthitāḥ varṇāḥ patanti nṛpate trayaḥ na ca api śūdraḥ patati iti niścayaḥ na ca api saṃskāram iha arhati iti vā vaidehakam śūdram udāharanti dvijāḥ mahā rāja śruta upapannāḥ aham hi paśyāmi narendra devam viśvasya viṣṇum jagataḥ pradhānam satām vṛttam anuṣṭhāya nihīnāḥ ujjihīrṣavaḥ mantra varjam na duṣyanti kurvāṇāḥ pauṣṭikīḥ kriyāḥ yathā yathā hi sat vṛttam ālambanti itare janāḥ parāśaraḥ uvāca asaṃśayam mahā rājaḥ ubhayam doṣa kārakam karma ca eva hi jātiḥ ca viśeṣam tu niśāmaya jātyā ca karmaṇā ca eva duṣṭam karma niṣevate jātyā duṣṭaḥ ca yaḥ pāpam na karoti sa pūruṣaḥ jātyā pradhānam puruṣam kurvāṇam karma dhikkṛtam na hiṃsanti iha bhūtāni kriyamāṇāni sarvadā parāśaraḥ uvāca śṛṇu me atra mahā rāja yat mām tvam paripṛcchasi yāni karmāṇi ahiṃsrāṇi naram trāyanti sarvadā saṃnyasya agnīn upāsīnāḥ paśyanti vigata jvarāḥ praśritāḥ vinaya upetāḥ dama nityāḥ su saṃśitāḥ sarve varṇāḥ dharma kāryāṇi samyak kṛtvā rājan satya vākyāni ca uktvā tyaktvā adharmam dāruṇam jīva loke yānti svargam na atra kāryaḥ vicāraḥ parāśaraḥ uvāca an anya bhaktāḥ priya vādinaḥ ca hitāḥ ca vaśyāḥ ca tathā eva rājan pitā param daivatam mānavānām mātuḥ viśiṣṭam pitaram vadanti jñānasya lābham paramam vadanti jita indriya arthāḥ param āpnuvanti raṇa ajire yatra śara agni saṃstare nṛpa ātmajaḥ ghātam avāpya dahyate śrāntam bhītam bhraṣṭa śastram rudantam parāṅmukham paribarhaiḥ ca hīnam an udyatam rogiṇam yācamānam na vai hiṃsyāt bāla vṛddhau ca rājan atikrameta nṛpatiḥ saṃgrāme kṣatriya ātmajam tulyāt iha vadhaḥ śreyān viśiṣṭāt ca iti niścayaḥ nihīnāt kātarāt ca eva nṛpāṇām garhitaḥ vadhaḥ pāpāt pāpa samācārāt nihīnāt ca narādhipa na kaḥ cit trāti vai rājan diṣṭānta vaśam āgatam sa avaśeṣa āyuṣam ca api kaḥ cit eva apakarṣati snigdhaiḥ ca kriyamāṇāni karmāṇi iha nivartayet hiṃsā ātmakāni karmāṇi na āyuḥ icchet para āyuṣā gṛhasthānām tu sarveṣām vināśam abhikāṅkṣatām nidhanam śobhanam tāta pulineṣu kriyāvatām na akāraṇāt tat bhavati kāraṇaiḥ upapāditam tathā śarīram bhavati dehāt yena upapāditam adhvānam gatakaḥ ca ayam prāptaḥ ca ayam gṛhāt gṛham dvitīyam kāraṇam tatra na anyat kim cana vidyate tat deham dehinām yuktam mokṣa bhūteṣu vartate sirā snāyu asthi saṃghātam bībhatsa amedhya saṃkulam bhūtānām indriyāṇām ca guṇānām ca samāgamam tvac antam deham iti āhuḥ vidvāṃsaḥ adhyātma cintakāḥ guṇaiḥ api parikṣīṇam śarīram martya tām gatam śarīriṇā parityaktam niśceṣṭam gata cetanam tad svabhāvaḥ aparaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ visargaḥ karmaṇaḥ tathā na jāyate tu nṛpate kam cit kālam ayam punar paribhramati bhūtātmā dyām iva ambudharaḥ mahān sa punar jāyate rājan prāpya iha āyatanam nṛpa dvividhānām ca bhūtānām jaṅgamāḥ paramāḥ nṛpa jaṅgamānām api tathā dvipadāḥ paramāḥ matāḥ dvipadānām api tathā dvijāḥ vai paramāḥ smṛtāḥ dvijānām api rāja indra prajñāvantaḥ parāḥ matāḥ prājñānām ātma saṃbuddhāḥ saṃbuddhānām amāninaḥ jātam anveti maraṇam nṛṇām iti viniścayaḥ antavanti hi karmāṇi sevante guṇataḥ prajāḥ āpanne tu uttarām kāṣṭhām sūrye yaḥ nidhanam vrajet nakṣatre ca muhūrte ca puṇye rājan sa puṇya kṛt a yojayitvā kleśena janam plāvya ca duṣkṛtam mṛtyunā aprākṛtena iha karma kṛtvā ātma śaktitaḥ daṃṣṭribhyaḥ ca paśubhyaḥ ca prākṛtaḥ vadhaḥ ucyate na ca ebhiḥ puṇya karmāṇaḥ yujyante na abhisaṃdhi jaiḥ ūrdhvam hitvā pratiṣṭhante prāṇāḥ puṇya kṛtām nṛpa madhyatas madhya puṇyānām adhas duṣkṛta karmaṇām ekaḥ śatruḥ na dvitīyaḥ asti śatruḥ ajñāna tulyaḥ puruṣasya rājan yena āvṛtaḥ kurute saṃprayuktaḥ ghorāṇi karmāṇi su dāruṇāni adhītya vedān tapasā brahmacārī yajñān śaktyā saṃnisṛjya iha pañca vanam gacchet puruṣaḥ dharma kāmaḥ śreyaḥ citvā sthāpayitvā sva vaṃśam caṇḍāla tve api mānuṣyam sarvathā tāta durlabham iyam hi yoniḥ prathamā yām prāpya jagatīpate ātmā vai śakyate trātum karmabhiḥ śubha lakṣaṇaiḥ kurvanti dharmam manujāḥ śruti prāmāṇya darśanāt yaḥ tu prīti purogeṇa cakṣuṣā tāta paśyati dīpa upamāni bhūtāni yāvat arciḥ na naśyati dānam tyāgaḥ śobhanā mūrtiḥ adbhyaḥ bhūyas plāvyam tapasā vai śarīram sarasvatī naimiṣa puṣkareṣu ye ca api anye puṇya deśāḥ pṛthivyām gṛheṣu yeṣām asavaḥ patanti teṣām atha u nirharaṇam praśastam yānena vai prāpaṇam ca śmaśāne śaucena nūnam vidhinā ca eva dāhaḥ iṣṭiḥ puṣṭiḥ yajanam yājanam ca śaktyā pitryam yat ca kim cit praśastam sarvāṇi ātma arthe mānavaḥ yaḥ karoti dharma śāstrāṇi vedāḥ ca ṣaṣ aṅgāni narādhipa śreyasaḥ arthe vidhīyante narasya akliṣṭa karmaṇaḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca vai sarvam ākhyātam muninā su mahātmanā bhīṣmaḥ uvāca parāśaram mahātmānam dharme parama niścayam kim śreyaḥ kā gatiḥ brahman kim kṛtam na vinaśyati parāśaraḥ uvāca asaṅgaḥ śreyasaḥ mūlam jñānam jñāna gatiḥ parā cīrṇam tapaḥ na praṇaśyet vāpaḥ kṣetre na naśyati dattvā abhaya kṛtam dānam tadā siddhim avāpnuyāt yaḥ dadāti sahasrāṇi gavām aśva śatāni ca na adharmaḥ śliṣyate prājñam āpaḥ puṣkaraparṇa vat aprājñam adhikam pāpam śliṣyate jatu kāṣṭha vat na adharmaḥ kāraṇa apekṣī kartāram abhimuñcati na bhidyante kṛtātmānaḥ ātma pratyaya darśinaḥ śubha aśubheṣu sakta ātmā prāpnoti su mahat bhayam puṣṭa srotaḥ iva āyattaḥ sphītaḥ bhavati saṃcayaḥ yathā bhānu gatam tejaḥ maṇiḥ śuddhaḥ samādhinā ādatte rāja śārdūla tathā yogaḥ pravartate yathā tilānām iha puṣpa saṃśrayāt pṛthak pṛthak yāti guṇaḥ ati saumya tām tathā narāṇām bhuvi bhāvitātmanām yathāśrayam sattva guṇaḥ pravartate jahāti dārān ihate na saṃpadaḥ sa sarva bhāva anugatena cetasā nṛpa āmiṣeṇa iva jhaṣaḥ vikṛṣyate saṃghātavān martya lokaḥ parasparam apāśritaḥ na dharma kālaḥ puruṣasya niścitaḥ na ca api mṛtyuḥ puruṣam pratīkṣate tathā yuktena manasā prājñaḥ gacchati tām gatim yathā mṛṇālaḥ anugatam āśu muñcati kardamam tathā śarīram tapasā taptam viṣayam aśnute viṣayān aśnute yaḥ tu na sa bhokṣyati asaṃśayam nīhāreṇa hi saṃvītaḥ śiśna udara parāyaṇaḥ jāti andhaḥ iva panthānam āvṛta ātmā na budhyate tathā martya arṇave jantoḥ karma vijñānataḥ gatiḥ svayam kṛtāni karmāṇi jātaḥ jantuḥ prapadyate śayānam yāntam āsīnam pravṛttam viṣayeṣu ca śubha aśubhāni karmāṇi prapadyante naram sadā yathā bhāra avasaktā hi nauḥ mahā ambhasi tantunā tathā manaḥ abhiyogāt vai śarīram pratikarṣati yathā samudram abhitas saṃsyūtāḥ saritaḥ aparāḥ tathā ādyā prakṛtiḥ yogāt abhisaṃsyūyate sadā śarīragṛha saṃsthasya śauca tīrthasya dehinaḥ vistarāḥ kleśa saṃyuktāḥ saṃkṣepāḥ tu sukha āvahāḥ para artham vistarāḥ sarve tyāgam ātma hitam viduḥ saṃkalpa jaḥ mitra vargaḥ jñātayaḥ kāraṇa ātmakāḥ bhāryāḥ dāsāḥ ca putrāḥ ca svam artham anuyuñjate mātā putraḥ pitā bhrātā bhāryā mitra janaḥ tathā sarvāṇi karmāṇi purā kṛtāni śubha aśubhāni ātmanaḥ yānti jantoḥ vyavasāyam samāśritya sahāyān yaḥ adhigacchati a dvaidha manasam yuktam śūram dhīram vipaścitam na śrīḥ saṃtyajate nityam ādityam iva raśmayaḥ āstikya vyavasāyābhyām upāyāt vismayāt dhiyā sarvaḥ svāni śubha aśubhāni niyatam karmāṇi jantuḥ svayam mṛtyuḥ ca aparihāravān sama gatiḥ kālena viccheditā dāroḥ cūrṇam iva aśmasāra vihitam karma antikam prāpayet sva rūpa tām ātma kṛtam ca vistaram kula anvayam dravya samṛddhi saṃcayam naraḥ hi sarvaḥ labhate yathākṛtam śubha aśubhena ātma kṛtena karmaṇā bhīṣmaḥ uvāca iti uktaḥ janakaḥ rājan yathātathyam manīṣiṇā śrutvā dharma vidām śreṣṭhaḥ parām mudam avāpa ha yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca satyam kṣamām damam prajñām praśaṃsanti pitāmaha bhīṣmaḥ uvāca sādhyānām iha saṃvādam haṃsasya ca yudhiṣṭhira haṃsaḥ bhūtvā atha sauvarṇaḥ tu ajaḥ nityaḥ prajāpatiḥ sādhyāḥ ūcuḥ pṛcchāmaḥ tvām mokṣa dharmam bhavān ca kila mokṣa vid śrutaḥ asi naḥ paṇḍitaḥ dhīra vādī sādhu śabdaḥ patate te patatrin tat naḥ kāryam pakṣi vara praśādhi yat kāryāṇām manyase śreṣṭham ekam haṃsaḥ uvāca idam kāryam amṛta āśāḥ śṛṇomi tapaḥ damaḥ satyam ātma abhiguptiḥ nāruṃtudaḥ syāt na nṛśaṃsa vādī na hīnataḥ param abhyādadīta yayā asya vācā paraḥ udvijeta na tām vadet ruśatīm pāpa lokyām vāc sāyakāḥ vadanāt niṣpatanti yaiḥ āhataḥ śocati rātri ahāni paraḥ ced enam ativāda bāṇaiḥ bhṛśam vidhyet śamaḥ eva iha kāryaḥ saṃroṣyamāṇaḥ pratimṛṣyate yaḥ saḥ ādatte sukṛtam vai parasya kṣepa abhimānāt abhiṣaṅga vyalīkam nigṛhṇāti jvalitam yaḥ ca manyum aduṣṭa cetāḥ muditaḥ anasūyuḥ saḥ ādatte sukṛtam vai pareṣām ākruśyamānaḥ na vadāmi kim cit kṣamāmi aham tāḍyamānaḥ ca nityam śreṣṭham hi etat kṣamam api āhuḥ āryāḥ satyam tathā eva ārjavam ānṛśaṃsyam etān vegān yaḥ viṣahati udīrṇān tam manye aham brāhmaṇam vai munim ca akrodhanaḥ krudhyatām vai viśiṣṭaḥ tathā titikṣuḥ a titikṣoḥ viśiṣṭaḥ amānuṣāt mānuṣaḥ vai viśiṣṭaḥ tathā ajñānāt jñānavān vai pradhānaḥ ākruśyamānaḥ na ākrośet manyuḥ eva titikṣataḥ ākroṣṭāram nirdahati sukṛtam ca asya vindati yaḥ na atyuktaḥ prāha rūkṣam priyam vā pāpīyasaḥ kṣameta eva śreyasaḥ sadṛśasya ca vimānitaḥ hataḥ evam siddhim gamiṣyati sadā aham āryān nibhṛtaḥ api upāse na me vivitsā na ca me asti roṣaḥ na ca api aham lipsamānaḥ paraimi na ca eva kim cit viṣameṇa yāmi na aham śaptaḥ pratiśapāmi kim cit damam dvāram hi amṛtasya iha vedmi guhyam brahma tat idam vaḥ bravīmi na mānuṣāt śreṣṭhataram hi kim cit virajāḥ kālam ākāṅkṣan dhīraḥ dhairyeṇa sidhyati yasmai vācam su praśastām vadanti sa vai devān gacchati saṃyata ātmā na tathā vaktum icchanti kalyāṇān puruṣe guṇān yathā eṣām vaktum icchanti nairguṇyam anuyuñjakāḥ vedāḥ tapaḥ ca tyāgaḥ ca saḥ idam sarvam āpnuyāt ākrośana avamānābhyām abudhāt vardhate budhaḥ catvāri yasya dvārāṇi su guptāni amara uttamāḥ satyam damam hi ārjavam ānṛśaṃsyam svādhyāya nityaḥ a spṛhayan pareṣām ekānta śīlī ūrdhva gatiḥ bhavet saḥ satyam svargasya sopānam pārāvārasya nauḥ iva yādṛśaiḥ saṃnivasati yādṛśān ca upasevate yādṛś icchet ca bhavitum tādṛś bhavati pūruṣaḥ vāsaḥ yathā raṅga vaśam prayāti tathā sa teṣām vaśam abhyupaiti sadā devāḥ sādhubhiḥ saṃvadante na mānuṣam viṣayam yānti draṣṭum na induḥ samaḥ syāt asamaḥ hi vāyuḥ uccāvacam viṣayam yaḥ sa veda aduṣṭam vartamāne tu hṛdaya antara pūruṣe śiśna udare ye abhiratāḥ sadā eva stenāḥ narāḥ vāc paruṣāḥ ca nityam apeta doṣān iti tān viditvā dūrāt devāḥ saṃparivarjayanti na vai devāḥ hīna sattvena toṣyāḥ sarva āśinā duṣkṛta karmaṇā vā satya vratāḥ ye tu narāḥ kṛtajñāḥ dharme ratāḥ taiḥ saha saṃbhajante a vyāhṛtam vyāhṛtāt śreyaḥ āhuḥ satyam vadet vyāhṛtam tat dvitīyam dharmam vadet vyāhṛtam tat tṛtīyam priyam vadet vyāhṛtam tat caturtham sādhyāḥ ūcuḥ kena ayam āvṛtaḥ lokaḥ kena vā na prakāśate haṃsaḥ uvāca ajñānena āvṛtaḥ lokaḥ mātsaryāt na prakāśate sādhyāḥ ūcuḥ kaḥ svid ekaḥ ramate brāhmaṇānām kaḥ svid ekaḥ bahubhiḥ joṣam āste haṃsaḥ uvāca prājñaḥ ekaḥ ramate brāhmaṇānām prājñaḥ ekaḥ bahubhiḥ joṣam āste prājñaḥ ekaḥ balavān durbalaḥ api prājñaḥ eṣām kalaham na anvavaiti sādhyāḥ ūcuḥ kim brāhmaṇānām deva tvam kim ca sādhu tvam ucyate asādhu tvam ca kim teṣām kim eṣām mānuṣam matam haṃsaḥ uvāca svādhyāyaḥ eṣām deva tvam vratam sādhu tvam ucyate asādhu tvam parīvādaḥ mṛtyuḥ mānuṣam ucyate bhīṣmaḥ uvāca saṃvādaḥ iti ayam śreṣṭhaḥ sādhyānām parikīrtitaḥ kṣetram vai karmaṇām yoniḥ sadbhāvaḥ satyam ucyate yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca sāṃkhye yoge ca me tāta viśeṣam vaktum arhasi bhīṣmaḥ uvāca sāṃkhyāḥ sāṃkhyam praśaṃsanti yogāḥ yogam dvijātayaḥ vadanti kāraṇaiḥ śraiṣṭhyam sva pakṣa udbhāvanāya vai anīśvaraḥ katham mucyet iti evam śatru karśana vadanti kāraṇaiḥ śraiṣṭhyam yogāḥ samyak manīṣiṇaḥ vadanti kāraṇam ca idam sāṃkhyāḥ samyak dvijātayaḥ vijñāya iha gatīḥ sarvāḥ viraktaḥ viṣayeṣu yaḥ etat āhuḥ mahā prājñāḥ sāṃkhyam vai mokṣa darśanam sva pakṣe kāraṇam grāhyam samartham vacanam hitam śiṣṭānām hi matam grāhyam tvadvidhaiḥ śiṣṭa saṃmataiḥ pratyakṣa hetavaḥ yogāḥ sāṃkhyāḥ śāstra viniścayāḥ ubhe ca ete mate jñāne nṛpate śiṣṭa saṃmate anuṣṭhite yathāśāstram nayetām paramām gatim tulyam śaucam tayoḥ yuktam dayā bhūteṣu ca anagha vratānām dhāraṇam tulyam darśanam na samam tayoḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca yadi tulyam vratam śaucam dayā ca atra pitāmaha tulyam na darśanam kasmāt tat me brūhi pitāmaha bhīṣmaḥ uvāca rāgam moham tathā sneham kāmam krodham ca kevalam yogāt chittvā āditas doṣān pañca etān prāpnuvanti tat yathā ca animiṣāḥ sthūlāḥ jālam chittvā punar jalam prāpnuvanti tathā yogāḥ tat padam vīta kalmaṣāḥ tathā eva vāgurām chittvā balavantaḥ yathā mṛgāḥ prāpnuyuḥ vimalam mārgam vimuktāḥ sarva bandhanaiḥ lobha jāni tathā rājan bandhanāni bala anvitāḥ chittvā yogāḥ param mārgam gacchanti vimalāḥ śivam abalāḥ ca mṛgāḥ rājan vāgurāsu tathā apare bala hīnāḥ ca kaunteya yathā jāla gatāḥ jhaṣāḥ antam gacchanti rāja indra tathā yogāḥ su durbalāḥ yathā ca śakunāḥ sūkṣmāḥ prāpya jālam ariṃdama alpakaḥ ca yathā rājan vahniḥ śāmyati durbalaḥ samīraṇa yutaḥ kṛtsnām dahet kṣipram mahīm api tadvat jāta balaḥ yogī dīpta tejāḥ mahā balaḥ antakāle iva ādityaḥ kṛtsnam saṃśoṣayet jagat tat eva ca yathā srotaḥ viṣṭambhayati vāraṇaḥ viśanti ca avaśāḥ pārtha yogāḥ yoga bala anvitāḥ prajāpatīn ṛṣīn devān mahābhūtāni ca īśvarāḥ ātmanām ca sahasrāṇi bahūni bharata ṛṣabha yogaḥ kuryāt balam prāpya taiḥ ca sarvaiḥ mahīm caret prāpnuyāt viṣayān ca eva punar ca ugram tapaḥ caret saṃkṣipet ca punar pārtha sūryaḥ tejaḥ guṇān iva balāni yoge proktāni mayā etāni viśām pate nidarśana artham sūkṣmāṇi vakṣyāmi ca punar tava ātmanaḥ ca samādhāne dhāraṇām prati ca abhibho nidarśanāni sūkṣmāṇi śṛṇu me bharata ṛṣabha yuktaḥ samyak tathā yogī mokṣam prāpnoti asaṃśayam sneha pūrṇe yathā pātre manaḥ ādhāya niścalam puruṣaḥ yattaḥ ārohet sopānam yukta mānasaḥ yuktvā tathā ayam ātmānam yogaḥ pārthiva niścalam yathā ca nāvam kaunteya karṇadhāraḥ samāhitaḥ mahā arṇava gatām śīghram nayet pārthiva pattanam durgamam sthānam āpnoti hitvā deham imam nṛpa sārathiḥ ca yathā yuktvā sat aśvān su samāhitaḥ deśam iṣṭam nayati āśu dhanvinam puruṣa ṛṣabha tathā eva nṛpate yogī dhāraṇāsu samāhitaḥ prāpnoti āśu param sthānam lakṣam muktaḥ iva āśugaḥ āveśya ātmani ca ātmānam yogī tiṣṭhati yaḥ acalaḥ pāpam hantā iva mīnānām padam āpnoti saḥ ajaram nābhyām kaṇṭhe ca śīrṣe ca hṛdi vakṣasi pārśvayoḥ darśane sparśane ca api ghrāṇe ca amita vikrama sthāneṣu eteṣu yaḥ yogī mahā vrata samāhitaḥ ātmanā sūkṣmam ātmānam yuṅkte samyak viśām pate sa śīghram amala prajñaḥ karma dagdhvā śubha aśubham yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca āhārān kīdṛśān kṛtvā kāni jitvā ca bhārata bhīṣmaḥ uvāca kaṇānām bhakṣaṇe yuktaḥ piṇyākasya ca bhakṣaṇe snehānām varjane yuktaḥ yogī balam avāpnuyāt bhuñjānaḥ yāvakam rūkṣam dīrgha kālam ariṃdama eka ārāmaḥ viśuddha ātmā yogī balam avāpnuyāt pakṣān māsān ṛtūn citrān saṃcaran ca guhāḥ tathā apaḥ pītvā payaḥ miśrāḥ yogī balam avāpnuyāt akhaṇḍam api vā māsam satatam manuja īśvara upoṣya samyak śuddha ātmā yogī balam avāpnuyāt kāmam jitvā tathā krodham śīta uṣṇe varṣam eva ca bhayam nidrām tathā śvāsam pauruṣam viṣayān tathā aratim durjayām ca eva ghorām tṛṣṇām ca pārthiva sparśān sarvān tathā tandrīm durjayām nṛpa sattama dīpayanti mahātmānaḥ sūkṣmam ātmānam ātmanā vīta rāgāḥ mahā prājñāḥ dhyāna adhyayana saṃpadā durgaḥ tu eṣa mataḥ panthāḥ brāhmaṇānām vipaścitām yathā kaḥ cit vanam ghoram bahu sarpa sarīsṛpam abhaktam aṭavī prāyam dāva dagdha mahīruham panthānam taskara ākīrṇam kṣemeṇa abhipatet yuvā yoga mārgam tathā āsādya yaḥ kaḥ cit bhajate dvijaḥ kṣemeṇa uparamet mārgāt bahu doṣaḥ hi sa smṛtaḥ sustheyam kṣura dhārāsu niśitāsu mahīpate dhāraṇāsu tu yogasya duḥstheyam akṛtātmabhiḥ vipannāḥ dhāraṇāḥ tāta nayanti naśubhām gatim netṛ hīnāḥ yathā nāvaḥ puruṣān arṇave nṛpa yaḥ tu tiṣṭhati kaunteya dhāraṇāsu yathāvidhi maraṇam janma duḥkham ca sukham ca sa vimuñcati nānā śāstreṣu niṣpannam yogeṣu idam udāhṛtam param yogam tu yat kṛtsnam niścitam tat dvijātiṣu param hi tat brahma mahat mahātman brahmāṇam īśam vara dam ca viṣṇum bhavam ca dharmam ca ṣaḍānanam ca ṣaṣ brahma putrān ca mahā anubhāvān tamaḥ ca kaṣṭam su mahat rajaḥ ca sattvam ca śuddham prakṛtim parām ca siddhim ca devīm varuṇasya patnīm tejaḥ ca kṛtsnam su mahat ca dhairyam tārādhipam vai vimalam sa tāram viśvān ca devān uragān pitṝn ca śailān ca kṛtsnān udadhīn ca ghorān nadīḥ ca sarvāḥ sa vanān ghanān ca nāgān nagān yakṣa gaṇān diśaḥ ca gandharva saṃghān puruṣān striyaḥ ca parasparam prāpya mahān mahātmā viśeta yogī nacirāt vimuktaḥ yogān sa sarvān abhibhūya martyān yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca samyak tvayā ayam nṛpate varṇitaḥ śiṣṭa saṃmataḥ yoga mārgaḥ yathānyāyam śiṣyāya iha hita eṣiṇā sāṃkhye tu idānīm kārtsnyena vidhim prabrūhi pṛcchate triṣu lokeṣu yat jñānam sarvam tat viditam hi te bhīṣmaḥ uvāca śṛṇu me tvam idam śuddham sāṃkhyānām vidita ātmanām guṇāḥ ca yasmin bahavaḥ doṣa hāniḥ ca kevalā jñānena parisaṃkhyāya sa doṣān viṣayān nṛpa mānuṣān durjayān kṛtsnān paiśācān viṣayān tathā rākṣasān viṣayān jñātvā yakṣāṇām viṣayān tathā viṣayān auragān jñātvā gāndharva viṣayān tathā pitṝṇām viṣayān jñātvā tiryakṣu caratām nṛpa suparṇa viṣayān jñātvā marutām viṣayān tathā rājarṣi viṣayān jñātvā brahmarṣi viṣayān tathā āsurān viṣayān jñātvā vaiśvadevān tathā eva ca devarṣi viṣayān jñātvā yogānām api ca īśvarān viṣayān ca prajā īśānām brahmaṇaḥ viṣayān tathā āyuṣaḥ ca param kālam loke vijñāya tattvataḥ sukhasya ca param tattvam vijñāya vadatām vara prāpte kāle ca yat duḥkham patatām viṣaya eṣiṇām tiryak ca patatām duḥkham patatām narake ca yat svargasya ca guṇān kṛtsnān doṣān sarvān ca bhārata veda vāde ca ye doṣāḥ guṇāḥ ye ca api vaidikāḥ jñāna yoge ca ye doṣāḥ guṇāḥ yoge ca ye nṛpa sāṃkhya jñāne ca ye doṣāḥ tathā eva ca guṇāḥ nṛpa sattvam daśaguṇam jñātvā rajaḥ navaguṇam tathā tamaḥ ca aṣṭaguṇam jñātvā buddhim saptaguṇām tathā ṣaḍguṇam ca nabhaḥ jñātvā manaḥ pañcaguṇam tathā buddhim caturguṇām jñātvā tamaḥ ca triguṇam mahat dviguṇam ca rajaḥ jñātvā sattvam ekaguṇam punar mārgam vijñāya tattvena pralaye prekṣaṇam tathā jñāna vijñāna saṃpannāḥ kāraṇaiḥ bhāvitāḥ śubhaiḥ prāpnuvanti śubham mokṣam sūkṣmāḥ iha nabhaḥ param rūpeṇa dṛṣṭim saṃyuktām ghrāṇam gandha guṇena ca śabde saktam tathā śrotram jihvām rasa guṇeṣu ca tanum sparśe tathā saktām vāyum nabhasi ca āśritam viṣṇum krānte bale śakram koṣṭhe saktam tathā analam apsu devīm tathā saktām apaḥ tejasi ca āśritāḥ tejaḥ vāyau tu saṃsaktam vāyum nabhasi ca āśritam buddhim tamasi saṃsaktām tamaḥ rajasi ca āśritam saktam ātmānam īśe ca deve nārāyaṇe tathā devam mokṣe ca saṃsaktam mokṣam saktam tu na kva cit jñātvā sattva yutam deham vṛtam ṣoḍaśabhiḥ guṇaiḥ svabhāvam cetanām ca eva jñātvā vai deham āśrite dvitīyam karma vijñāya nṛpate viṣaya eṣiṇām indriyāṇi indriya arthān ca sarvān ātmani saṃśritān prāṇa apānau samānam ca vyāna udānau ca tattvataḥ avāk ca eva anilam jñātvā pravaham ca anilam punar sapta vātān tathā śeṣān saptadhā vidhivat punar prajāpatīn ṛṣīn ca eva mārgān ca su bahūn varān saptarṣīn ca bahūn jñātvā rājarṣīn ca paraṃtapa sura ṛṣīn mahataḥ ca anyān mahā ṛṣīn sūrya saṃnibhān aiśvaryāt cyāvitān jñātvā kālena mahatā nṛpa mahatām bhūta saṃghānām śrutvā nāśam ca pārthiva gatim ca api aśubhām jñātvā nṛpate pāpa karmaṇām vaitaraṇyām ca yat duḥkham patitānām yama kṣaye ca vicitrāsu saṃsārān aśubhān tathā jaṭhare ca aśubhe vāsam śoṇita udaka bhājane śleṣma mūtra purīṣe ca tīvra gandha samanvite śukra śoṇita saṃghāte majjā snāyu parigrahe sirā śata samākīrṇe nava dvāre pure aśucau vijñāya āhitam ātmānam yogān ca vividhān nṛpa tāmasānām ca jantūnām ramaṇīya āvṛta ātmanām sāttvikānām ca jantūnām kutsitam bharata ṛṣabha garhitam mahatām arthe sāṃkhyānām vidita ātmanām upaplavān tathā ghorān śaśinaḥ tejasaḥ tathā tārāṇām patanam dṛṣṭvā nakṣatrāṇām ca paryayam dvaṃdvānām viprayogam ca vijñāya kṛpaṇam nṛpa anyonya bhakṣaṇam dṛṣṭvā bhūtānām api ca aśubham bālye moham ca vijñāya kṣayam dehasya ca aśubham sahasreṣu naraḥ kaḥ cit mokṣa buddhim samāśritaḥ viṣayāṇām ca daurātmyam vijñāya nṛpate punar gatāsūnām ca kaunteya dehān dṛṣṭvā tathā aśubhān vāsam kuleṣu jantūnām duḥkham vijñāya bhārata brahma ghnānām gatim jñātvā patitānām su dāruṇām surā pāne ca saktānām brāhmaṇānām durātmanām guru dāra prasaktānām gatim vijñāya ca aśubhām tena jñānena vijñāya gatim ca aśubha karmaṇām tiryagyoni gatānām ca vijñāya gatayaḥ pṛthak veda vādān tathā citrān ṛtūnām paryayān tathā kṣayam saṃvatsarāṇām ca māsānām prakṣayam tathā pakṣa kṣayam tathā dṛṣṭvā divasānām ca saṃkṣayam kṣayam vṛddhim ca candrasya dṛṣṭvā pratyakṣataḥ tathā vṛddhim dṛṣṭvā samudrāṇām kṣayam teṣām tathā punar kṣayam dhanānām ca tathā punar vṛddhim tathā eva ca saṃyogānām kṣayam dṛṣṭvā yugānām ca viśeṣataḥ kṣayam ca dṛṣṭvā śailānām kṣayam ca saritām tathā varṇānām ca kṣayam dṛṣṭvā kṣaya antam ca punar punar jarā mṛtyum tathā janma dṛṣṭvā duḥkhāni ca eva ha deha doṣān tathā jñātvā teṣām duḥkham ca tattvataḥ ātma doṣān ca vijñāya sarvān ātmani saṃśritān sva dehāt utthitān gandhān tathā vijñāya ca aśubhān yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca bhīṣmaḥ uvāca pañca doṣān prabho dehe pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ mārga jñāḥ kāpilāḥ sāṃkhyāḥ śṛṇu tān ari sūdana kāma krodhau bhayam nidrā pañcamaḥ śvāsaḥ ucyate ete doṣāḥ śarīreṣu dṛśyante sarva dehinām chindanti kṣamayā krodham kāmam saṃkalpa varjanāt sattva saṃśīlanāt nidrām apramādāt bhayam tathā chindanti pañcamam śvāsam laghu āhāra tayā nṛpa guṇān guṇa śataiḥ jñātvā doṣān doṣa śataiḥ api hetūn hetu śataiḥ citraiḥ citrān vijñāya tattvataḥ apām phena upamam lokam viṣṇoḥ māyā śataiḥ vṛtam tamaḥ śvabhra nibham dṛṣṭvā varṣa budbuda saṃnibham nāśa prāyam sukhāt hīnam nāśa uttaram abhāva gam sāṃkhyāḥ rājan mahā prājñāḥ tyaktvā deham prajā kṛtam jñāna jñeyena sāṃkhyena vyāpinā mahatā nṛpa rājasān aśubhān gandhān tāmasān ca tathāvidhān puṇyān ca sāttvikān gandhān sparśa jān deha saṃśritān chittvā āśu jñāna śastreṇa tapaḥ daṇḍena bhārata tatas duḥkha udakam ghoram cintā śoka mahā hradam vyādhi mṛtyu mahā grāham mahā bhaya mahā uragam tamaḥ kūrmam rajaḥ mīnam prajñayā saṃtaranti uta sneha paṅkam jarā durgam sparśa dvīpam ariṃdama karma agādham satya tīram sthita vratam idam nṛpa hiṃsā śīghra mahā vegam nānā rasa mahā ākaram nānā prīti mahā ratnam duḥkha jvara samīraṇam śoka tṛṣṇā mahā āvartam tīkṣṇa vyādhi mahā gajam asthi saṃghāta saṃghāṭam śleṣma phenam ariṃdama dāna muktā ākaram bhīmam śoṇita hrada vidrumam hasita utkruṣṭa nirghoṣam nānā jñāna su dustaram rodana aśru mala kṣāram saṅga tyāga parāyaṇam ahiṃsā satya maryādam prāṇatyāga mahā ūrmiṇam mokṣa duṣprāpa viṣayam vaḍavāmukha sāgaram tatas tān sukṛtīn sāṃkhyān sūryaḥ vahati raśmibhiḥ tatra tān pravahaḥ vāyuḥ pratigṛhṇāti bhārata vīta rāgān yatīn siddhān vīrya yuktān tapodhanān sūkṣmaḥ śītaḥ sugandhī ca sukha sparśaḥ ca bhārata saptānām marutām śreṣṭhaḥ lokān gacchati yaḥ śubhān sattvam vahati śuddha ātman param nārāyaṇam prabhum prabhuḥ vahati śuddha ātmā paramātmānam ātmanā paramātmānam āsādya tad bhūta āyatana amalāḥ paramā sā gatiḥ pārtha nirdvaṃdvānām mahātmanām yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca tvat ṛte mānavam na anyam praṣṭum arhāmi kaurava mokṣa doṣaḥ mahān eṣa prāpya siddhim gatān ṛṣīn pravṛtti lakṣaṇam dharmam paśyāmi paramam nṛpa bhīṣmaḥ uvāca yathānyāyam tvayā tāta praśnaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ su saṃkaṭaḥ atrā api tattvam paramam śṛṇu samyak mayā īritam buddhiḥ ca paramā yatra kāpilānām mahātmanām kāraṇāni ātmanaḥ tāni sūkṣmaḥ paśyati taiḥ tu saḥ ātmanā viprahīṇāni kāṣṭha kuḍya samāni tu vinaśyanti na saṃdehaḥ phenāḥ iva mahā arṇave sūkṣmaḥ carati sarvatra nabhasi iva samīraṇaḥ sa paśyati yathānyāyam sparśān spṛśati ca abhibho indriyāṇi iha sarvāṇi sve sve sthāne yathāvidhi anīśa tvāt pralīyante sarpāḥ hata viṣāḥ iva indriyāṇām tu sarveṣām sva sthāneṣu eva sarvaśas ākramya gatayaḥ sūkṣmāḥ carati ātmā na saṃśayaḥ sattvasya ca guṇān kṛtsnān rajasaḥ ca guṇān punar guṇān ca tamasaḥ sarvān guṇān buddheḥ ca bhārata guṇān ca manasaḥ tadvat nabhasaḥ ca guṇān tathā guṇān vāyoḥ ca dharma ātman tejasaḥ ca guṇān punar apām guṇān tathā pārtha pārthivān ca guṇān api sarva ātmanā guṇaiḥ vyāpya kṣetrajñaḥ sa yudhiṣṭhira ātmā ca yāti kṣetrajñam karmaṇī ca śubha aśubhe śiṣyāḥ iva mahātmānam indriyāṇi ca tam vibho param nārāyaṇa ātmānam nirdvaṃdvam prakṛteḥ param vimuktaḥ puṇya pāpebhyaḥ praviṣṭaḥ tam anāmayam śiṣṭam tu atra manaḥ tāta indriyāṇi ca bhārata āgacchanti yathākālam guroḥ saṃdeśa kāriṇaḥ śakyam ca alpena kālena śāntim prāptum guṇa arthinā evam yuktena kaunteya yukta jñānena mokṣiṇā sāṃkhyāḥ rājan mahā prājñāḥ gacchanti paramām gatim jñānena anena kaunteya tulyam jñānam na vidyate atra te saṃśayaḥ mā bhūt jñānam sāṃkhyam param matam an ādi madhya nidhanam nirdvaṃdvam kartṛ śāśvatam kūṭastham ca eva nityam ca yat vadanti śama ātmakāḥ yat ca śaṃsanti śāstreṣu vadanti parama ṛṣayaḥ sarve viprāḥ ca devāḥ ca tathā āgama vidaḥ janāḥ samyak yuktāḥ tathā yogāḥ sāṃkhyāḥ ca amita darśanāḥ amūrteḥ tasya kaunteya sāṃkhyam mūrtiḥ iti śrutiḥ abhijñānāni tasya āhuḥ matam hi bharata ṛṣabha dvividhāni iha bhūtāni pṛthivyām pṛthivīpate jaṅgama agama saṃjñāni jaṅgamam tu viśiṣyate yat ca api dṛṣṭam vividham purāṇam sāṃkhya āgatam tat nikhilam narendra yat ca itihāseṣu mahatsu dṛṣṭam yat ca artha śāstre nṛpa śiṣṭa juṣṭe jñānam ca loke yat iha asti kim cit sāṃkhya āgatam tat ca mahat mahātman śamaḥ ca dṛṣṭaḥ paramam balam ca tapāṃsi sūkṣmāṇi sukhāni ca eva sāṃkhye yathāvat vihitāni rājan tān ca anusaṃcārya tatas kṛtārthāḥ patanti vipreṣu yateṣu bhūyas hitvā ca deham praviśanti mokṣam divaukasaḥ dyām iva pārtha sāṃkhyāḥ tatas adhikam te abhiratāḥ mahārhe sāṃkhye dvijāḥ pārthiva śiṣṭa juṣṭe teṣām na tiryak gamanam hi dṛṣṭam na avāk gatiḥ pāpa kṛtām nivāsaḥ na ca abudhānām api te dvijātayaḥ ye jñānam etat nṛpate anuraktāḥ sāṃkyam viśālam paramam purāṇam mahā arṇavam vimalam udāra kāntam kṛtsnam ca sāṃkhyam nṛpate mahātmā nārāyaṇaḥ dhārayate aprameyam etat mayā uktam naradeva tattvam nārāyaṇaḥ viśvam idam purāṇam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca ṛṣibhiḥ ca mahābhāgaiḥ yatibhiḥ ca mahātmabhiḥ śeṣam alpam dinānām te dakṣiṇāyana bhāskare tvayi pratigate śreyaḥ kutas śroṣyāmahe vayam kuru vaṃśa pradīpaḥ tvam jñāna dravyeṇa dīpyase na tṛpyāmi iha rāja indra śṛṇvan amṛtam īdṛśam bhīṣmaḥ uvāca vasiṣṭhasya ca saṃvādam karālajanakasya ca vasiṣṭham śreṣṭham āsīnam ṛṣīṇām bhāskara dyutim papraccha janakaḥ rājā jñānam naiḥśreyasam param maitrāvaruṇim āsīnam abhivādya kṛtāñjaliḥ su akṣaram praśritam vākyam madhuram ca api anulbaṇam papraccha ṛṣi varam rājā karālajanakaḥ purā yasmāt na punarāvṛttim āpnuvanti manīṣiṇaḥ yat ca akṣaram iti proktam śivam kṣemyam anāmayam vasiṣṭhaḥ uvāca śrūyatām pṛthivīpāla kṣarati idam yathā jagat yat na kṣarati pūrveṇa yāvat kālena ca api atha yugam dvādaśa sāhasram kalpam viddhi caturguṇam daśa kalpa śata āvṛttam tat ahar brāhmam ucyate sṛjati ananta karmāṇam mahāntam bhūtam agrajam mūrtimantam amūrta ātmā viśvam śaṃbhuḥ svayaṃbhuvaḥ aṇimā laghimā prāptiḥ īśānam jyotiḥ avyayam sarvatas pāṇi pāda antam sarvatas akṣi śiraḥ mukham sarvatas śrutimat loke sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati sāṃkhye ca paṭhyate śāstre nāmabhiḥ bahudhā ātmakaḥ vicitra rūpaḥ viśvātmā eka akṣaraḥ iti smṛtaḥ vṛtam na eka ātmakam yena kṛtsnam trailokyam ātmanā tathā eva bahu rūpa tvāt viśvarūpaḥ iti smṛtaḥ eṣa vai vikriyā āpannaḥ sṛjati ātmānam ātmanā ahaṃkāram mahā tejāḥ prajāpatim ahaṃkṛtam mahāntam ca api ahaṃkāram avidyā sargam eva ca vidyā avidyā iti vikhyāte śruti śāstra artha cintakaiḥ bhūta sargam ahaṃkārāt tṛtīyam viddhi pārthiva ahaṃkāreṣu bhūteṣu caturtham viddhi vaikṛtam vāyuḥ jyotiḥ atha ākāśam āpaḥ atha pṛthivī tathā śrotram tvac cakṣuṣī jihvā ghrāṇam eva ca pañcamam buddhīndriyāṇi ca etāni tathā karmendriyāṇi ca saṃbhūtāni iha yugapad manasā saha pārthiva eṣā tattva caturviṃśā sarva ākṛtiṣu vartate yām jñātvā na abhiśocanti brāhmaṇāḥ tattva darśinaḥ sa cāraṇa piśāce vai sa deva ṛṣi niśācare sa daṃśa kīṭa maśake sa pūti kṛmi mūṣake śuni śvapāke vaiṇeye sa caṇḍāle sa pulkase hasti aśva khara śārdūle sa vṛkṣe gavi ca eva ha jale bhuvi tathā ākāśe na anyatra iti viniścayaḥ ahani ahani bhūtātmā tatas kṣaraḥ iti smṛtaḥ etat akṣaram iti uktam kṣarati idam yathā jagat kathitam te mahā rāja yasmāt na āvartate punar pañcaviṃśatimaḥ viṣṇuḥ nistattvaḥ tattva saṃjñakaḥ tattva saṃśrayaṇāt etat tattvam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ caturviṃśatimaḥ vyaktaḥ hi amūrtaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ saḥ eva hṛdi sarvāsu mūrtiṣu ātiṣṭhate ātmavān cetayan cetanaḥ nityaḥ sarva mūrtiḥ a mūrtimān gocare vartate nityam nirguṇaḥ guṇa saṃjñakaḥ tamasā tāmasān bhāvān vividhān pratipadyate rajasā rājasān ca eva sāttvikān sattva saṃśrayāt śukla lohita kṛṣṇāni rūpāṇi etāni trīṇi tu sarvāṇi etāni rūpāṇi jānīhi prākṛtāni vai tāmasāḥ nirayam yānti rājasāḥ mānuṣān tathā puṇya pāpena mānuṣyam puṇyena ekena devatāḥ evam avyakta viṣayam kṣaram āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ pañcaviṃśatimaḥ yaḥ ayam jñānāt eva pravartate vasiṣṭhaḥ uvāca upapadyati saṃyogāt guṇaiḥ saha guṇa kṣayāt mānuṣa tvāt divam yāti divaḥ mānuṣyam eva ca kośakāraḥ yathā ātmānam kīṭaḥ samanurundhati sūtra tantu guṇaiḥ nityam tathā ayam aguṇaḥ guṇaiḥ śīrṣa roge akṣi roge ca danta śūle galagrahe jalodare arśasām roge jvara gaṇḍa viṣūcike śvitre kuṣṭhe agnidāhe ca sidhma apasmārayoḥ api yāni ca anyāni dvaṃdvāni prākṛtāni śarīriṣu eka vāsāḥ ca durvāsāḥ śāyī nityam adhas tathā maṇḍūkaśāyī ca tathā vīrāsana gataḥ tathā cīra dhāraṇam ākāśe śayanam sthānam eva ca iṣṭakā prastare ca eva kaṇṭaka prastare tathā bhasma prastara śāyī ca bhūmi śayyā anulepanaḥ vīrasthāna ambu paṅke ca śayanam phalakeṣu ca muñja mekhala nagna tvam kṣauma kṛṣṇa ajināni ca śāṇī vāla parīdhānaḥ vyāghra carma paricchadaḥ siṃha carma parīdhānaḥ paṭṭa vāsāḥ tathā eva ca ca eva cīra vāsāḥ tathā eva ca caturtha aṣṭama kālaḥ ca ṣaṣṭhakālikaḥ eva ca ṣaṣ rātra bhojanaḥ ca eva tathā eva aṣṭa aha bhojanaḥ sapta rātra daśa āhāraḥ dvādaśa āhāraḥ eva ca māsa upavāsī mūla āśī phala āhāraḥ tathā eva ca go mūtra bhojanaḥ ca eva śāka puṣpa ādaḥ eva ca vartayan śīrṇa parṇaiḥ ca prakīrṇa phala bhojanaḥ vividhāni ca kṛcchrāṇi sevate sukha kāṅkṣayā cāndrāyaṇāni vidhivat liṅgāni vividhāni ca cāturāśramya panthānam āśrayati āśramān api upāsīnaḥ ca pāṣaṇḍān guhāḥ śailān tathā eva ca viviktāḥ ca śilā chāyāḥ tathā prasravaṇāni ca niyamān su vicitrān ca vividhāni tapāṃsi ca yajñān ca vividha ākārān vidhīn ca vividhān tathā vaṇikpatham dvijakṣatram vaiśya śūdram tathā eva ca dānam ca vividha ākāram dīna andha kṛpaṇeṣu api prakṛtyā ātmānam eva ātmā evam pravibhajati uta svadhākāra vaṣaṭkārau svāhākāra namaskriyāḥ yājana adhyāpanam dānam tathā eva āhuḥ pratigraham śubha aśubha mayam sarvam etat āhuḥ kriyā patham divasa ante guṇān etān abhyetya ekaḥ avatiṣṭhati evam eṣaḥ asakṛt sarvam krīḍā artham abhimanyate ātma rūpa guṇān etān vividhān hṛdaya priyān nistartavyāni atha etāni sarvāṇi iti narādhipa yāvadantam ca me saukhyam jātyām jātyām bhaviṣyati mahat duḥkham hi mānuṣyam niraye ca api majjanam nirayāt ca api mānuṣyam kālena eṣyāmi aham punar manuṣya tvāt ca deva tvam deva tvāt pauruṣam punar yaḥ evam vetti vai nityam nirātmā ātma guṇaiḥ vṛtaḥ sarga koṭi sahasrāṇi maraṇa antāsu mūrtiṣu saḥ eva phalam aśnāti triṣu lokeṣu mūrtimān prakṛtiḥ kurute karma śubha aśubha phala ātmakam prakṛtiḥ ca tat aśnāti triṣu lokeṣu kāmagā trīṇi sthānāni ca etāni jānīyāt prākṛtāni ha aliṅgām prakṛtim tu āhuḥ liṅgaiḥ anumimīmahe tathā eva pauruṣam liṅgam anumānāt hi paśyati sa liṅga antaram āsādya prākṛtam liṅgam avraṇam vraṇa dvārāṇi adhiṣṭhāya karmāṇi ātmani manyate śrotra ādīni tu sarvāṇi pañca karmendriyāṇi ca vāc ādīni pravartante guṇeṣu eva guṇaiḥ saha aliṅgaḥ liṅgam ātmānam akālaḥ kālam ātmanaḥ a mṛtyuḥ mṛtyum ātmānam a caraḥ caram ātmanaḥ akṣetraḥ kṣetram ātmānam asargaḥ sargam ātmanaḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ uvāca dhāmnā dhāma sahasrāṇi maraṇa antāni gacchati candramāḥ iva kośānām punar tatra sahasraśas kalāḥ pañcadaśā yoniḥ tat dhāma iti paṭhyate nityam etat vijānīhi somaḥ ṣoḍaśamī kalā kalāyām jāyate ajasram punar punar abuddhimān ṣoḍaśī tu kalā sūkṣmā sa somaḥ upadhāryatām evam tām kṣapayitvā hi jāyate nṛpa sattama sā hi asya prakṛtiḥ dṛṣṭā tad kṣayāt mokṣaḥ ucyate tat evam ṣoḍaśa kalam deham avyakta saṃjñakam pañcaviṃśaḥ tathā eva ātmā tasya eva pratibodhanāt vimalasya viśuddhasya śuddha anila niṣevaṇāt aśuddhaḥ eva śuddha ātmā tādṛś bhavati pārthiva prakṛteḥ triguṇāyāḥ tu sevanāt prākṛtaḥ bhavet akṣara kṣarayoḥ eṣa dvayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ iṣyate ṛte na puruṣeṇa iha strī garbham dhārayati uta ṛte striyam na puruṣaḥ rūpam nirvartayet tathā anyonyasya abhisaṃbandhāt anyonya guṇa saṃśrayāt ṛtau nirvartate rūpam tat vakṣyāmi nidarśanam ye guṇāḥ puruṣasya iha ye ca mātṛ guṇāḥ tathā asthi snāyu ca majjā ca jānīmaḥ pitṛtaḥ dvija tvac māṃsam śoṇitam ca eva mātṛ jāni api śuśruma evam etat dvijaśreṣṭha veda śāstreṣu paṭhyate pramāṇam yat ca veda uktam śāstra uktam yat ca paṭhyate veda śāstra pramāṇam ca pramāṇam tat sanātanam evam eva abhisaṃbaddhau nityam prakṛti pūruṣau mokṣa kāmāḥ vayam ca api kāṅkṣāmaḥ yat anāmayam vasiṣṭhaḥ uvāca evam etat yathā ca etat na gṛhṇāti tathā bhavān na ca grantha artha tattva jñaḥ tasya tat dhāraṇam vṛthā granthasya artham ca pṛṣṭaḥ san tādṛśaḥ vaktum arhati sa katham manda vijñānaḥ grantham vakṣyati nirṇayāt nirṇayam ca api chidra ātmā na tam vakṣyati tattvataḥ sa upahāsa ātma tām eti yasmāt ca eva ātmavān api tasmāt tvam śṛṇu rāja indra yathā etat anudṛśyate yāthātathyena sāṃkhyeṣu yogeṣu ca mahātmasu ekam sāṃkhyam ca yogam ca yaḥ paśyati sa buddhimān tvac māṃsam rudhiram medaḥ pittam majja asthi snāyu ca dehāt deham avāpnoti bījāt bījam tathā eva ca katham guṇāḥ bhaviṣyanti nirguṇa tvāt mahātmanaḥ guṇāḥ guṇeṣu jāyante tatra eva niviśanti ca evam guṇāḥ prakṛtitaḥ jāyante ca na santi ca tvac māṃsam rudhiram medaḥ pittam majja asthi snāyu ca aṣṭau tāni atha śukreṇa jānīhi prākṛtāni vai pumān ca eva a pumān ca eva trailiṅgyam prākṛtam smṛtam na eva pumān pumān ca eva sa liṅgī iti abhidhīyate pañcaviṃśatimaḥ tāta liṅgeṣu aniyata ātmakaḥ kevalam tu abhimāni tvāt guṇeṣu aguṇaḥ ucyate guṇāḥ guṇavataḥ santi nirguṇasya kutas guṇāḥ tasmāt evam vijānanti ye janāḥ guṇa darśinaḥ yadā tu eṣa guṇān sarvān prākṛtān abhimanyate tadā sa guṇavān eva parameṇa anupaśyati yat tat buddheḥ param prāhuḥ sāṃkhyāḥ yogāḥ ca sarvaśas aprabuddham atha avyaktam sa guṇam prāhuḥ īśvaram nirguṇam ca īśvaram nityam adhiṣṭhātāram eva ca prakṛteḥ ca guṇānām ca pañcaviṃśatikam budhāḥ sāṃkhya yoge ca kuśalāḥ budhyante parama eṣiṇaḥ budhyamāna aprabuddhābhyām pṛthak pṛthak ariṃdama paraspareṇa etat uktam kṣara akṣara nidarśanam ekatvam akṣaram prāhuḥ nānātvam kṣaram ucyate pañcaviṃśati niṣṭhaḥ ayam yadā samyak pravartate ekatvam darśanam ca asya nānātvam ca api adarśanam pañcaviṃśati sargam tu tattvam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ sthūla buddhyā na paśyāmi tattvam etat na saṃśayaḥ akṣara kṣarayoḥ uktam tvayā yat api kāraṇam sāṃkhyam yogam ca kārtsnyena pṛthak ca eva apṛthak ca ha vasiṣṭhaḥ uvāca yoga kṛtyam mahā rāja pṛthak eva śṛṇuṣva me yoga kṛtyam tu yogānām dhyānam eva param balam tat ca api dvividham dhyānam āhuḥ veda vidaḥ janāḥ ekāgra tā ca manasaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ tathā eva ca prāṇāyāmaḥ tu sa guṇaḥ nirguṇaḥ manasaḥ tathā tri kālam na abhiyuñjīta śeṣam yuñjīta tatparaḥ daśa dvādaśabhiḥ vā api caturviṃśāt param tatas tam codanābhiḥ matimān ātmānam codayet atha tiṣṭhantam ajaram tam tu yat tat uktam manīṣibhiḥ taiḥ ca ātmā satatam jñeyaḥ iti evam anuśuśruma manaḥ buddhyā sthiram kṛtvā pāṣāṇaḥ iva niścalaḥ sthāṇu vat ca api akampaḥ syāt giri vat ca api niścalaḥ budhāḥ vidhi vidhāna jñāḥ tadā yuktam pracakṣate na śṛṇoti na ca āghrāti na rasyati na paśyati na ca sparśam vijānāti na saṃkalpayate manaḥ tadā prakṛtim āpannam yuktam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ nivāte ca yathā dīpyan dīpaḥ tadvat sa dṛśyate niriṅgaḥ ca acalaḥ ca ūrdhvam na tiryaggatim āpnuyāt vaidyutaḥ agniḥ iva ākāśe dṛśyate ātmā tathā ātmani yam paśyanti mahātmānaḥ dhṛtimantaḥ manīṣiṇaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ hi ayonim amṛta ātmakam tat antar sarva bhūteṣu dhruvam tiṣṭhat na dṛśyate mahataḥ tamasaḥ tāta pāre tiṣṭhan atāmasaḥ evam ātmānam ajaram param sāṃkhya jñānam pravakṣyāmi parisaṃkhyā nidarśanam avyaktam āhuḥ prakṛtim parām prakṛti vādinaḥ ahaṃkāraḥ tu mahataḥ tṛtīyam iti naḥ śrutam pañca bhūtāni ahaṃkārāt āhuḥ sāṃkhya anudarśinaḥ etāḥ prakṛtayaḥ tu aṣṭau vikārāḥ ca api ṣoḍaśa pañca ca eva viśeṣāḥ vai tathā pañca indriyāṇi ca etāvat eva tattvānām sāṃkhyam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ sāṃkhye vidhi vidhāna jñāḥ nityam sāṃkhya pathe ratāḥ līyante pratilomāni sṛjyante ca antarātmanā guṇāḥ guṇeṣu satatam sāgarasya ūrmayaḥ yathā bahudhā ātmā prakurvīta prakṛtim prasava ātmikām tat ca kṣetram mahān ātmā pañcaviṃśaḥ adhitiṣṭhati adhiṣṭhānāt adhiṣṭhātā kṣetrāṇām iti naḥ śrutam kṣetram jānāti ca avyaktam kṣetrajñaḥ iti ca ucyate kṣetram avyaktam iti uktam jñātā vai pañcaviṃśakaḥ anyat eva ca jñānam syāt anyat jñeyam tat ucyate jñānam avyaktam iti uktam jñeyaḥ vai pañcaviṃśakaḥ anīśvaram atattvam ca tattvam tat pañcaviṃśakam sāṃkhya darśanam etāvat parisaṃkhyāna darśanam sāṃkhyāḥ saha prakṛtyā tu nistattvaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ pañcaviṃśaḥ aprabuddha ātmā budhyamānaḥ iti smṛtaḥ evam etat vijānantaḥ sāmyatām pratiyānti uta samyak nidarśanam nāma pratyakṣam prakṛteḥ tathā na tu evam vartamānānām āvṛttiḥ vidyate punar vasiṣṭhaḥ uvāca sāṃkhya darśanam etāvat uktam te nṛpa sattama vidyā avidye tu idānīm me tvam nibodha anupūrvaśas parasparam avidyām vai tat nibodha anupūrvaśas yathā uktam ṛṣibhiḥ tāta sāṃkhyasya asya nidarśanam karmendriyāṇām sarveṣām vidyā buddhīndriyam smṛtam buddhīndriyāṇām ca tathā viśeṣāḥ iti naḥ śrutam viśeṣāṇām manaḥ teṣām vidyām āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ manasaḥ pañcabhūtāni vidyāḥ iti abhicakṣate ahaṃkāraḥ tu bhūtānām pañcānām na atra saṃśayaḥ buddheḥ prakṛtiḥ avyaktam tattvānām parama īśvaram vidyā jñeyā nara śreṣṭha vidhiḥ ca paramaḥ smṛtaḥ avyaktasya param prāhuḥ vidyām vai pañcaviṃśakam jñānam avyaktam iti uktam jñeyam vai pañcaviṃśakam tathā eva jñānam avyaktam vijñātā pañcaviṃśakaḥ ubhau etau kṣarau uktau ubhau etau ca nakṣarau kāraṇam tu pravakṣyāmi yathā khyātau tu tattvataḥ tattva saṃjñau ubhau etau procyete jñāna cintakaiḥ tat etat guṇa sargāya vikurvāṇam punar punar guṇānām mahat ādīnām utpadyati parasparam adhiṣṭhānāt kṣetram āhuḥ etat tat pañcaviṃśakam yadā tu guṇa jālam tat avyakta ātmani saṃkṣipet tadā saha guṇaiḥ taiḥ tu pañcaviṃśaḥ vilīyate guṇāḥ guṇeṣu līyante tadā ekā prakṛtiḥ bhavet kṣetrajñaḥ api yadā tāta tad kṣetre saṃpralīyate tadā akṣara tvam prakṛtiḥ gacchate guṇa saṃjñitā evam eva ca kṣetrajñaḥ kṣetra jñāna parikṣaye prakṛtyāḥ nirguṇaḥ tu eṣaḥ iti evam anuśuśruma kṣaraḥ bhavati eṣa yadā tadā guṇavatīm atha prakṛtim tu abhijānāti nirguṇa tvam tathā ātmanaḥ prakṛtyā ca eva rāja indra namiśraḥ anyaḥ ca dṛśyate yadā tu guṇa jālam tat prākṛtam vijugupsate paśyate ca aparam paśyam tadā paśyan na saṃjvaret kim mayā kṛtam etāvat yaḥ aham kālam imam janam matsyaḥ jālam hi avijñānāt anuvartitavān tathā matsyaḥ anya tvam yathā ajñānāt udakāt na abhimanyate ātmānam tadvat ajñānāt anya tvam ca eva vedmi aham sāmyam eka tvam āyātaḥ yādṛśaḥ tādṛśaḥ tu aham yaḥ aham ajñāna saṃmohāt ajñayā saṃpravṛttavān sa saṅgayā aham niḥsaṅgaḥ sthitaḥ kālam imam tu aham anayā aham vaśībhūtaḥ kālam etam na buddhavān ucca madhyama nīcānām tām aham katham āvase gacchāmi a buddha bhāva tvāt eṣā idānīm sthiraḥ bhave sahavāsam na yāsyāmi kālam etat hi vañcanāt tatas asmi bahu rūpāsu sthitaḥ mūrtiṣu a mūrtimān amūrtaḥ ca api mūrta ātmā mamatvena pradharṣitaḥ yonīṣu vartamānena naṣṭa saṃjñena cetasā na mama atrā anayā kāryam ahaṃkāra kṛtātmayā ātmānam bahudhā kṛtvā yā iyam bhūyas yunakti mām idānīm eṣa buddhaḥ asmi nirmamaḥ nirahaṃkṛtaḥ apetya aham imām hitvā saṃśrayiṣye nirāmayam anena sāmyam yāsyāmi na anayā aham acetasā evam parama saṃbodhāt pañcaviṃśaḥ anubuddhavān avyaktam vyakta dharmāṇam sa guṇam nirguṇam tathā nirguṇam prathamam
