dṛṣṭvā tādṛś bhavati maithila mayā iha jñāna saṃpannam yathāśruti nidarśanāt niḥsaṃdigdham ca sūkṣmam ca vibuddham vimalam tathā sāṃkhya yogau mayā proktau śāstra dvaya nidarśanāt yat eva śāstram sāṃkhya uktam yoga darśanam eva tat prabodhana karam jñānam sāṃkhyānām avanīpate vispaṣṭam procyate tatra śiṣyāṇām hita kāmyayā bṛhat ca eva hi tat śāstram iti āhuḥ kuśalāḥ janāḥ asmin ca śāstre yogānām punar dadhi punar śaraḥ pañcaviṃśāt param tattvam na paśyati narādhipa sāṃkhyānām tu param tatra yathāvat anuvarṇitam vasiṣṭhaḥ uvāca aprabuddham atha avyaktam imam guṇa vidhim śṛṇu guṇān dhārayate hi eṣā sṛjati ākṣipate tathā ajasram tu iha krīḍā artham vikurvantī narādhipa ātmānam bahudhā kṛtvā tāni eva ca vicakṣate etat evam vikurvāṇām budhyamānaḥ na budhyate budhyamānaḥ bhavati eṣa saṅga ātmakaḥ iti śrutiḥ pañcaviṃśam mahātmānam na ca asau api budhyate ṣaḍviṃśam vimalam buddham aprameyam sanātanam satatam pañcaviṃśam ca caturviṃśam ca budhyate dṛśya adṛśye hi anugatam ubhau eva mahā dyutī kevalam pañcaviṃśam ca caturviṃśam na paśyati budhyate ca parām buddhim viśuddhām amalām yadā ṣaḍviṃśaḥ rāja śārdūla tadā buddha tvam āvrajet nirguṇaḥ prakṛtim veda guṇa yuktām acetanām pañcaviṃśati tattvāni pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ eṣa muñcati tattvam hi kṣipram buddhasya lakṣaṇam ṣaḍviṃśaḥ aham iti prājñaḥ gṛhyamāṇaḥ ajara amaraḥ etat nānātvam iti uktam sāṃkhya śruti nidarśanāt saṅga dharmā bhavati eṣa niḥsaṅga ātmā narādhipa niḥsaṅga ātmānam āsādya ṣaḍviṃśakam ajam viduḥ caturviṃśam agādham ca ṣaḍviṃśasya prabodhanāt nānātva ekatvam etāvat draṣṭavyam śāstra dṛṣṭibhiḥ pañcaviṃśatikasya asya yaḥ ayam deheṣu vartate vimokṣiṇā vimokṣaḥ ca sametya iha tathā bhavet śuci karmā śuciḥ ca eva bhavati amita dīptimān na paṇḍita jñāna para upatāpine deyam tvayā idam vinibodha yādṛśe śraddhā anvitāya atha guṇa anvitāya para apavādāt viratāya nityam vivikta śīlāya vidhi priyāya vivāda hīnāya bahu śrutāya na śreyasā yokṣyati tādṛśe kṛtam dharma pravaktāram apātra dānāt pṛthvīm imām yadi api ratna pūrṇām dadyāt nadeyam tu idam avratāya agādha janma amaraṇam ca rājan nirāmayam vīta bhayam śivam ca samīkṣya moham tyaja ca adya sarvam jñānasya tattva artham idam viditvā tathā avāptam brahmaṇaḥ me narendra mahat jñānam mokṣa vidām purāṇam bhīṣmaḥ uvāca pañcaviṃśaḥ mahā rāja parama ṛṣi nidarśanāt punarāvṛttim āpnoti param jñānam avāpya ca etat niḥśreyasa karam jñānānām te param mayā kathitam tattvataḥ tāta śrutvā deva ṛṣitaḥ nṛpa hiraṇyagarbhāt ṛṣiṇā vasiṣṭhena mahātmanā vasiṣṭhāt ṛṣi śārdūlāt nāradaḥ avāptavān idam avijñānāt ca mūḍha ātmā punar punar upadravan pretya jāti sahasrāṇi maraṇa antāni upāśnute deva lokam tathā tiryak mānuṣyam api ca aśnute yadi śudhyati kālena tasmāt ajñāna sāgarāt yasmāt agādhāt avyaktāt uttīrṇaḥ tvam sanātanāt bhīṣmaḥ uvāca mṛgayām vicaran kaḥ cit vijane janaka ātmajaḥ vane dadarśa vipra indram ṛṣim vaṃśa dharam bhṛgoḥ tam āsīnam upāsīnaḥ praṇamya śirasā munim satkṛtya paripṛṣṭaḥ san su mahātmā mahā tapāḥ dharmaḥ satām hitaḥ puṃsām dharmaḥ ca eva āśrayaḥ satām dharmāt lokāḥ trayaḥ tāta pravṛttāḥ sa carācarāḥ svādu kāmuka kāmānām vaitṛṣṇyam kim na gacchasi nivṛttau vā pravṛttau vā saṃpradhārya guṇa aguṇān nityam ca bahu dātavyam sādhubhyaḥ ca anasūyatā prārthitam vrata śaucābhyām satkṛtam deśa kālayoḥ anṛśaṃsaḥ śuciḥ dāntaḥ satya vāc ārjave sthitaḥ satkṛtā ca ekapatnī ca jātyā yoniḥ iha iṣyate ṛk yajuḥ sāma gaḥ vidvān ṣaṭkarmā pātram ucyate pātra karma viśeṣeṇa deśa kālau avekṣya ca līlayā alpam yathā gātrāt pramṛjyāt rajasaḥ pumān mānasam sarva bhūteṣu vartate vai śubha aśubhe aśubhebhyaḥ samākṣipya śubheṣu eva avatārayet sarvam sarveṇa sarvatra kriyamāṇam ca pūjaya apraśānta praśāmya tvam aprājña prājña vat cara tejasā śakyate prāptum upāya sahacāriṇā iha ca pretya ca śreyaḥ tasya mūlam dhṛtiḥ parā rājarṣiḥ adhṛtiḥ svargāt patitaḥ hi mahābhiṣaḥ yayātiḥ kṣīṇa puṇyaḥ ca dhṛtyā lokān avāptavān tapasvinām dharmavatām viduṣām ca upasevanāt yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca janma mṛtyu vimuktam ca vimuktam puṇya pāpayoḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca yājñavalkyasya saṃvādam janakasya ca bhārata yājñavalkyam ṛṣi śreṣṭham daivarātiḥ mahā yaśāḥ papraccha janakaḥ rājā praśnam praśna vidām varaḥ kati indriyāṇi viprarṣe kati prakṛtayaḥ smṛtāḥ prabhavam ca apyayam ca eva kāla saṃkhyām tathā eva ca ajñānāt paripṛcchāmi tvam hi jñāna mayaḥ nidhiḥ yājñavalkyaḥ uvāca śrūyatām avanīpāla yat etat anupṛcchasi yogānām paramam jñānam sāṃkhyānām ca viśeṣataḥ na tava aviditam kim cit mām tu jijñāsate bhavān pṛṣṭena ca api vaktavyam eṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ aṣṭau prakṛtayaḥ proktāḥ vikārāḥ ca api ṣoḍaśa avyaktam ca mahān ca eva tathā ahaṃkāraḥ eva ca pṛthivī vāyuḥ ākāśam āpaḥ jyotiḥ ca pañcamam etāḥ prakṛtayaḥ tu aṣṭau vikārān api me śṛṇu śrotram tvac ca eva cakṣuḥ ca jihvā ghrāṇam ca pañcamam ete viśeṣāḥ rāja indra mahābhūteṣu pañcasu buddhīndriyāṇi atha etāni sa viśeṣāṇi maithila manaḥ ṣoḍaśakam prāhuḥ adhyātma gati cintakāḥ tvam ca eva anye ca vidvāṃsaḥ tattva buddhi viśāradāḥ prathamam sargam iti etat āhuḥ prādhānikam budhāḥ ahaṃkārāt ca saṃbhūtam manaḥ bhūta guṇa ātmakam tṛtīyaḥ sargaḥ iti eṣaḥ āhaṃkārikaḥ ucyate manasaḥ tu samudbhūtāḥ mahā bhūtāḥ narādhipa pañcamam sargam iti āhuḥ bhautikam bhūta cintakāḥ śrotram tvac ca eva cakṣuḥ ca jihvā ghrāṇam ca pañcamam sargam tu ṣaṣṭham iti āhuḥ bahu cintā ātmakam smṛtam aṣṭamam sargam iti āhuḥ etat ārjavakam budhāḥ navamam sargam iti āhuḥ etat ārjavakam budhāḥ caturviṃśatiḥ uktāni yathāśruti nidarśanāt atas ūrdhvam mahā rāja guṇasya etasya tattvataḥ mahātmabhiḥ anuproktām kāla saṃkhyām nibodha me yājñavalkyaḥ uvāca avyaktasya nara śreṣṭha kāla saṃkhyām nibodha me sṛjati oṣadhim eva agre jīvanam sarva dehinām tatas brahmāṇam asṛjat hairaṇya aṇḍa samudbhavam sā mūrtiḥ sarva bhūtānām iti evam anuśuśruma saṃvatsaram uṣitvā aṇḍe niṣkramya ca mahā muniḥ saṃdadhe ardham mahīm kṛtsnām divam ardham prajāpatiḥ dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ iti eṣa rājan vedeṣu paṭhyate tayoḥ śakalayoḥ madhyam ākāśam akarot prabhuḥ etasya api ca saṃkhyānam veda vedāṅga pāragaiḥ rātrim etāvatīm ca asya prāhuḥ adhyātma cintakāḥ sṛjati ahaṃkāram ṛṣiḥ bhūtam divya ātmakam tathā caturaḥ ca aparān putrān dehāt pūrvam mahān ṛṣiḥ te vai pitṛbhyaḥ pitaraḥ śrūyante rāja sattama devāḥ pitṝṇām ca sutāḥ devaiḥ lokāḥ samāvṛtāḥ cara acarāḥ nara śreṣṭhaḥ iti evam anuśuśruma parameṣṭhī tu ahaṃkāraḥ asṛjat bhūtāni pañcadhā pṛthivī vāyuḥ ākāśam āpaḥ jyotiḥ ca pañcamam etasya api niśām āhuḥ tṛtīyam iha kurvataḥ śabdaḥ sparśaḥ ca rūpam ca rasaḥ gandhaḥ ca pañcamaḥ ete viśeṣāḥ rāja indra mahābhūteṣu pañcasu yaiḥ āviṣṭāni bhūtāni ahani ahani pārthiva te vadhyamānāḥ anyonyam guṇaiḥ hāribhiḥ avyayāḥ trīṇi kalpa sahasrāṇi eteṣām ahar ucyate cakṣuḥ paśyati rūpāṇi manasā tu na cakṣuṣā tathā indriyāṇi sarvāṇi paśyanti iti abhicakṣate evam manaḥ pradhānāni indriyāṇi vibhāvayet indriyāṇām hi sarveṣām īśvaram manaḥ ucyate etat viśanti bhūtāni sarvāṇi iha mahā yaśāḥ yājñavalkyaḥ uvāca tattvānām sarga saṃkhyā ca kāla saṃkhyā tathā eva ca mayā prokta ānupūrvyeṇa saṃhāram api me śṛṇu codayām āsa bhagavān avyaktaḥ ahaṃkṛtam naram tatas śata sahasra aṃśuḥ avyaktena abhicoditaḥ kṛtvā dvādaśadhā ātmānam ādityaḥ jvalat agni vat caturvidham prajā jālam nirdahati āśu tejasā jarāyu aṇḍa sveda jātam udbhijjam ca narādhipa etat unmeṣa mātreṇa sthāṇu jaṅgamam kūrma pṛṣṭha samā bhūmiḥ bhavati atha samantataḥ jagat dagdhvā amita balaḥ kevalam jagatīm tatas ambhasā balinā kṣipram āpūryata samantataḥ tatas kālāgnim āsādya tat ambhaḥ yāti saṃkṣayam vinaṣṭe ambhasi rāja indra analaḥ mahān ūṣmāṇam sarva bhūtānām sapta atha añjasā bhakṣayām āsa balavān vāyuḥ aṣṭa ātmakaḥ balī tam apratibalam bhīmam ākāśam grasate manaḥ grasati sarva ātmā saḥ ahaṃkāraḥ prajāpatiḥ ahaṃkāram mahān ātmā bhūta bhavya bhaviṣya vid tam api anupama ātmānam viśvam śaṃbhuḥ prajāpatiḥ aṇimā laghimā prāptiḥ īśānaḥ jyotiḥ avyayaḥ sarvatas pāṇi pāda antaḥ sarvatas akṣi śiraḥ mukhaḥ sarvatas śrutimān loke sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati hṛdayam sarva bhūtānām parvaṇaḥ aṅguṣṭha mātrakaḥ anugrasati anantam hi mahātmā viśvam īśvaraḥ bhūta bhavya manuṣyāṇām sraṣṭāram anagham tathā eṣaḥ apyayaḥ te rāja indra yathāvat paribhāṣitaḥ adhyātmam adhibhūtam ca adhidaivam ca śrūyatām yājñavalkyaḥ uvāca pādau adhyātmam iti āhuḥ brāhmaṇāḥ tattva darśinaḥ pāyuḥ adhyātmam iti āhuḥ yathā tattva artha darśinaḥ adhibhūtam tathā ānandaḥ daivatam ca prajāpatiḥ hastau adhyātmam iti āhuḥ yathā sāṃkhya nidarśanam ghrāṇam adhyātmam iti āhuḥ yathā śruti nidarśanam gandhaḥ eva adhibhūtam tu pṛthivī ca adhidaivatam sparśaḥ eva adhibhūtam tu pavanaḥ ca adhidaivatam eṣā te vyaktataḥ rājan vibhūtiḥ anuvarṇitā krīḍā artham tu mahā rāja śataśas atha sahasraśas yathā dīpa sahasrāṇi dīpān martyāḥ prakurvate prakṛtiḥ tathā vikurute puruṣasya guṇān bahūn sattvam ānandaḥ udrekaḥ prītiḥ prākāśyam eva ca sukham śuddhi tvam ārogyam saṃtoṣaḥ śraddadhāna tā akārpaṇyam asaṃrambhaḥ kṣamā dhṛtiḥ ahiṃsa tā sama tā satyam ānṛṇyam mārdavam hrīḥ acāpalam śaucam ārjavam ācāram a laulyam hṛdi asaṃbhramaḥ iṣṭa aniṣṭa viyogānām kṛtānām avikatthanam dānena ca anugrahaṇam aspṛhā arthe parārtha tā sarva bhūta dayā ca eva sattvasya ete guṇāḥ smṛtāḥ rajaḥ guṇānām saṃghātaḥ rūpam aiśvarya vigrahe ati āśi tvam akāruṇyam sukha duḥkha upasevanam para apavādeṣu ratiḥ vivādānām ca sevanam paritāpaḥ apaharaṇam hrī nāśaḥ anārjavam tathā darpaḥ dveṣaḥ ativādaḥ ca ete proktāḥ rajaḥ guṇāḥ tāmasānām tu saṃghātam pravakṣyāmi upadhāryatām maraṇam ca andhatāmisram tāmisram krodhaḥ ucyate tamasaḥ lakṣaṇāni iha bhakṣāṇām abhirocanam bhojanānām aparyāptiḥ tathā peyeṣu atṛpta tā gandha vāsaḥ vihāreṣu śayaneṣu āsaneṣu ca nṛtya vāditra gītānām ajñānāt śraddadhāna tā dveṣaḥ dharma viśeṣāṇām ete vai tāmasāḥ guṇāḥ yājñavalkyaḥ uvāca koṭiśas ca karoti eṣa pratyagātmānam ātmanā tāmasasya adhamam sthānam prāhuḥ adhyātma cintakāḥ puṇya pāpena mānuṣyam adharmeṇa api adhogatim dvaṃdvam eṣām trayāṇām tu saṃnipātam ca tattvataḥ sattvasya rajasaḥ ca eva tamasaḥ ca śṛṇuṣva me sattvasya tu rajaḥ dṛṣṭam rajasaḥ ca tamaḥ tathā puṇya pāpa viyuktānām sthānam āhuḥ manīṣiṇām śāsvatam ca avyayam ca eva akṣaram ca abhayam ca yat jñāninām saṃbhavam śreṣṭham sthānam avraṇam acyutam avyakta stham param yat tat pṛṣṭaḥ te aham narādhipa acetanaḥ ca eṣa mataḥ prakṛti sthaḥ ca pārthiva etena adhiṣṭhitaḥ ca eva sṛjate saṃharati api an ādi nidhanau etau ubhau eva mahā mune agrāhyau ṛṣi śārdūla katham ekaḥ hi acetanaḥ cetanāvān tathā ca ekaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ iti bhāṣitaḥ sāṃkhya jñānam ca tattvena pṛthak yogam tathā eva ca viditam sarvam etat te pāṇau āmalakam yathā yājñavalkyaḥ uvāca na śakyaḥ nirguṇaḥ tāta guṇīkartum viśām pate guṇavān ca api aguṇavān yathātattvam nibodha me guṇaiḥ hi guṇavān eva nirguṇaḥ ca aguṇaḥ tathā prāhuḥ evam mahātmānaḥ munayaḥ tattva darśinaḥ upayuṅkte ca tān eva sa ca eva ajñaḥ svabhāvataḥ avyaktaḥ tu na jānīte puruṣaḥ jñaḥ svabhāvataḥ nitya tvāt akṣara tvāt ca kṣarāṇām tattvataḥ anyathā yadā ajñānena kurvīta guṇa sargam punar punar yadā ātmānam na jānīte tadā avyaktam iha ucyate kartṛ tvāt ca api tattvānām tattva dharmī tathā ucyate kartṛ tvāt prakṛtīnām tu tathā prakṛti dharmi tā kartṛ tvāt ca api bījānām bīja dharmī tathā ucyate guṇānām prasava tvāt ca tathā prasava dharmavān kartṛ tvāt pralayānām ca tathā pralaya dharmi tā sarva bhūta dayāvantaḥ kevalam jñānam āsthitāḥ yathā muñjaḥ iṣīkāyāḥ tathā eva etat hi jāyate anyam ca maśakam vidyāt anyat ca udumbaram tathā eteṣām saha saṃvāsam vivāsam ca eva nityaśas yathā tathā enam paśyanti na nityam prākṛtāḥ janāḥ evam hi parisaṃkhyāya sāṃkhyāḥ kevala tām gatāḥ atas param pravakṣyāmi yogānām api darśanam yājñavalkyaḥ uvāca sāṃkhya jñānam mayā proktam yoga jñānam nibodha me yathāśrutam yathādṛṣṭam tattvena nṛpa sattama nā asti sāṃkhya samam jñānam nā asti yoga samam balam vayam tu rājan paśyāmaḥ ekam eva tu niścayāt yat eva yogāḥ paśyanti tat sāṃkhyaiḥ api dṛśyate ekam sāṃkhyam ca yogam ca yaḥ paśyati sa tattva vid yāvat hi pralayaḥ tāta sūkṣmeṇa aṣṭaguṇena vai vedeṣu ca aṣṭa guṇitam yogam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ sūkṣmam aṣṭaguṇam prāhuḥ na itaram nṛpa sattama dviguṇam yoga kṛtyam tu yogānām prāhuḥ uttamam sa guṇam nirguṇam ca eva yathā śāstra nidarśanam dhāraṇā ca eva manasaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ ca pārthiva prāṇāyāmaḥ hi sa guṇaḥ nirguṇam dhāraṇam manaḥ niśāyāḥ prathame yāme codanāḥ dvādaśa smṛtāḥ madhye suptvā pare yāme dvādaśā eva tu codanāḥ tat evam upaśāntena dāntena ekānta śīlinā ātma ārāmeṇa buddhena yoktavyaḥ ātmā na saṃśayaḥ pañcānām indriyāṇām tu doṣān ākṣipya pañcadhā śabdam sparśam tathā rūpam rasam gandham tathā eva ca manaḥ tathā eva ahaṃkāre pratiṣṭhāpya narādhipa ahaṃkāram tathā buddhau buddhim ca prakṛtau api śāśvatam ca avyayam ca eva īśānam brahma ca avyayam yuktasya tu mahā rāja lakṣaṇāni upadhārayet lakṣaṇam tu prasādasya yathā tṛptaḥ sukham svapet niścala ūrdhva śikhaḥ tadvat yuktam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ pāṣāṇaḥ iva megha utthaiḥ yathā bindubhiḥ āhataḥ na alam cālayitum śakyaḥ tathā yuktasya lakṣaṇam taila pātram yathā pūrṇam karābhyām gṛhya pūruṣaḥ sopānam āruhet bhītaḥ tarjyamānaḥ asi pāṇibhiḥ saṃyata ātmā bhayāt teṣām na pātrāt bindum utsṛjet sthira tvāt indriyāṇām tu niścala tvāt tathā eva ca kālena mahatā rājan śrutiḥ eṣā sanātanī etat hi yogam yogānām kim anyat yoga lakṣaṇam vijñāya tat hi manyante kṛtakṛtyāḥ manīṣiṇaḥ yājñavalkyaḥ uvāca tathā evā utkramamāṇam tu śṛṇuṣva avahitaḥ nṛpa padbhyām utkramamāṇasya vaiṣṇavam sthānam ucyate jaṅghābhyām tu vasūn devān āpnuyāt iti naḥ śrutam jānubhyām ca mahābhāgān devān sādhyān avāpnuyāt pāyunā utkramamāṇaḥ tu maitram sthānam avāpnuyāt pṛthivīm jaghanena atha ūrubhyām tu prajāpatim pārśvābhyām marutaḥ devān nāsābhyām indum eva ca grīvāyāḥ tam ṛṣi śreṣṭham naram āpnoti anuttamam viśvedevān mukhena atha diśaḥ śrotreṇa ca āpnuyāt ghrāṇena gandha vahanam netrābhyām sūryam eva ca bhrūbhyām ca eva aśvinau devau lalāṭena pitṝn atha brahmāṇam āpnoti vibhum mūrdhnā devāgrajam tathā etāni utkramaṇa sthānāni uktāni mithilā īśvara ariṣṭāni tu vakṣyāmi vihitāni manīṣibhiḥ saṃvatsara viyogasya saṃbhaveyuḥ śarīriṇaḥ yaḥ arundhatīm na paśyeta dṛṣṭa pūrvām kadā cana khaṇḍa ābhāsam dakṣiṇatas te api saṃvatsara āyuṣaḥ para cakṣuṣi ca ātmānam ye na paśyanti pārthiva te api saṃvatsara āyuṣaḥ ati dyutiḥ ati prajñā aprajñā ca adyutiḥ tathā prakṛteḥ vikriyā āpattiḥ ṣaṣ māsāt mṛtyu lakṣaṇam daivatāni avajānāti brāhmaṇaiḥ ca virudhyate kṛṣṇa śyāva chavi chāyaḥ ṣaṣ māsāt mṛtyu lakṣaṇam śīrṇa nābhi yathā cakram chidram somam prapaśyati tathā eva ca sahasrāṃśum sapta rātreṇa mṛtyu bhāj devatāyatana sthaḥ tu ṣaṣ rātreṇa sa mṛtyu bhāj karṇa nāsā avanamanam danta dṛṣṭi virāgi tā saṃjñā lopaḥ nirūṣma tvam sadyas mṛtyuni darśanam etāvanti tu ariṣṭāni viditvā mānavaḥ ātmavān niśi ca ahani ca ātmānam yojayet paramātmani pratīkṣamāṇaḥ tat kālam yat kālam prati tat bhavet atha asya na iṣṭam maraṇam sthātum icchet imām kriyām sarva gandhān rasān ca eva dhārayeta samāhitaḥ tathā hi mṛtyum jayati tatpareṇa antarātmanā sa sāṃkhya dhāraṇam ca eva viditvā manuja ṛṣabha jayet ca mṛtyum yogena tatpareṇa antarātmanā śāśvatam sthānam acalam duṣprāpam akṛtātmabhiḥ yājñavalkyaḥ uvāca avyakta stham param yat tat pṛṣṭaḥ te aham narādhipa param guhyam imam praśnam śṛṇuṣva avahitaḥ nṛpa mayā ādityāt avāptāni yajūṃṣi mithilā adhipa mahatā tapasā devaḥ tapiṣṭhaḥ sevitaḥ mayā prītena ca aham vibhunā sūryeṇa uktaḥ tadā anagha varam vṛṇīṣva viprarṣe yat iṣṭam te su durlabham tat te dāsyāmi prīta ātmā mad prasādaḥ hi durlabhaḥ tatas praṇamya śirasā mayā uktaḥ tapatām varaḥ yajūṃṣi na upayuktāni kṣipram icchāmi veditum tatas mām bhagavān āha vitariṣyāmi te dvija sarasvatī iha vāc bhūtā śarīram te pravekṣyati tatas mām āha bhagavān āsyam svam vivṛtam kuru vivṛtam ca tatas me praviṣṭā ca sarasvatī avijñānāt amarṣāt ca bhāskarasya mahātmanaḥ tatas vidahyamānam mām uvāca bhagavān raviḥ muhūrtam sahyatām dāhaḥ tatas śītībhaviṣyasi śītībhūtam ca mām dṛṣṭvā bhagavān āha bhāskaraḥ kṛtsnam śatapatham ca eva praṇeṣyasi dvijarṣabha prāpsyase ca yat iṣṭam tat sāṃkhya yoga īpsitam padam tatas anuvyāhṛtam śrutvā gate deve vibhāvasau gṛham āgatya saṃhṛṣṭaḥ acintayam vai sarasvatīm tatas pravṛttā ati śubhā svara vyañjana bhūṣitā oṃkāram āditas kṛtvā mama devī sarasvatī tapatām ca variṣṭhāya niṣaṇṇaḥ tad parāyaṇaḥ tatas śatapatham kṛtsnam sa rahasyam sa saṃgraham cakre sa pariśeṣam ca harṣeṇa parameṇa ha kṛtvā ca adhyayanam teṣām śiṣyāṇām śatam uttamam vipriya artham sa śiṣyasya mātulasya mahātmanaḥ tatas sa śiṣyeṇa mayā sūryeṇa iva gabhastibhiḥ vyāptaḥ yajñaḥ mahā rāja pituḥ tava mahātmanaḥ daśa pañca ca prāptāni yajūṃṣi arkāt mayā anagha sūryasya ca anubhāvena pravṛttaḥ aham narādhipa kartum śata patham vedam apūrvam kāritam ca me yathā abhilaṣitam mārgam tathā tat ca upapāditam śiṣyāṇām akhilam kṛtsnam anujñātam sa saṃgraham sarve ca śiṣyāḥ śucayaḥ gatāḥ parama harṣitāḥ śākhāḥ pañcadaśa imāḥ tu vidyāḥ bhāskara darśitāḥ pratiṣṭhāpya yathākāmam vedyam tat anucintayam viśvāvasuḥ tatas rājan vedānta jñāna kovidaḥ caturviṃśatikān praśnān pṛṣṭvā vedasya pārthiva pañcaviṃśatimam praśnam papraccha ānvīkṣikīm tathā mitram varuṇam eva ca jñānam jñeyam tathā ajñaḥ jñaḥ kaḥ tapāḥ atapāḥ tathā athā uktaḥ ca mayā rājan rājā gandharva sattamaḥ pṛṣṭavān anupūrveṇa praśnam uttamam arthavat muhūrtam mṛṣyatām tāvat yāvat enam vicintaye bāḍham iti eva kṛtvā sa tūṣṇīm gandharvaḥ āsthitaḥ tatra upaniṣadam ca eva pariśeṣam ca pārthiva mathnāmi manasā tāta dṛṣṭvā ca ānvīkṣikīm parām caturthī rāja śārdūla vidyā eṣā sāṃparāyikī udīritā mayā tubhyam pañcaviṃśe adhi dhiṣṭhitā athā uktaḥ tu mayā rājan rājā viśvāvasuḥ tadā śrūyatām yat bhavān asmān praśnam saṃpṛṣṭavān iha viśva avyaktam param vidyāt bhūta bhavya bhayaṃkaram triguṇam guṇa kartṛ tvāt aviśvaḥ niṣkalaḥ tathā avyaktam prakṛtim prāhuḥ puruṣa iti ca nirguṇam tathā eva mitram puruṣam varuṇam prakṛtim tathā jñānam tu prakṛtim prāhuḥ jñeyam niṣkalam eva ca ajñaḥ ca jñaḥ ca puruṣaḥ tasmāt niṣkalaḥ ucyate tapāḥ prakṛtiḥ iti āhuḥ atapāḥ niṣkalaḥ smṛtaḥ cala acalam iti proktam tvayā tat api me śṛṇu calām tu prakṛtim prāhuḥ kāraṇam kṣepa sargayoḥ akṣepa sargayoḥ kartā niścalaḥ puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ akṣayam puruṣam prāhuḥ kṣayaḥ hi asya na vidyate guṇa kṣaya tvāt prakṛtiḥ kartṛ tvāt akṣayam budhāḥ eṣā te vidyā caturthī sāṃparāyikī vidyā upetam dhanam kṛtvā karmaṇā nityakarmaṇi ekānta darśanāḥ vedāḥ sarve viśvāvaso smṛtāḥ sa aṅga upāṅgān api yadi pañca vedān adhīyate yaḥ ghṛta arthī kharī kṣīram mathet gandharva sattama viṣṭhām tatra anupaśyeta na maṇḍam na api vā ghṛtam sa kevalam mūḍha matiḥ jñāna bhāravahaḥ smṛtaḥ tadā sa kevalībhūtaḥ ṣaḍviṃśam anupaśyati anyaḥ ca śaśvat avyaktaḥ tathā anyaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ janma mṛtyu bhayāt yogāḥ sāṃkhyāḥ ca parama eṣiṇaḥ viśvāvasuḥ uvāca pañcaviṃśam yat etat te proktam brāhmaṇa sattama parāśarasya viprarṣeḥ vārṣagaṇyasya dhīmataḥ gautamasya ārṣṭiṣeṇasya gargasya ca mahātmanaḥ bhavān prabarhaḥ śāstrāṇām pragalbhaḥ ca ati buddhimān na tava aviditam kim cit bhavān śruti nidhiḥ smṛtaḥ patiḥ ca tapatām śaśvat ādityaḥ tava bhāṣate sāṃkhya jñānam tvayā brahman avāptam kṛtsnam eva ca tathā eva yoga jñānam ca yājñavalkya viśeṣataḥ śrotum icchāmi tat jñānam ghṛtam maṇḍa mayam yathā yājñavalkyaḥ uvāca jijñāsasi ca mām rājan tat nibodha yathāśrutam a budhyamānām prakṛtim budhyate pañcaviṃśakaḥ sāṃkhya yogāḥ ca tattva jñāḥ yathāśruti nidarśanāt paśyan tathā eva a paśyan ca paśyati anyaḥ tathā anagha ṣaḍviṃśaḥ pañcaviṃśam ca caturviṃśam ca paśyati na caturviṃśakaḥ a grāhyaḥ manujaiḥ jñāna darśibhiḥ sa snehaḥ sahavāsāt ca sa abhimānaḥ ca nityaśas tadā sa kevalībhūtaḥ ṣaḍviṃśam anupaśyati anyaḥ ca rājan avaraḥ tathā anyaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ janma mṛtyu bhayāt bhītāḥ yogāḥ sāṃkhyāḥ ca kāśyapa ṣaḍviṃśam anupaśyanti śucayaḥ tad parāyaṇāḥ yadā sa kevalībhūtaḥ ṣaḍviṃśam anupaśyati buddhaḥ ca uktaḥ yathātattvam mayā śruti nidarśanāt paśya apaśyam yaḥ anupaśyet kṣemam tattvam ca kāśyapa kevala akevalam ca ādyam pañcaviṃśāt param ca yat viśvāvasuḥ uvāca tathyam śubham ca etat uktam tvayā bhoḥ samyak kṣemyam devatā ādyam yathāvat yājñavalkyaḥ uvāca evam uktvā saṃprayātaḥ divam sa vibhrājan vai śrīmatā darśanena tuṣṭaḥ ca tuṣṭyā parayā abhinandya pradakṣiṇam mama kṛtvā mahātmā brahma ādīnām khecarāṇām kṣitau ca ye ca adhastāt saṃvasante narendra sāṃkhyāḥ sarve sāṃkhya dharme ratāḥ ca tadvat yogāḥ yoga dharme ratāḥ ca ye ca api anye mokṣa kāmāḥ manuṣyāḥ teṣām etat darśanam jñāna dṛṣṭam jñānāt mokṣaḥ jāyate pūruṣāṇām na asti ajñānāt evam āhuḥ narendra tasmāt jñānam tattvataḥ anveṣitavyam yena ātmānam mokṣayet janma mṛtyoḥ prāpya jñānam brāhmaṇāt kṣatriyāt vā vaiśyāt śūdrāt api nīcāt abhīkṣṇam śraddhātavyam śraddadhānena nityam na śraddhinam janma mṛtyū viśetām sarve varṇāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ brahma jāḥ ca sarve nityam vyāharante ca brahma brahma āsyataḥ brāhmaṇāḥ saṃprasūtāḥ bāhubhyām vai kṣatriyāḥ saṃprasūtāḥ nābhyām vaiśyāḥ pādataḥ ca api śūdrāḥ sarve varṇāḥ na anyathā veditavyāḥ ajñānataḥ karma yonim bhajante tām tām rājan te yathā yānti abhāvam tathā varṇāḥ jñāna hīnāḥ patante ghorāt ajñānāt prākṛtam yoni jālam tasmāt jñānam sarvatas mārgitavyam sarvatra stham ca etat uktam mayā te tasthau brahmā tasthivān ca aparaḥ yaḥ tasmai nityam mokṣam āhuḥ dvijendrāḥ yat te pṛṣṭam tat mayā ca upadiṣṭam yāthātathyam tat viśokaḥ bhavasva bhīṣmaḥ uvāca saḥ evam anuśāstaḥ tu yājñavalkyena dhīmatā prītimān abhavat rājā mithilā adhipatiḥ tadā go koṭim sparśayām āsa hiraṇyasya tathā eva ca sāṃkhya jñānam adhīyānaḥ yoga śāstram ca kṛtsnaśas janma mṛtyū ca rāja indra prākṛtam tat acintayat paśyanti yogāḥ sāṃkhyāḥ ca sva śāstra kṛta lakṣaṇāḥ iṣṭa aniṣṭa viyuktam hi tasthau brahma parātparam nityam tam āhuḥ vidvāṃsaḥ śuciḥ tasmāt śuciḥ bhava dadāti ca nara śreṣṭha pratigṛhṇāti yat ca ha yasya avyaktam na viditam sa guṇam nirguṇam punar tena tīrthāni yajñāḥ ca sevitavyāḥ vipaścitā labhate avyakta saṃsthānam jñātvā avyaktam mahīpate ahaṃkārāt param ca api sthānāni samavāpnuyāt ye tu avyaktāt param nityam jānate śāstra tatparāḥ etat mayā āptam janakāt purastāt tena api ca āptam nṛpa yājñavalkyāt jñānam viśiṣṭam na tathā hi yajñāḥ jñānena durgam tarate na yajñaiḥ kṣetrajña vid pārthiva jñāna yajñam upāsya vai tattvam ṛṣiḥ bhaviṣyasi yat upagaṇita śāśvata avyayam tat śubham amṛta tvam aśokam ṛcchati iti yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca aiśvaryam vā mahat prāpya dhanam vā bharata ṛṣabha tapasā vā su mahatā karmaṇā vā śrutena vā bhīṣmaḥ uvāca atrā api udāharanti imam itihāsam purātanam bhikṣoḥ pañcaśikhasya iha saṃvādam janakasya ca tapasā vā atha buddhyā vā karmaṇā vā śrutena vā na hi ahāni nivartante na māsāḥ na punar kṣapāḥ kālena jātāḥ jātāḥ hi vāyunā iva abhra saṃcayāḥ jarā mṛtyū hi bhūtānām khāditārau vṛkau iva balinām durbalānām ca hrasvānām mahatām api evaṃbhūteṣu bhūteṣu nitya bhūta adhruveṣu ca katham hṛṣyeta jāteṣu mṛteṣu ca katham jvaret yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca saṃnyasyate yathā ātmā ayam saṃnyasta ātmā yathā ca yaḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca atrā api udāharanti imam itihāsam purātanam janakasya ca saṃvādam sulabhāyāḥ ca bhārata saṃnyāsa phalikaḥ kaḥ cit babhūva nṛpatiḥ purā sa vede mokṣa śāstre ca sve ca śāstre kṛta āgamaḥ indriyāṇi samādhāya śaśāsa vasudhām imām tasya veda vidaḥ prājñāḥ śrutvā tām sādhu vṛtta tām lokeṣu spṛhayanti anye puruṣāḥ puruṣa īśvara mahīm anucacāra ekā sulabhā nāma bhikṣukī tayā jagat idam sarvam aṭantyā mithilā īśvaraḥ sā su sūkṣmām kathām śrutvā tathyam na iti sa saṃśayā tatas sā viprahāya atha pūrva rūpam hi yogataḥ cakṣuḥ nimeṣa mātreṇa laghu astra gati gāminī videhānām purīm subhrūḥ jagāma kamala īkṣaṇā sā prāpya mithilām ramyām samṛddha jana saṃkulām rājā tasyāḥ param dṛṣṭvā saukumāryam vapuḥ tathā tatas asyāḥ svāgatam kṛtvā vyādiśya ca varāsanam pūjitām pāda śaucena vara annena api atarpayat atha bhuktavatī prītā rājānam mantribhiḥ vṛtam sarva bhāṣya vidām madhye āsa bhikṣukī netrābhyām netrayoḥ asya raśmīn saṃyojya raśmibhiḥ janakaḥ api utsmayan rājā bhāvam asyāḥ viśeṣayan pratijagrāha bhāvena bhāvam asyāḥ nṛpa uttamaḥ tat ekasmin adhiṣṭhāne saṃvādaḥ śrūyatām ayam chatra ādiṣu vimuktasya muktāyāḥ ca tridaṇḍake bhagavatyāḥ kva caryā iyam kṛtā kva ca gamiṣyasi eṣu artheṣu uttaram tasmāt pravedyam sat samāgame chatra ādiṣu viśeṣeṣu muktam mām viddhi sarvaśas sa tvām saṃmantum icchāmi māna arhā asi matā hi me yasmāt ca etat mayā prāptam jñānam vaiśeṣikam purā yasya na anyaḥ pravaktā asti mokṣe tam api me śṛṇu pārāśarya sagotrasya vṛddhasya su mahātmanaḥ bhikṣoḥ pañcaśikhasya aham śiṣyaḥ parama saṃmataḥ sāṃkhya jñāne tathā yoge mahīpāla vidhau tathā sa yathā śāstra dṛṣṭena mārgeṇa iha parivrajan vārṣikān caturaḥ māsān purā mayi sukha uṣitaḥ tena aham sāṃkhya mukhyena su dṛṣṭa arthena tattvataḥ śrāvitaḥ trividham mokṣam na ca rājyāt vicālitaḥ saḥ aham tām akhilām vṛttim trividhām mokṣa saṃhitām jñānāt eva ca vairāgyam jāyate yena mucyate sā iyam paramikā buddhiḥ prāptā nirdvaṃdva tā mayā yathā kṣetram mṛdūbhūtam adbhiḥ āplāvitam tathā yathā ca uttāpitam bījam kapāle yatra tatra vā prāpya api aṅkura hetu tvam abīja tvāt na jāyate tadvat bhagavatā tena śikhā proktena bhikṣuṇā jñānam kṛtam abījam me viṣayeṣu na jāyate yaḥ ca me dakṣiṇam bāhum candanena samukṣayet savyam vā asyā ca yaḥ takṣet samau etau ubhau mama sukhī saḥ aham avāpta arthaḥ sama loṣṭa aśma kāñcanaḥ mukta saṅgaḥ sthitaḥ rājye viśiṣṭaḥ anyaiḥ tridaṇḍibhiḥ mokṣe hi trividhā niṣṭhā dṛṣṭā pūrvaiḥ mahā ṛṣibhiḥ jñānam loka uttaram yat ca sarva tyāgaḥ ca karmaṇām jñāna niṣṭhām vadanti eke mokṣa śāstra vidaḥ janāḥ karma niṣṭhām tathā eva anye yatayaḥ sūkṣma darśinaḥ tṛtīyā iyam samākhyātā niṣṭhā tena mahātmanā māne dambhe tathā snehe sadṛśāḥ te kuṭumbibhiḥ tridaṇḍa ādiṣu yadi asti mokṣaḥ jñānena kena cit doṣa darśī tu gārhasthye yaḥ vrajati āśrama antaram utsṛjan parigṛhṇan ca saḥ api saṅgāt na mucyate rājarṣi bhikṣuka ācāryāḥ mucyante kena hetunā kāṣāya dhāraṇam mauṇḍyam tri viṣṭabdhaḥ kamaṇḍaluḥ liṅgāni atyartham etāni na mokṣāya iti me matiḥ yadi sati api liṅge asmin jñānam eva atra kāraṇam atha vā duḥkha śaithilyam vīkṣya liṅge kṛtā matiḥ kim tat eva artha sāmānyam chatra ādiṣu na lakṣyate rājya aiśvarya mayaḥ pāśaḥ sneha āyatana bandhanaḥ mokṣa aśma niśitena iha chinnaḥ tyāga asinā mayā ayathārthaḥ hi te varṇaḥ vakṣyāmi śṛṇu tat mama saukumāryam tathā rūpam vapuḥ agryam tathā vayaḥ tava etāni samastāni niyamaḥ ca iti saṃśayaḥ yat ca api ananurūpam te liṅgasya asya viceṣṭitam mad pakṣa saṃśrayāt ca ayam śṛṇu yaḥ te vyatikramaḥ āśrayantyāḥ svabhāvena mama pūrva parigraham praveśaḥ te kṛtaḥ kena mama rāṣṭre pure tathā kasya vā saṃnisargāt tvam praviṣṭā hṛdayam mama na āvayoḥ eka yogaḥ asti mā kṛthāḥ varṇa saṃkaram ayam ca api su kaṣṭaḥ te dvitīyaḥ āśrama saṃkaraḥ sagotrām vā asagotrām vā na veda tvām na vettha mām sagotram āviśantyāḥ te tṛtīyaḥ gotra saṃkaraḥ sā tvam etāni akāryāṇi kārya apekṣā vyavasyasi avijñānena vā yuktāḥ mithyā jñānena vā punar idam anyat tṛtīyam te bhāva sparśa vighātakam duṣṭāyāḥ lakṣyate liṅgam pravaktavyam prakāśitam na mayi eva abhisaṃdhiḥ te jaya eṣiṇyā jaye kṛtaḥ tathā hi evam punar ca tvam dṛṣṭim svām pratimuñcasi mad pakṣa pratighātāya sva pakṣa udbhāvanāya ca bhūyas sṛjasi yoga astram viṣa amṛtam iva ekadhā alābhaḥ ca api araktasya saḥ atra doṣaḥ viṣa upamaḥ mā sprākṣīḥ sadhu jānīṣva sva śāstram anupālaya kṛtā iyam hi vijijñāsā muktaḥ na iti tvayā mama sā yadi tvam sva kāryeṇa yadi anyasya mahīpateḥ na rājānam mṛṣā gacchet na dvijātim katham cana na striyam strī guṇa upetām hanyuḥ hi ete mṛṣā āgatāḥ rājñām hi balam aiśvaryam brahma brahma vidām balam rūpa yauvana saubhāgyam strīṇām balam anuttamam ārjavena abhigantavyāḥ vināśāya hi anārjavam sā tvam jātim śrutam vṛttam bhāvam prakṛtim ātmanaḥ pratyādiṣṭā narendreṇa sulabhā na vyakampata ukta vākye tu nṛpatau sulabhā cāru darśanā tatas cārutaram vākyam pracakrāma atha bhāṣitum navabhiḥ navabhiḥ ca eva doṣaiḥ vāc buddhi dūṣaṇaiḥ apetam upapanna artham aṣṭādaśa guṇa anvitam pañca etāni artha jātāni vākyam iti ucyate nṛpa eṣām ekaikaśas arthānām saukṣmya ādīnām su lakṣaṇam śṛṇu saṃsāryamāṇānām padārthaiḥ pada vākyataḥ jñānam jñeyeṣu bhinneṣu yathā abhedena vartate doṣāṇām ca guṇānām ca pramāṇam pravibhāgaśaḥ idam pūrvam idam paścāt vaktavyam yat vivakṣitam krama yogam tam api āhuḥ vākyam vākya vidaḥ janāḥ dharma artha kāma mokṣeṣu pratijñāya viśeṣataḥ tāni etāni yathā uktāni saukṣmya ādīni janādhipa eka artha samavetāni vākyam mama niśāmaya upeta artham abhinna artham na apavṛttam na ca adhikam na aślakṣṇam na ca saṃdigdham vakṣyāmi paramam tava na anṛtam na trivargeṇa viruddham na api asaṃskṛtam na nyūnam kaṣṭa śabdam vā vyutkrama abhihitam na ca na śeṣam na anukalpena niṣkāraṇam ahetukam kāmāt krodhāt bhayāt lobhāt dainyāt ānāryakāt tathā hrītaḥ anukrośataḥ mānāt na vakṣyāmi katham cana vaktā śrotā ca vākyam ca yadā tu avikalam nṛpa samam eti vivakṣāyām tadā saḥ arthaḥ prakāśate sva artham āha para artham vā tadā vākyam na rohati atha yaḥ sva artham utsṛjya para artham prāha mānavaḥ viśaṅkā jāyate tasmin vākyam tat api doṣavat śrotuḥ ca eva ātmanaḥ ca eva sa vaktā na itaraḥ nṛpa tat arthavat idam vākyam upetam vākya saṃpadā avikṣipta manāḥ rājan ekāgraḥ śrotum arhasi tatra uttaram idam vākyam rājan ekamanāḥ śṛṇu yathā jatu ca kāṣṭham ca pāṃsavaḥ ca uda bindubhiḥ su śliṣṭāni tathā rājan prāṇinām iha saṃbhavaḥ śabdaḥ sparśaḥ rasaḥ rūpam gandhaḥ pañca indriyāṇi ca pṛthak ātmā daśa ātmānaḥ saṃśliṣṭāḥ jatu kāṣṭha vat na ca eṣām codanā kā cit asti iti eṣa viniścayaḥ ekaikasya iha vijñānam na asti ātmani tathā pare na veda cakṣuḥ cakṣuṣṭvam śrotram na ātmani vartate saṃśliṣṭāḥ na abhijāyante yathā apaḥ iha pāṃsavaḥ bāhyān anyān apekṣante guṇān tān api me śṛṇu rūpam cakṣuḥ prakāśaḥ ca darśane hetavaḥ trayaḥ yathā eva atra tathā anyeṣu jñāna jñeyeṣu hetavaḥ jñāna jñeya antare tasmin manaḥ nāma aparaḥ guṇaḥ vicārayati yena ayam niścaye sādhu asādhunī dvādaśaḥ tu aparaḥ tatra buddhiḥ nāma guṇaḥ smṛtaḥ atha dvādaśake tasmin sattvam nāma aparaḥ guṇaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ iti ca api anyaḥ guṇaḥ tatra caturdaśaḥ atha pañcadaśaḥ rājan guṇaḥ tatra aparaḥ smṛtaḥ guṇaḥ tu eva aparaḥ tatra saṃghātaḥ iti ṣoḍaśaḥ sukha duḥkhe jarā mṛtyū lābha alābhau priya apriye iti ca ekonaviṃśaḥ ayam dvaṃdva yogaḥ iti smṛtaḥ ūrdhvam ekonaviṃśatyāḥ kālaḥ nāma aparaḥ guṇaḥ iti imam viddhi viṃśatyā bhūtānām prabhava apyayam viṃśakaḥ ca eṣa saṃghātaḥ mahābhūtāni pañca ca iti evam viṃśatiḥ ca eva guṇāḥ sapta ca ye smṛtāḥ vidhiḥ śukram balam ca iti trayaḥ ete guṇāḥ pare ekaviṃśaḥ ca daśa ca kalāḥ saṃkhyānataḥ smṛtāḥ avyaktam prakṛtim tu āsām kalānām kaḥ cit icchati vyaktam ca āsām tathā eva anyaḥ sthūla darśī prapaśyati avyaktam yadi vā vyaktam dvayīm atha catuṣṭayīm prakṛtim sarva bhūtānām paśyanti adhyātma cintakāḥ sā iyam prakṛtiḥ avyaktā kalābhiḥ vyakta tām gatā aham ca tvam ca rāja indra ye ca api anye śarīriṇaḥ bindunyāsa ādayaḥ avasthāḥ śukra śoṇita saṃbhavāḥ yāsām eva nipātena kalalam nāma jāyate kalalāt arbuda utpattiḥ peśī ca api arbuda udbhavā peśyāḥ tu aṅga abhinirvṛttiḥ nakha romāṇi ca aṅgataḥ jāyate nāma rūpa tvam strī pumān vā iti liṅgataḥ jāta mātram tu tat rūpam dṛṣṭvā tāmra nakha aṅguli kaumārāt yauvanam ca api sthāviryam ca api yauvanāt kalānām pṛthak arthānām pratibhedaḥ kṣaṇe kṣaṇe avasthāyām avasthāyām dīpasya iva arciṣaḥ gatiḥ kasya idam kasya vā na idam kutas vā idam na vā kutas yathā ādityāt maṇeḥ ca eva vīrudbhyaḥ ca eva pāvakaḥ ātmani eva ātmanā ātmānam yathā tvam anupaśyasi kṛtavān yaḥ mahīpāla kim tasmin mukta lakṣaṇam yasya nā asti samam cakṣuḥ kim tasmin mukta lakṣaṇam tāni tāni anusaṃdṛśya saṅga sthānāni ariṃdama ātmanā ātmani saṃpaśyet kim tasmin mukta lakṣaṇam imāni anyāni sūkṣmāṇi mokṣam āśritya kāni cit catur aṅga pravṛttāni saṅga sthānāni me śṛṇu yaḥ imām pṛthivīm kṛtsnām eka chatrām praśāsti ha gṛhe śayanam api ekam niśāyām yatra līyate śayyā ardham tasya ca api atra strī pūrvam adhitiṣṭhati strīṣu krīḍā vihāreṣu nityam asya asvatantra tā yadā tu ājñāpayati anyān tadā asya uktā svatantra tā śayane ca api anujñātaḥ suptaḥ utthāpyate avaśaḥ vadasva śṛṇu ca api iti vivaśaḥ kāryate paraiḥ abhigamya abhigamya enam yācante satatam narāḥ na ca api utsahate dātum vitta rakṣī mahājanāt kṣaṇena asya upavartante doṣāḥ vairāgya kārakāḥ prājñān śūrān tathā eva āḍhyān eka sthāne api śaṅkate yadā ca ete praduṣyanti rājan ye kīrtitāḥ mayā tadā eva asya bhayam tebhyaḥ jāyate paśya yādṛśam sarvaḥ sve sve gṛhe rājā sarvaḥ sve sve gṛhe gṛhī putrāḥ dārāḥ tathā eva ātmā kośaḥ mitrāṇi saṃcayaḥ paraiḥ sādhāraṇāḥ hi ete taiḥ taiḥ eva asya hetubhiḥ hataḥ deśaḥ puram dagdham pradhānaḥ kuñjaraḥ mṛtaḥ loka sādhāraṇeṣu eṣu mithyājñānena tapyate bahu pratyarthikam rājyam upāste gaṇayan niśāḥ mama idam iti yat ca idam puram rāṣṭram ca manyase balam kośam amātyān ca kasya etāni na vā nṛpa mitra amātyam puram rāṣṭram daṇḍaḥ kośaḥ mahīpatiḥ sapta aṅgaḥ cakrasaṃghātaḥ rājyam iti ucyate nṛpa sapta aṅgasya asya rājyasya tridaṇḍasya iva tiṣṭhataḥ teṣu teṣu hi kāleṣu tat tat aṅgam viśiṣyate sapta aṅgaḥ ca api saṃghātaḥ trayaḥ ca anye nṛpa uttama saṃbhūya daśa vargaḥ ayam bhuṅkte rājyam hi rāja vat sa tuṣyet daśa bhāgena tatas tu anyaḥ daśa avaraiḥ na asti asādhāraṇaḥ rājā na asti rājyam arājakam pṛthivī dakṣiṇā yasya saḥ aśvamedhaḥ na vidyate sā aham etāni karmāṇi rājya duḥkhāni maithila samarthā śataśas vaktum atha vā api sahasraśas na mām evaṃvidhām muktām īdṛśam vaktum arhasi nanu nāma tvayā mokṣaḥ kṛtsnaḥ pañcaśikhāt śrutaḥ sa upāyaḥ sa upaniṣadaḥ sa upāsaṅgaḥ sa niścayaḥ tasya te mukta saṅgasya pāśān ākramya tiṣṭhataḥ chatra ādiṣu viśeṣeṣu katham saṅgaḥ punar nṛpa śrutam te na śrutam manye mithyā vā api śrutam śrutam atha vā śruta saṃkāśam śrutam anyat śrutam tvayā atha api imāsu saṃjñāsu laukikīṣu pratiṣṭhasi abhiṣaṅga avarodhābhyām baddhaḥ tvam prākṛtaḥ mayā niyamaḥ hi eṣa dharmeṣu yatīnām śūnya vāsi tā śūnyam āvāsayantyā ca mayā kim kasya dūṣitam na pāṇibhyām na bāhubhyām pāda ūrubhyām na ca anagha na gātra avayavaiḥ anyaiḥ spṛśāmi tvā narādhipa kule mahati jātena hrīmatā dīrghadarśinā brāhmaṇāḥ guravaḥ ca ime tathā amātyāḥ guru uttamāḥ tat evam anusaṃdṛśya vācya avācyam parīkṣatā strī puṃsoḥ samavāyaḥ ayam tvayā vācyaḥ na saṃsadi yathā puṣkara parṇa stham jalam tad parṇa saṃsthitam yadi vā api a spṛśantyāḥ me sparśam jānāsi kam cana jñānam kṛtam abījam te katham tena iha bhikṣuṇā sa gārhasthyāt cyutaḥ ca tvam mokṣam na avāpya durvidam bhāva abhāva samāyoge jāyate varṇa saṃkaraḥ varṇa āśrama pṛthaktve ca dṛṣṭa arthasya apṛthaktvinaḥ pāṇau kuṇḍam tathā kuṇḍe payaḥ payasi makṣikāḥ āśrita āśraya yogena pṛthaktvena āśrayāḥ vayam na tu kuṇḍe payaḥ bhāvaḥ payaḥ ca api na makṣikāḥ svayam eva āśrayanti ete bhāvāḥ na tu para āśrayam pṛthaktvāt āśramāṇām ca varṇa anyatve tathā eva ca na asmi varṇa uttamā jātyā na vaiśyā na avarā tathā pradhānaḥ nāma rājarṣiḥ vyaktam te śrotram āgataḥ droṇaḥ ca śataśṛṅgaḥ ca vakradvāraḥ ca parvataḥ mama satreṣu pūrveṣām citā maghavatā saha vinītā mokṣa dharmeṣu carāmi ekā muni vratam na asthirā sva pratijñāyām na asamīkṣyapravādinī na a samīkṣya āgatā ca aham tvad sakāśam janādhipa mokṣe te bhāvitām buddhim śrutvā aham kuśala eṣiṇī tava mokṣasya ca api asya jijñāsā artham iha āgatā muktaḥ na mucyate yaḥ ca śāntaḥ yaḥ ca na śāmyati yathā śūnye pura āgāre bhikṣuḥ ekām niśām vaset tathā hi tvad śarīre asmin imām vatsyāmi śarvarīm sā aham āsana dānena vāc ātithyena ca arcitā suptā su śaraṇā prītā śvas gamiṣyāmi maithila śrutvā na adhijagau rājā kim cit anyat atas param yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca katham nirvedam āpannaḥ śukaḥ vaiyāsakiḥ purā bhīṣmaḥ uvāca adhyāpya kṛtsnam svādhyāyam anvaśāt vai pitā sutam kṣudh pipāse ca vāyum ca jaya nityam jita indriyaḥ satyam ārjavam akrodham anasūyām damam tapaḥ ahiṃsām ca ānṛśaṃsyam ca vidhivat paripālaya devatā atithi śeṣeṇa yātrām prāṇasya saṃśraya antaram lipsamāneṣu bālaḥ tvam na avabudhyase gaṇyamāneṣu varṣeṣu kṣīyamāṇe tathā āyuṣi jīvite śiṣyamāṇe ca kim utthāya na dhāvasi pāralaukika kāryeṣu prasuptāḥ bhṛśa nāstikāḥ apathā gacchatām teṣām anuyātā api pīḍyate ye tu tuṣṭāḥ su niyatāḥ satya āgama parāyaṇāḥ dharmyam panthānam ārūḍhāḥ tān upāssva ca pṛccha ca upadhārya matam teṣām vṛddhānām dharma darśinām adyakālikayā buddhyā dūre śvas iti nirbhayāḥ dharma niḥśreṇim āsthāya kim cit kim cit samāruha kośakāra vat ātmānam veṣṭayan na avabudhyase nāstikam bhinna maryādam kūla pātam iva asthiram kāmam krodham ca mṛtyum ca pañca indriya jalām nadīm nāvam dhṛti mayīm kṛtvā janma durgāṇi saṃtara mṛtyunā abhyāhate loke jarayā paripīḍite tiṣṭhantam ca śayānam ca mṛtyuḥ anveṣate yadā nirvṛtim labhase kasmāt akasmāt mṛtyu nāśitaḥ saṃcinvānakam eva enam kāmānām a vitṛptakam vṛkī iva uraṇam āsādya mṛtyuḥ ādāya gacchati andhakāre praveṣṭavye dīpaḥ yatnena dhāryatām saṃpatan deha jālāni kadā cit iha mānuṣe brāhmaṇasya hi dehaḥ ayam na kāma arthāya jāyate avyakta prakṛtiḥ ayam kalā śarīraḥ sūkṣmātmā kṣaṇa truṭiśas nimeṣa romā ṛtvā āsyaḥ sama bala śukla kṛṣṇa netraḥ māṃsa aṅgaḥ dravati vayaḥ hayaḥ narāṇām tam dṛṣṭvā prasṛtam ajasram ugra vegam gacchantam satatam iha a vyapekṣamāṇam ye amī tu pracalita dharma kāma vṛttāḥ krośantaḥ satatam aniṣṭa saṃprayogāḥ kliśyante parigata vedanā śarīrāḥ bahvībhiḥ su bhṛśam adharma vāsanābhiḥ rājā dharma paraḥ sadā śubha goptā samīkṣya su kṛtinām dadhāti lokān śvānaḥ bhīṣaṇa ayaḥ mukhāni vayāṃsi vaḍa gṛdhra kula pakṣiṇām ca saṃghāḥ maryādāḥ niyatāḥ svayaṃbhuvā yaḥ iha imāḥ prabhinatti daśaguṇāḥ manonuga tvāt nivasati bhṛśam asukham pitṛ viṣaya avagāhya sa pāpaḥ yaḥ lubdhaḥ su bhṛśam priya anṛtaḥ ca manuṣyaḥ satata nikṛti vañcanā ratiḥ syāt uṣṇām vaitaraṇīm mahā nadīm avagāḍhaḥ asipatravana bhinna gātraḥ cirasya mṛtyu kārikām anāgatām na budhyase ati pramāthi dāruṇam sukhasya saṃvidhīyatām purā mṛtaḥ praṇīyase yamasya mṛtyu śāsanāt purā vivāti mārutaḥ yamasya yaḥ puraḥsaraḥ kṛta akṛte śubha aśubhe pramāda karma viplute bala aṅga rūpa hāriṇī nidhatsva kevalam nidhim purā vṛkāḥ bhayaṃkarāḥ manuṣya deha gocarāḥ purā hiraṇmayān nagān nirīkṣase adri mūrdhani purā kusaṃgatāni te suhṛd mukhāḥ ca śatravaḥ na mātṛ pitṛ bāndhavāḥ na saṃstutaḥ priyaḥ janaḥ yat eva karma kevalam svayam kṛtam śubha aśubham hiraṇya ratna saṃcayāḥ śubha aśubhena saṃcitāḥ na tasya deha saṃkṣaye bhavanti kārya sādhakāḥ paratragāmikasya te kṛta a kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ na sākṣiḥ ātmanā samaḥ nṛṇām iha asti kaḥ cana prapaśya buddhi cakṣuṣā pradṛśyate hi sarvatas iha agni sūrya vāyavaḥ śarīram āśritāḥ trayaḥ yathāniśeṣu sarvatas spṛśatsu sarva dāriṣu prakāśa gūḍha vṛttiṣu svadharmam eva pālaya yathā apsaraḥ gaṇāḥ phalam sukham mahā ṛṣibhiḥ saha yathā iha yat kṛtam śubham vipāpmabhiḥ kṛtātmabhiḥ tat āpnuvanti mānavāḥ tathā viśuddha yonayaḥ prajāpateḥ salokatām bṛhaspateḥ śatakratoḥ gatāḥ dvis aṣṭa varṣatā dhruvaḥ asi pañcaviṃśakaḥ tathā gatim gamiṣyataḥ kim ātmanā pareṇa vā yat eka pātinām satām bhavati amutra gacchatām bhayeṣu sāṃparāyikam nidhatsva tam mahā nidhim sva darśana anumānataḥ pravarṇitam kuruṣva tat śrutam samartham astu te prakurvataḥ śubhāḥ kriyāḥ nibandhanī rajjuḥ eṣā yā grāme vasataḥ ratiḥ chittvā enām su kṛtaḥ yānti na enām chindanti duṣkṛtaḥ ātmānam anviccha guhām praviṣṭam pitāmahāḥ te kva gatāḥ ca sarve śvas kāryam adya kurvīta pūrvāhṇe ca āparāhṇikam anugamya śmaśāna antam nivartanti iha bāndhavāḥ agnau prakṣipya puruṣam jñātayaḥ suhṛdaḥ tathā nāstikān niranukrośān narān pāpa matau sthitān athā imam darśana upāyam samyak yaḥ vetti mānavaḥ na dehabhede maraṇam vijānatām na ca praṇāśaḥ su anupālite pathi sopāna bhūtam svargasya mānuṣyam prāpya durlabham tathā ātmānam samādadhyāt bhraśyeta na punar yathā yasya nā utkrāmati matiḥ svarga mārga anusāriṇī tam āhuḥ puṇya karmāṇam aśocyam mitra bāndhavaiḥ tapaḥ vaneṣu ye jātāḥ tatra eva nidhanam gatāḥ teṣām alpataraḥ dharmaḥ kāma bhogam a jānatām mātā pitṛ sahasrāṇi putra dāra śatāni ca na teṣām bhavatā kāryam na kāryam tava taiḥ api sva kṛtaiḥ tāni yātāni bhavān ca eva gamiṣyati sva janaḥ tu daridrāṇām jīvatām eva naśyati saṃcinoti aśubham karma kalatra apekṣayā naraḥ paśya tvam chidra bhūtam hi jīva lokam sva karmaṇā tat etat saṃpradṛśya eva karma bhūmim praviśya tām śubhāni ācaritavyāni para lokam abhīpsatā māsa ṛtu saṃjñā parivartakena sūrya agninā rātri diva indhanena sva karma niṣṭhā phala sākṣikeṇa bhūtāni kālaḥ pacati prasahya yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca katham vyāsasya dharma ātmā śukaḥ jajñe mahā tapāḥ kasyām ca utpādayām āsa śukam vyāsaḥ tapodhanaḥ katham ca bālasya sataḥ sūkṣma jñāne gatā matiḥ etat icchāmi aham śrotum vistareṇa mahā dyute na hi me tṛptiḥ asti iha śṛṇvataḥ amṛtam uttamam māhātmyam ātma yogam ca vijñānam ca śukasya ha yathāvat ānupūrvyeṇa tat me brūhi pitāmaha bhīṣmaḥ uvāca ṛṣayaḥ cakrire dharmam yaḥ anūcānaḥ sa naḥ mahān tapaḥ mūlam idam sarvam yat mām pṛcchasi pāṇḍava indriyāṇām prasaṅgena doṣam ṛcchati asaṃśayam śukasya agryām gatim ca eva durvidām akṛtātmabhiḥ meru śṛṅge kila purā karṇikāra vana ayute vijahāra mahādevaḥ bhīmaiḥ bhūta gaṇaiḥ vṛtaḥ śailarājasutā ca eva devī tatra abhavat purā tatra divyam tapaḥ tepe kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ yogena ātmānam āviśya yoga dharma parāyaṇaḥ agneḥ bhūmeḥ apām vāyoḥ antarikṣasya ca abhibho vīryeṇa saṃmitaḥ putraḥ mama bhūyāt iti sma ha saṃkalpena atha saḥ anena duṣprāpeṇa akṛtātmabhiḥ atiṣṭhat māruta āhāraḥ śatam kila samāḥ prabhuḥ ārādhayat mahādevam bahu rūpam umāpatim lokapālāḥ ca lokeśam sādhyāḥ ca vasubhiḥ saha ādityāḥ ca eva rudrāḥ ca divākara niśākarau marutaḥ mārutaḥ ca eva sāgarāḥ saritaḥ tathā viśvāvasuḥ ca gandharvaḥ siddhāḥ ca apsarasām gaṇāḥ tatra rudraḥ mahādevaḥ karṇikāra mayīm śubhām dhārayāṇaḥ srajam bhāti jyotsnām iva niśākaraḥ āsthitaḥ paramam yogam ṛṣiḥ putra artham udyataḥ trayāṇām api lokānām tat adbhutam iva abhavat jaṭāḥ ca tejasā tasya vaiśvānara śikhā upamāḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ hi bhagavān etat ākhyātavān mama sa deva caritāni iha kathayām āsa me sadā tāḥ kṛṣṇasya tapasā tena dīpitāḥ agni varṇāḥ jaṭāḥ tāta prakāśante mahātmanaḥ maheśvaraḥ prasanna ātmā cakāra manasā matim tad bhāva bhāvī tad buddhiḥ tad ātmā tad apāśrayaḥ tejasā āvṛtya lokān trīn yaśaḥ prāpsyati kevalam bhīṣmaḥ uvāca sa labdhvā paramam devāt varam satyavatī sutaḥ araṇīm tu atha saṃgṛhya mamantha agni cikīrṣayā atha rūpam param rājan bibhratīm svena tejasā ghṛtācīm nāma apsarasam apaśyat bhagavān ṛṣiḥ ṛṣiḥ apsarasam dṛṣṭvā sahasā kāma mohitaḥ sā ca kṛtvā tadā vyāsam kāma saṃvigna mānasam śukī bhūtvā mahā rāja ghṛtācī samupāgamat sa tām apsarasam dṛṣṭvā rūpeṇa anyena saṃvṛtām śarīrajena anugataḥ sarva gātra atigena ha sa tu dhairyeṇa mahatā nigṛhṇan hṛcchayam muniḥ na śaśāka niyantum tat vyāsaḥ pravisṛtam manaḥ bhāvi tvāt ca eva bhāvasya ghṛtācyāḥ vapuṣā hṛtaḥ araṇīm mamantha brahmarṣiḥ tasyām jajñe śukaḥ nṛpa śukre nirmathyamāne tu śukaḥ jajñe mahā tapāḥ parama ṛṣiḥ mahā yogī araṇī garbha saṃbhavaḥ tathārūpaḥ śukaḥ jajñe prajvalan iva tejasā tam gaṅgā saritām śreṣṭhā meru pṛṣṭhe janeśvara svarūpiṇī tadā abhyetya snāpayām āsa vāriṇā antarikṣāt ca kauravya daṇḍaḥ kṛṣṇājinam ca ha papāta bhuvi rāja indra śukasya arthe mahātmanaḥ jegīyante sma gandharvāḥ nanṛtuḥ ca apsaraḥ gaṇāḥ hāhā hūhū ca gandharvau tuṣṭuvuḥ śuka saṃbhavam tatra śakra purogāḥ ca lokapālāḥ samāgatāḥ divyāni sarva puṣpāṇi pravavarṣa atra mārutaḥ jaṅgamam sthāvaram ca eva prahṛṣṭam abhavat jagat tam mahātmā svayam prītyā devyā saha mahā dyutiḥ jāta mātram muneḥ putram vidhinā upānayat tadā dadau kamaṇḍalum prītyā deva vāsāṃsi ca abhibho haṃsāḥ ca śatapatrāḥ ca sārasāḥ ca sahasraśas pradakṣiṇam avartanta śukāḥ ca āṣāḥ ca bhārata āraṇeyaḥ tathā divyam prāpya janma mahā dyutiḥ tatra eva uvāsa medhāvī vrata cārī samāhitaḥ utpanna mātram tam vedāḥ sa rahasyāḥ sa saṃgrahāḥ bṛhaspatim tu vavre sa veda vedāṅga bhāṣya vid upādhyāyam mahā rāja dharmam eva anucintayan itihāsam ca kārtsnyena rāja śāstrāṇi ca abhibho gurave dakṣiṇām dattvā samāvṛttaḥ mahā muniḥ ugram tapaḥ samārebhe brahmacārī samāhitaḥ devatānām ṛṣīṇām ca bālye api sa mahā tapāḥ saṃmantraṇīyaḥ mānyaḥ ca jñānena tapasā tathā triṣu gārhasthya mūleṣu mokṣa dharma anudarśinaḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca prāha abhivādya ca gurum śreyaḥ ṛthī vinaya anvitaḥ yathā me manasaḥ śāntiḥ paramā saṃbhavet prabho adhīṣva putra mokṣam vai dharmān ca vividhān api pituḥ niyogāt jagrāha śukaḥ brahma vidām varaḥ yoga śāstram ca nikhilam kāpilam ca eva bhārata sa tam brāhmyā śriyā yuktam brahma tulya parākramam mene putram yadā vyāsaḥ mokṣa vidyā viśāradam sa te vakṣyati mokṣa artham nikhilena viśeṣataḥ praṣṭum dharmasya niṣṭhām vai mokṣasya ca parāyaṇam uktaḥ ca mānuṣeṇa tvam pathā gaccha iti avismitaḥ ārjaveṇa eva gantavyam na sukha anveṣiṇā pathā na anveṣṭavyāḥ viśeṣāḥ tu viśeṣāḥ hi prasaṅginaḥ sa dharma kuśalaḥ rājā mokṣa śāstra viśāradaḥ yājyaḥ mama sa yat brūyāt tat kāryam aviśaṅkayā evam uktaḥ sa dharma ātmā jagāma mithilām muniḥ padbhyām śaktaḥ antarikṣeṇa krāntum bhūmim sa sāgarām sa girīn ca api atikramya nadīḥ tīrtvā sarāṃsi ca bahu vyāla mṛga ākīrṇāḥ vividhāḥ ca aṭavīḥ tathā sa deśān vividhān paśyan cīna hūṇa niṣevitān āryāvartam imam deśam ājagāma mahā muniḥ pattanāni ca ramyāṇi sphītāni nagarāṇi ca ratnāni ca vicitrāṇi śukaḥ paśyan na paśyati udyānāni ca ramyāṇi tathā eva āyatanāni ca saḥ acireṇa eva kālena videhān āsasāda ha pallī ghoṣān samṛddhān ca bahu gokula saṃkulān sphītān ca śāli yavasaiḥ haṃsa sārasa sevitān padminībhiḥ ca śataśas śrīmatībhiḥ alaṃkṛtān hasti aśva ratha saṃkīrṇam nara nārī samākulam ātma ārāmaḥ prasanna ātmā mithilām āsasāda ha tasyāḥ dvāram samāsādya dvārapālaiḥ nivāritaḥ sa rājamārgam āsādya samṛddha jana saṃkulam pārthiva kṣayam āsādya niḥśaṅkaḥ praviveśa ha tatra api dvārapālāḥ tam ugra vācaḥ nyaṣedhayan na ca ātapa adhva saṃtaptaḥ kṣudh pipāsā śrama anvitaḥ pratāmyati glāyati vā na apaiti ca tathā ātapāt teṣām tu dvārapālānām ekaḥ śoka samanvitaḥ madhyaṃgatam iva ādityam dṛṣṭvā śukam avasthitam pūjayitvā yathānyāyam abhivādya kṛtāñjaliḥ prāveśayat tatas kakṣyām dvitīyām rāja veśmanaḥ tatra āsīnaḥ śukaḥ tāta mokṣam eva anucintayan chāyāyām ātape ca eva sama darśī mahā dyutiḥ tam muhūrtāt iva āgamya rājñaḥ mantrī kṛtāñjaliḥ prāveśayat tatas kakṣyām tṛtīyām rāja veśmanaḥ suvibhakta jala ākrīḍam ramyam puṣpita pādapam tat darśayitvā sa śukam mantrī kānanam uttamam arham āsanam ādiśya niścakrāma tatas punar tam cāru veṣāḥ su śroṇyaḥ taruṇyaḥ priya darśanāḥ sūkṣma rakta ambara dharāḥ tapta kāñcana bhūṣaṇāḥ saṃlāpa ullāpa kuśalāḥ nṛtta gīta viśāradāḥ smita pūrva abhibhāṣiṇyaḥ rūpeṇa apsarasām samāḥ kāma upacāra kuśalāḥ bhāva jñāḥ sarva kovidāḥ param pañcāśataḥ nāryaḥ vāramukhyāḥ samādravan pādya ādīni pratigrāhya pūjayā parayā arcya ca su ramyam darśayām āsuḥ ekaikaśyena bhārata krīḍantyaḥ ca hasantyaḥ ca gāyantyaḥ ca eva tāḥ śukam udāra sattvam sattva jñāḥ sarvāḥ paryacaran tadā āraṇeyaḥ tu śuddha ātmā tri saṃdehaḥ tri karma kṛt tasmai śayyā āsanam divyam vara arham ratna bhūṣitam spardhya āstaraṇa saṃstīrṇam daduḥ tāḥ parama striyaḥ pāda śaucam tu kṛtvā eva śukaḥ saṃdhyām upāsya ca niṣasāda āsane puṇye tam eva artham vicintayan pūrvarātre tu tatra asau bhūtvā dhyāna parāyaṇaḥ madhyarātre yathānyāyam nidrām āhārayat prabhuḥ tatas muhūrtāt utthāya kṛtvā śaucam anantaram strībhiḥ parivṛtaḥ dhīmān dhyānam eva anvapadyata anena vidhinā kārṣṇiḥ tat ahar śeṣam acyutaḥ tām ca rātrim nṛpa kule vartayām āsa bhārata bhīṣmaḥ uvāca puras purohitam kṛtvā sarvāṇi antaḥpurāṇi ca śirasā ca arghyam ādāya guru putram samabhyagāt purodhasā saṃgṛhītam hastena ālabhya pārthivaḥ tatra upaviṣṭam tam kārṣṇim śāstrataḥ pratyapūjayat sa ca tām mantravat pūjām pratyagṛhṇāt yathāvidhi pratigṛhya ca tām pūjām janakāt dvijasattamaḥ gām ca eva samanujñāya rājānam anumānya ca paryapṛcchat mahā tejāḥ rājñaḥ kuśalam avyayam anāmayam ca rāja indra śukaḥ sa anucarasya ha anujñātaḥ sa tena atha niṣasāda saha anugaḥ udāra sattva abhijanaḥ bhūmau rājā kṛtāñjaliḥ kuśalam ca avyayam ca eva pṛṣṭvā vaiyāsakim nṛpaḥ śukaḥ uvāca tatra gacchasva vai tūrṇam yadi te hṛdi saṃśayaḥ saḥ aham pituḥ niyogāt tvām upapraṣṭum iha āgataḥ tat me dharma bhṛtām śreṣṭha yathāvat vaktum arhasi kim kāryam brāhmaṇena iha mokṣa arthaḥ ca kim ātmakaḥ katham ca mokṣaḥ kartavyaḥ jñānena tapasā api vā yat kāryam brāhmaṇena iha janma prabhṛti tat śṛṇu devatānām pitṝṇām ca api anṛṇaḥ ca anasūyakaḥ tān eva agnīn yathāśāstram arcayan atithi priyaḥ nirdvaṃdvaḥ vīta rāga ātmā brahma āśrama pade vaset śukaḥ uvāca utpanne jñāna vijñāne pratyakṣe hṛdi śāśvate kim avaśyam nivastavyam āśrameṣu vaneṣu ca na vinā jñāna vijñānam mokṣasya adhigamaḥ bhavet na vinā guru saṃbandham jñānasya adhigamaḥ smṛtaḥ ācāryaḥ plāvitā tasya jñānam plavaḥ iha ucyate vijñāya kṛtakṛtyaḥ tu tīrṇaḥ tat ubhayam tyajet an ucchedāya lokānām an ucchedāya karmaṇām pūrvaiḥ ācaritaḥ dharmaḥ cāturāśramya saṃkathaḥ kṛtvā śubha aśubham karma mokṣaḥ nāma iha labhyate kāraṇaiḥ ca ayam bahu saṃsāra yoniṣu āsādayati śuddha ātmā mokṣam vai prathama āśrame tam āsādya tu muktasya dṛṣṭa arthasya vipaścitaḥ rājasān tāmasān ca eva nityam doṣān vivarjayet sāttvikam mārgam āsthāya paśyet ātmānam ātmanā sarva bhūteṣu ca ātmānam sarva bhūtāni ca ātmani vihāya deham nirmuktaḥ nirdvaṃdvaḥ praśamam gataḥ atra gāthāḥ purā gītāḥ śṛṇu rājñā yayātinā dhāryante yāḥ dvijaiḥ tāta mokṣa śāstra viśāradaiḥ svayam ca śakyam tat draṣṭum su samāhita cetasā yadā bhāvam na kurute sarva bhūteṣu pāpakam karmaṇā manasā vācā brahma saṃpadyate tadā saṃyojya tapasā ātmānam īrṣyām utsṛjya mohinīm yadā śravye ca dṛśye ca sarva bhūteṣu ca api ayam śītam uṣṇam tathā eva artham anartham priyam apriyam jīvitam maraṇam ca eva brahma saṃpadyate tadā prasārya iha yathā aṅgāni kūrmaḥ saṃharate punar tathā indriyāṇi manasā saṃyantavyāni bhikṣuṇā tamaḥ parigatam veśma yathā dīpena dṛśyate tathā buddhi pradīpena śakyaḥ ātmā nirīkṣitum brahmarṣe viditaḥ ca asi viṣaya antam upāgataḥ jñānam divyam mama api idam tena asi viditaḥ mama bālyāt vā saṃśayāt vā api bhayāt vā api a vimokṣa jāt utpanne ca api vijñāne na adhigacchati tām gatim vimucya hṛdaya granthīn āsādayati tām gatim bhavān ca utpanna vijñānaḥ sthira buddhiḥ a lolupaḥ na asti te sukha duḥkheṣu viśeṣaḥ na asti lolupā na autsukyam nṛtta gīteṣu na rāgaḥ upajāyate paśyāmi tvām mahābhāga tulya loṣṭa aśma kāñcanam aham ca tvā anupaśyāmi ye ca api anye manīṣiṇaḥ āsthitam paramam mārgam akṣayam tam anāmayam yat phalam brāhmaṇasya iha mokṣa arthaḥ ca yat ātmakaḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca etat śrutvā tu vacanam kṛtātmā kṛta niścayaḥ ātmanā ātmānam āsthāya dṛṣṭvā ca ātmānam ātmanā kṛta kāryaḥ sukhī śāntaḥ tūṣṇīm prāyāt udak mukhaḥ śaiśiram girim uddiśya sadharmā mātariśvanaḥ himavantam iyāt draṣṭum siddha cāraṇa sevitam tam apsaraḥ gaṇa ākīrṇam gīta svana nināditam kiṃnarāṇām samūhaiḥ ca bhṛṅgarājaiḥ tathā eva ca madgubhiḥ khañjarīṭaiḥ ca vicitraiḥ jīvajīvakaiḥ citra varṇaiḥ mayūraiḥ ca kekā śata virājitaiḥ rājahaṃsa samūhaiḥ ca hṛṣṭaiḥ parabhṛtaiḥ tathā catvāraḥ lokapālāḥ ca devāḥ sa ṛṣi gaṇāḥ tathā viṣṇunā yatra putra arthe tapaḥ taptam mahātmanā yatra eva ca kumāreṇa bālye kṣiptāḥ divaukasaḥ yaḥ brahmaṇyaḥ dvitīyaḥ asti triṣu lokeṣu vīryavān apaśyat bhagavān viṣṇuḥ kṣiptam sa asura rākṣasam sa nā amṛṣyata tam kṣepam avaikṣata ca pāvakim sa prahasya viśuddha ātmā śaktim prajvalitām tadā kampayām āsa savyena pāṇinā puruṣottamaḥ śaktyām tu kampamānāyām viṣṇunā balinā tadā medinī kampitā sarvā sa śaila vana kānanā śaktena api samuddhartum kampitā sā na tu uddhṛtā rakṣatā skanda rājasya dharṣaṇām prabhaviṣṇunā paśya vīryam kumārasya na etat anyaḥ kariṣyati saḥ amṛṣyamāṇaḥ tat vākyam samuddharaṇa niścitaḥ nādam mahāntam muktvā sa mūrchitaḥ giri mūrdhani vihvalaḥ prāpatat bhūmau hiraṇyakaśipoḥ sutaḥ yatra uttarām diśam gatvā śailarājasya pārśvatas pāvakena parikṣiptaḥ dīpyatā tasya ca āśramaḥ ādityabandhanam nāma durdharṣam akṛtātmabhiḥ na tatra śakyate gantum yakṣa rākṣasa dānavaiḥ daśa yojana vistāram agni jvālā samāvṛtam bhagavān pāvakaḥ tatra svayam tiṣṭhati vīryavān divyam varṣa sahasram hi pādena ekena tiṣṭhataḥ devān saṃtāpayan tatra mahādevaḥ dhṛta vrataḥ aindrīm tu diśam āsthāya śailarājasya dhīmataḥ vivikte parvata taṭe pārāśaryaḥ mahā tapāḥ vedān adhyāpayām āsa vyāsaḥ śiṣyān mahā tapāḥ sumantum ca mahābhāgam vaiśaṃpāyanam eva ca jaiminim ca mahā prājñam pailam ca api tapasvinam ebhiḥ śiṣyaiḥ parivṛtaḥ vyāsaḥ āste mahā tapāḥ tatra āśrama padam puṇyam dadarśa pituḥ uttamam āraṇeyaḥ viśuddha ātmā nabhasi iva divākaraḥ a sajjamānam vṛkṣeṣu śaileṣu viṣameṣu ca yoga yuktam mahātmānam yathā bāṇam guṇa cyutam saḥ abhigamya pituḥ pādau agṛhṇāt araṇī sutaḥ yathopajoṣam taiḥ ca api samāgacchan mahā muniḥ śukaḥ janaka rājena saṃvādam prīta mānasaḥ evam adhyāpayan śiṣyān vyāsaḥ putram ca vīryavān uvāsa himavat pṛṣṭhe pārāśaryaḥ mahā muniḥ tatas kadā cit śiṣyāḥ tam parivārya avatasthire veda adhyayana saṃpannāḥ śānta ātmānaḥ jita indriyāḥ vedeṣu niṣṭhām saṃprāpya sa aṅgeṣu ati tapasvinaḥ athā ūcuḥ te tadā vyāsam śiṣyāḥ prāñjalayaḥ gurum mahatā śreyasā yuktāḥ yaśasā ca sma vardhitāḥ ekam tu idānīm icchāmaḥ guruṇā anugraham kṛtam iti teṣām vacaḥ śrutvā brahmarṣiḥ tān uvāca ha ucyatām iti tat vatsāḥ yat vaḥ kāryam priyam mayā etat vākyam guroḥ śrutvā śiṣyāḥ te hṛṣṭa mānasāḥ punar prāñjalayaḥ bhūtvā praṇamya śirasā gurum kāṅkṣāmaḥ tu vayam sarve varam dattam mahā ṛṣiṇā ṣaṣṭhaḥ śiṣyaḥ na te khyātim gacchet atra prasīda naḥ catvāraḥ te vayam śiṣyāḥ guru putraḥ ca pañcamaḥ iha vedāḥ pratiṣṭheran eṣa naḥ kāṅkṣitaḥ varaḥ śiṣyāṇām vacanam śrutvā vyāsaḥ veda artha tattva vid parāśara ātmajaḥ dhīmān para loka artha cintakaḥ uvāca śiṣyān dharma ātmā dharmyam naiḥśreyasam vacaḥ brāhmaṇāya sadā deyam brahma śuśrūṣave bhavet na a śiṣye saṃpradātavyaḥ na avrate na akṛtātmani ete śiṣya guṇāḥ sarve vijñātavyāḥ yathārthataḥ na aparīkṣita cāritre vidyā deyā katham cana yathā hi kanakam śuddham tāpa cheda nigharṣaṇaiḥ parīkṣeta tathā śiṣyān īkṣet kula guṇa ādibhiḥ na niyojyāḥ ca vaḥ śiṣyāḥ aniyoge mahā bhaye yathāmati yathāpāṭham tathā vidyā phaliṣyati śrāvayet caturaḥ varṇān kṛtvā brāhmaṇam agratas vedasya adhyayanam hi idam tat ca kāryam mahat smṛtam stuti artham iha devānām vedāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ svayaṃbhuvā yaḥ nirvadeta saṃmohāt brāhmaṇam vedapāragam saḥ apadhyānāt brāhmaṇasya parābhūyāt asaṃśayam yaḥ ca adharmeṇa vibrūyāt yaḥ ca adharmeṇa pṛcchati etat vaḥ sarvam ākhyātam svādhyāyasya vidhim prati upakuryāt ca śiṣyāṇām etat ca hṛdi vaḥ bhavet bhīṣmaḥ uvāca etat śrutvā guroḥ vākyam vyāsa śiṣyāḥ mahā ojasaḥ anyonyam hṛṣṭa manasaḥ pariṣasvajire tadā uktāḥ smaḥ yat bhagavatā tadātva āyati saṃhitam tat naḥ manasi saṃrūḍham kariṣyāmaḥ tathā ca tat vijñāpayanti sma gurum punar vākya viśāradāḥ śailāt asmāt mahīm gantum kāṅkṣitam naḥ mahā mune śiṣyāṇām vacanam śrutvā parāśara sutaḥ prabhuḥ kṣitim vā deva lokam vā gamyatām yadi rocate te anujñātāḥ tatas sarve guruṇā satya vādinā jagmuḥ pradakṣiṇam kṛtvā vyāsam mūrdhnā abhivādya ca saṃyājayantaḥ viprān ca rājanyān ca viśaḥ tathā pūjyamānāḥ dvijaiḥ nityam modamānāḥ gṛhe ratāḥ yājana adhyāpana ratāḥ śrīmantaḥ loka viśrutāḥ avatīrṇeṣu śiṣyeṣu vyāsaḥ putra sahāyavān tūṣṇīm dhyāna paraḥ dhīmān ekānte samupāviśat tam dadarśa āśrama pade nāradaḥ su mahā tapāḥ athā enam abravīt kāle madhura akṣarayā girā ekaḥ dhyāna paraḥ tūṣṇīm kim āsse cintayan iva na bhrājate yathāpūrvam niṣādānām iva ālayaḥ deva ṛṣi gaṇa juṣṭaḥ api veda dhvani nirākṛtaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca hi devāḥ ca gandharvāḥ ca mahā ojasaḥ vimuktāḥ brahma ghoṣeṇa na bhrājante yathā purā nāradasya vacaḥ śrutvā kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ abravīt mahā ṛṣe yat tvayā proktam veda vāda vicakṣaṇa sarva jñaḥ sarva darśī ca sarvatra ca kutūhalī tat ājñāpaya viprarṣe brūhi kim karavāṇi te yat mayā samanuṣṭheyam brahmarṣe tat udāhara viyuktasya iha śiṣyaiḥ me na ati hṛṣṭam idam manaḥ nāradaḥ uvāca an āmnāya malāḥ vedāḥ brāhmaṇasya a vratam malam malam pṛthivyāḥ vāhīkāḥ strīṇām kautūhalam malam bhavān vedān sārdham putreṇa dhīmatā bhīṣmaḥ uvāca tathā iti uvāca saṃhṛṣṭaḥ veda abhyāse dṛḍha vrataḥ svareṇa uccais sa śaikṣeṇa lokān āpūrayan iva ākhyātum arhati bhavān vāyoḥ sarvam viceṣṭitam śukasya etat vacaḥ śrutvā vyāsaḥ parama vismitaḥ ādarśe svām iva chāyām paśyasi ātmānam ātmanā deva yāna caraḥ viṣṇoḥ pitṛ yānaḥ ca tāmasaḥ pṛthivyām antarikṣe ca yatra saṃvānti vāyavaḥ sapta ete vāyu mārgāḥ vai tān nibodha anupūrvaśas tatra deva gaṇāḥ sādhyāḥ samabhūvan mahā balāḥ teṣām api abhavat putraḥ samānaḥ nāma durjayaḥ apānaḥ ca tatas jñeyaḥ prāṇaḥ ca api tatas param anapatyaḥ abhavat prāṇaḥ durdharṣaḥ śatru tāpanaḥ pṛthak karmāṇi teṣām tu pravakṣyāmi yathātatham prāṇinām sarvatas vāyuḥ ceṣṭāḥ vartayate pṛthak prāṇanāt ca eva bhūtānām prāṇaḥ iti abhidhīyate prerayati abhra saṃghātān dhūma jān ca ūṣma jān ca yaḥ āvahaḥ nāma saṃvāti dvitīyaḥ śvasanaḥ nadan udayam jyotiṣām śaśvat soma ādīnām karoti yaḥ antar deheṣu ca udānam yam vadanti mahā ṛṣayaḥ uddhṛtya ādadate ca apaḥ jīmūtebhyaḥ ambare anilaḥ udvahaḥ nāma varṣiṣṭhaḥ tritīyaḥ sa sadāgatiḥ samuhyamānāḥ bahudhā yena nīlāḥ pṛthak ghanāḥ varṣa mokṣa kṛta ārambhāḥ te bhavanti ghana aghanāḥ saṃhatāḥ yena ca āviddhāḥ bhavanti nadatām nadāḥ rakṣaṇa arthāya saṃbhūtāḥ megha tvam upayānti ca yaḥ asau vahati devānām vimānāni vihāyasā caturthaḥ saṃvahaḥ nāma vāyuḥ sa giri mardanaḥ yena vegavatā rugṇāḥ rūkṣeṇa ārujatā rasān vāyunā vihatāḥ meghāḥ na bhavanti balāhakāḥ dāruṇa utpāta saṃcāraḥ nabhasaḥ stanayitnumān pañcamaḥ sa mahā vegaḥ vivahaḥ nāma mārutaḥ puṇyam ca ākāśagaṅgāyāḥ toyam viṣṭabhya tiṣṭhati ṣaṣṭhaḥ parivahaḥ nāma sa vāyuḥ javatām varaḥ sarva prāṇabhṛtām prāṇān yaḥ antakāle nirasyati samyak anvīkṣatām buddhyā śāntayā adhyātma nityayā dhyāna abhyāsa abhirāmāṇām yaḥ amṛta tvāya kalpate yam samāsādya vegena diśām antam prapedire dakṣasya daśa putrāṇām sahasrāṇi prajāpateḥ yena sṛṣṭaḥ parābhūtaḥ yāti eva na nivartate evam ete aditeḥ putrāḥ mārutāḥ parama adbhutāḥ an āramantaḥ saṃvānti sarva gāḥ sarva dhāriṇaḥ kampitaḥ sahasā tena viṣṇoḥ niḥśvāsa vātaḥ ayam yadā vega samīritaḥ vāyoḥ vāyu bhayam hi uktam brahma tat pīḍitam bhavet etāvat uktvā vacanam parāśara sutaḥ prabhuḥ uktvā putram adhīṣva iti vyomagaṅgām ayāt tadā bhīṣmaḥ uvāca śukam svādhyāya niratam veda arthān vaktum īpsitān deva ṛṣim tu śukaḥ dṛṣṭvā nāradam samupasthitam nāradaḥ athā bravīt prītaḥ brūhi brahma vidām vara kena tvām śreyasā tāta yojayāmi iti hṛṣṭa vat nāradasya vacaḥ śrutvā śukaḥ provāca bhārata nāradaḥ uvāca tattvam jijñāsatām pūrvam ṛṣīṇām bhāvitātmanām na asti vidyā samam cakṣuḥ na asti vidyā samam tapaḥ na asti rāga samam duḥkham na asti tyāga samam sukham nivṛttiḥ karmaṇaḥ pāpāt satatam puṇya śīla tā sat vṛttiḥ samudācāraḥ śreyaḥ etat anuttamam na alam sa duḥkha mokṣāya saṅgaḥ vai duḥkha lakṣaṇam moha jāla āvṛtaḥ duḥkham iha ca amutra ca aśnute kāryaḥ śreyaḥ arthinā tau hi śreyaḥ ghāta artham udyatau vidyām māna avamānābhyām ātmānam tu pramādataḥ ānṛśaṃsyam paraḥ dharmaḥ kṣamā ca paramam balam ātma jñānam param jñānam na satyāt vidyate param sarva ārambha phala tyāgī nirāśīḥ niṣparigrahaḥ asajjamānaḥ śānta ātmā nirvikāraḥ samāhitaḥ a darśanam a saṃsparśaḥ tathā a saṃbhāṣaṇam sadā na hiṃsyāt sarva bhūtāni maitrāyaṇa gataḥ caret ākiṃcanyam su saṃtoṣaḥ nirāśīṣṭvam acāpalam etat āhuḥ param śreyaḥ ātma jñasya jita ātmanaḥ aśokam sthānam ātiṣṭhe iha ca amutra ca abhayam nirāmiṣāḥ na śocanti tyaja iha āmiṣam ātmanaḥ parityajya āmiṣam saumya duḥkha tāpāt vimokṣyase a jitam jetu kāmena bhāvyam saṅgeṣu a saṅginā guṇa saṅgeṣu anāsaktaḥ eka caryā rataḥ sadā dvaṃdva ārāmeṣu bhūteṣu yaḥ ekaḥ ramate muniḥ viddhi prajñāna tṛptam tam jñāna tṛptaḥ na śocati saṃveṣṭyamānam bahubhiḥ moha tantubhiḥ ātma jaiḥ kośakāra vat ātmānam veṣṭayan na avabudhyase putra dāra kuṭumbeṣu saktāḥ sīdanti jantavaḥ saraḥ paṅka arṇave magnāḥ jīrṇāḥ vana gajāḥ iva mahā jāla samākṛṣṭān sthale matsyān iva uddhṛtān sneha jāla samākṛṣṭān paśya jantūn su duḥkhitān kuṭumbam putra dāram ca śarīram dravya saṃcayāḥ pārakyam adhruvam sarvam kim svam sukṛta duṣkṛtam tamaḥ kāntāram adhvānam katham ekaḥ gamiṣyasi na hi tvā prasthitam kaḥ cit pṛṣṭhatas anugamiṣyati sukṛtam duṣkṛtam ca tvā yāsyantam anuyāsyati nibandhanī rajjuḥ eṣā yā grāme vasataḥ ratiḥ chittvā enām su kṛtaḥ yānti na enām chindanti duṣkṛtaḥ rūpa kūlām manaḥ srotām sparśa dvīpām rasa āvahām gandha paṅkām śabda jalām svarga mārga durāvahām kṣamā aritrām satya mayīm dharma sthairya vaṭākarām tyāga vāta adhva gām śīghrām buddhi nāvā nadīm taret asthi sthūṇam snāyu yutam māṃsa śoṇita lepanam carma avanaddham durgandhi pūrṇam mūtra purīṣayoḥ jarā śoka samāviṣṭam roga āyatanam āturam rajasvalam anityam ca bhūtāvāsam samutsṛja mahābhūta ātmakam sarvam mahat yat parama aṇu yat iti eṣa saptadaśakaḥ rāśiḥ avyakta saṃjñakaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ iti eṣa vyakta avyakta mayaḥ guṇaḥ trivargaḥ atra sukham duḥkham jīvitam maraṇam tathā pārāśarya iha boddhavyam jñānānām yat ca kim cana loke vitatam ātmānam lokam ca ātmani paśyati parāvara dṛśaḥ śaktiḥ jñāna velām na paśyati paśyataḥ sarva bhūtāni sarva avasthāsu sarvadā jñānena vividhān kleśān ativṛttasya moha jān akartāram amūrtam ca bhagavān āha tīrtha vid ajasram eva moha ārtaḥ duḥkheṣu sukha saṃjñitaḥ tatas nivṛttaḥ bandhāt svāt karmaṇām udayāt iha saṃprāptāḥ bahavaḥ siddhim api abādhām sukha udayām nāradaḥ uvāca aśokam śoka nāśa artham śāstram śānti karam śivam śoka sthāna sahasrāṇi bhaya sthāna śatāni ca divase divase mūḍham āviśanti na paṇḍitam tasmāt aniṣṭa nāśa artham itihāsam nibodha me tiṣṭhate ced vaśe buddhiḥ labhate śoka nāśanam dravyeṣu samatīteṣu ye guṇāḥ tān na cintayet aniṣṭa vat hitam paśyet tathā kṣipram virajyate mṛtam vā yadi vā naṣṭam yaḥ atītam anuśocati na aśru kurvanti ye buddhyā dṛṣṭvā lokeṣu saṃtatim duḥkha upaghāte śārīre mānase vā api upasthite prajñayā mānasam duḥkham hanyāt śārīram auṣadhaiḥ etat vijñāna sāmarthyam na bālaiḥ sama tām iyāt anityam yauvanam rūpam jīvitam dravya saṃcayaḥ ārogyam priya saṃvāsaḥ gṛdhyet tatra na paṇḍitaḥ sukhāt bahutaram duḥkham jīvite na atra saṃśayaḥ abhyeti brahma saḥ atyantam na tam śocanti paṇḍitāḥ duḥkhena ca adhigamyante nāśam eṣām na cintayet anyām anyām dhana avasthām prāpya vaiśeṣikīm narāḥ atṛptāḥ yānti vidhvaṃsam saṃtoṣam yānti paṇḍitāḥ sarve kṣaya antāḥ nicayāḥ patana antāḥ samucchrayāḥ saṃyogāḥ viprayoga antāḥ maraṇa antam hi jīvitam antaḥ nā asti pipāsāyāḥ tuṣṭiḥ tu paramam sukham tasmāt saṃtoṣam eva iha dhanam paśyanti paṇḍitāḥ bhūteṣu abhāvam saṃcintya ye buddhvā tamasaḥ param na śocanti gata adhvānaḥ paśyantaḥ paramām gatim saṃcinvānakam eva enam kāmānām a vitṛptakam vyāghraḥ paśum iva āsādya mṛtyuḥ ādāya gacchati atha api upāyam saṃpaśyet duḥkhasya parimokṣaṇe prāk saṃprayogāt bhūtānām na asti duḥkham anāmayam dhṛtyā śiśna udaram rakṣet pāṇi pādam ca cakṣuṣā cakṣuḥ śrotre ca manasā manaḥ vācam ca vidyayā praṇayam pratisaṃhṛtya saṃstuteṣu itareṣu ca adhyātma ratiḥ āsīnaḥ nirapekṣaḥ nirāmiṣaḥ nāradaḥ uvāca na enam prajñā su nītam vā trāyate na api pauruṣam svabhāvāt yatnam ātiṣṭhet yatnavān na avasīdati rujanti hi śarīrāṇi rogāḥ śārīra mānasāḥ sāyakāḥ iva tīkṣṇa agrāḥ prayuktāḥ dṛḍha dhanvibhiḥ avaśasya vināśāya śarīram apakṛṣyate āyuḥ ādāya martyānām rātri ahāni punar punar vyatyayaḥ hi ayam atyantam pakṣayoḥ śukla kṛṣṇayoḥ jātam martyam jarayati nimeṣam na avatiṣṭhate a dṛṣṭa pūrvān ādāya bhāvān a pariśaṅkitān iṣṭa aniṣṭān manuṣyāṇām astam gacchanti rātrayaḥ yaḥ yam icchet yathākāmam kāmānām tat tat āpnuyāt yadi syāt na para adhīnam puruṣasya kriyā phalam saṃyatāḥ ca hi dakṣāḥ ca matimantaḥ ca mānavāḥ dṛśyante niṣphalāḥ santaḥ prahīṇāḥ ca sva karmabhiḥ apare bāliśāḥ santaḥ nirguṇāḥ puruṣa adhamāḥ āśīrbhiḥ api a saṃyuktāḥ dṛśyante sarva kāminaḥ bhūtānām aparaḥ kaḥ cit hiṃsāyām satata utthitaḥ vañcanāyām ca lokasya sa sukheṣu eva jīryate a ceṣṭamānam āsīnam śrīḥ kam cit upatiṣṭhati aparādham samācakṣva puruṣasya svabhāvataḥ keṣām cit putra kāmānām anusaṃtānam icchatām siddhau prayatamānānām na eva aṇḍam upajāyate garbhāt ca udvijamānānām kruddhāt āśīviṣāt iva āyuṣmān jāyate putraḥ katham pretaḥ pitā eva saḥ devān iṣṭvā tapaḥ taptvā kṛpaṇaiḥ putra gṛddhibhiḥ daśa māsān paridhṛtāḥ jāyante kula pāṃsanāḥ apare dhana dhānyāni bhogān ca pitṛ saṃcitān śīrṇam para śarīreṇa nicchavīkam śarīriṇam prāṇinām prāṇa saṃrodhe māṃsa śleṣma viceṣṭitam vinaśyantam vināśa ante nāvi nāvam iva āhitam anna pānāni jīryante yatra bhakṣāḥ ca bhakṣitāḥ garbha mūtra purīṣāṇām svabhāva niyatā gatiḥ dhāraṇe vā visarge vā na kartuḥ vidyate vaśaḥ sravanti hi udarāt garbhāḥ jāyamānāḥ tathā apare āgamena saha anyeṣām vināśaḥ upapadyate śatasya sahajātasya saptamīm daśamīm daśām prāpnuvanti tatas pañca na bhavanti śata āyuṣaḥ na abhyutthāne manuṣyāṇām yogāḥ syuḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ vyādhibhiḥ ca vimathyante vyālaiḥ kṣudra mṛgāḥ iva vyādhibhiḥ bhakṣyamāṇānām tyajatām vipulam dhanam vedanām na apakarṣanti yatamānāḥ cikitsakāḥ te ca api nipuṇāḥ vaidyāḥ kuśalāḥ saṃbhṛta auṣadhāḥ vyādhibhiḥ parikṛṣyante mṛgāḥ vyādhaiḥ iva arditāḥ te pibantaḥ kaṣāyān ca sarpīṃṣi vividhāni ca dṛśyante jarayā bhagnāḥ nāgāḥ nāgaiḥ iva uttamaiḥ ke vā bhuvi cikitsante roga ārtān mṛga pakṣiṇaḥ śvāpadāni daridrān ca prāyas na ārtāḥ bhavanti te ghorān api durādharṣān nṛpatīn ugra tejasaḥ ākramya rogaḥ ādatte paśūn paśu pacaḥ yathā srotasā sahasā kṣiptam hriyamāṇam balīyasā svabhāvāḥ vyativartante ye niyuktāḥ śarīriṣu apramattāḥ śaṭhāḥ krūrāḥ vikrāntāḥ paryupāsate kleśāḥ pratinivartante keṣām cit a samīkṣitāḥ vahanti śibikām anye yānti anye śibikā gatāḥ sarveṣām ṛddhi kāmānām anye ratha puraḥsarāḥ manujāḥ ca śata strīkāḥ śataśas vidhavāḥ striyaḥ dvaṃdva ārāmeṣu bhūteṣu gacchanti ekaikaśas narāḥ yena devāḥ parityajya martya lokam divam gatāḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca nāradasya vacaḥ śrutvā śukaḥ parama buddhimān putra dāraiḥ mahān kleśaḥ vidyā āmnāye mahān śramaḥ kim nu syāt śāśvatam sthānam alpa kleśam mahā udayam tatas muhūrtam saṃcintya niścitām gatim ātmanaḥ parāvara jñaḥ dharmasya parām naiḥśreyasīm gatim katham tu aham asaṃkliṣṭaḥ gaccheyam paramām gatim na āvarteyam yathā bhūyas yoni saṃsāra sāgare param bhāvam hi kāṅkṣāmi yatra na āvartate punar tatra yāsyāmi yatra ātmā śamam me adhigamiṣyati akṣayaḥ ca avyayaḥ ca eva yatra sthāsyāmi śāśvataḥ na tu yogam ṛte śakyā prāptum sā paramā gatiḥ vāyu bhūtaḥ pravekṣyāmi tejaḥ rāśim divākaram na hi eṣa kṣayam āpnoti somaḥ sura gaṇaiḥ yathā kṣīyate hi sadā somaḥ punar ca eva abhipūryate raviḥ tu saṃtāpayati lokān raśmibhiḥ ulbaṇaiḥ atra vatsyāmi durdharṣaḥ niḥsaṅgena antarātmanā ṛṣibhiḥ saha yāsyāmi sauram tejaḥ ati duḥsaham āpṛcchāmi nagān nāgān girīn urvīm diśaḥ divam deva dānava gandharvān piśāca uraga rākṣasān lokeṣu sarva bhūtāni pravekṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ paśyantu yoga vīryam me sarve devāḥ saha ṛṣibhiḥ athā anujñāpya tam ṛṣim nāradam loka viśrutam tasmāt anujñām saṃprāpya jagāma pitaram prati saḥ abhivādya mahātmānam ṛṣim dvaipāyanam munim śukaḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya kṛṣṇam āpṛṣṭavān muniḥ śrutvā ṛṣiḥ tat vacanam śukasya bho bhoḥ putra sthīyatām tāvat adya yāvat cakṣuḥ prīṇayāmi tvad artham nirapekṣaḥ śukaḥ bhūtvā niḥsnehaḥ mukta bandhanaḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca giri pṛṣṭham samāruhya sutaḥ vyāsasya bhārata same deśe vivikte ca niḥśalāke upāviśat dhārayām āsa ca ātmānam yathāśāstram mahā muniḥ pādāt prabhṛti gātreṣu krameṇa krama yoga vid pāṇi pādam samādhāya vinīta vat upāviśat na tatra pakṣi saṃghātaḥ na śabdaḥ na api darśanam sa dadarśa tadā ātmānam sarva saṅga viniḥsṛtam prajahāsa tatas hāsam śukaḥ saṃprekṣya bhāskaram mahā yogi īśvaraḥ bhūtvā saḥ atyakrāmat vihāyasam tatas pradakṣiṇam kṛtvā devarṣim nāradam tadā nivedayām āsa tadā svam yogam parama ṛṣaye tvad prasādāt gamiṣyāmi gatim iṣṭām mahā dyute nāradena abhyanujñātaḥ tatas dvaipāyana ātmajaḥ abhivādya punar yogam āsthāya ākāśam āviśat kailāsa pṛṣṭhāt utpatya sa papāta divam tadā dadṛśuḥ sarva bhūtāni manaḥ māruta raṃhasam dadṛśuḥ sarva bhūtāni jaṅgamāni itarāṇi ca yathāśakti yathānyāyam pūjayām cakrire tadā tam dṛṣṭvā vismitāḥ sarve gandharva apsarasām gaṇāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca eva saṃsiddhāḥ param vismayam āgatāḥ antarikṣa caraḥ kaḥ ayam tapasā siddhim āgataḥ tatas parama dhīra ātmā triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ bhāskaram samudīkṣan sa prāc mukhaḥ vāgyataḥ agamat śabdena ākāśam akhilam pūrayan iva sarvatas tam āpatantam sahasā dṛṣṭvā sarva apsaraḥ gaṇāḥ saṃbhrānta manasaḥ rājan āsan parama vismitāḥ pañcacūḍā prabhṛtayaḥ bhṛśam utphulla locanāḥ pitṛ śuśrūṣayā siddhim saṃprāptaḥ ayam anuttamām pitṛ bhaktaḥ dṛḍha tapāḥ pituḥ su dayitaḥ sutaḥ urvaśyāḥ vacanam śrutvā śukaḥ parama dharma vid udaikṣata diśaḥ sarvāḥ vacane gata mānasaḥ saḥ antarikṣam mahīm ca eva sa śaila vana kānanām ālokayām āsa tadā sarāṃsi saritaḥ tathā kṛta añjali puṭāḥ sarvāḥ nirīkṣante sma devatāḥ abravīt tāḥ tadā vākyam śukaḥ parama dharma vid pitā yadi anugacchet mām krośamānaḥ śuka iti vai śukasya vacanam śrutvā diśaḥ sa vana kānanāḥ samudrāḥ saritaḥ śailāḥ pratyūcuḥ tam samantataḥ yathā ājñāpayase vipra bāḍham evam bhaviṣyati ṛṣeḥ vyāharataḥ vākyam prativakṣyāmahe vayam bhīṣmaḥ uvāca iti evam uktvā vacanam brahmarṣiḥ su mahā tapāḥ prātiṣṭhata śukaḥ siddhim hitvā lokān caturvidhān tamaḥ hi aṣṭavidham hitvā jahau pañcavidham rajaḥ ulkā pātāḥ diśām dāhāḥ bhūmikampāḥ tathā eva ca prādurbhūtāḥ kṣaṇe tasmin tat adbhutam iva abhavat drumāḥ śākhāḥ ca mumucuḥ śikharāṇi ca parvatāḥ nirghāta śabdaiḥ ca giriḥ himavān dīryati iva ha na babhāse sahasrāṃśuḥ na jajvāla ca pāvakaḥ hradāḥ ca saritaḥ ca eva cukṣubhuḥ sāgarāḥ tathā vavau samīraṇaḥ ca api divya gandha vahaḥ śuciḥ saṃśliṣṭe śveta pīte dve rukma rūpya maye śubhe udīcīm diśam āśritya rucire saṃdadarśa ha tatas parvata śṛṅge dve sahasā eva dvidhākṛte adṛśyetām mahā rāja tat adbhutam iva abhavat tatas parvata śṛṅgābhyām sahasā eva viniḥsṛtaḥ gandharvāṇām ṛṣīṇām ca ye ca śaila nivāsinaḥ dṛṣṭvā śukam atikrāntam parvatam ca dvidhākṛtam sādhu sādhu iti tatra āsīt nādaḥ sarvatra bhārata yakṣa rākṣasa saṃghaiḥ ca vidyādhara gaṇaiḥ tathā divyaiḥ puṣpaiḥ samākīrṇam antarikṣam samantataḥ āsīt kila mahā rāja śuka abhipatane tadā tatas mandākinīm ramyām upariṣṭāt abhivrajan śukaḥ dadarśa dharma ātmā puṣpita druma kānanām tasyām krīḍanti abhiratāḥ snānti ca eva apsaraḥ gaṇāḥ śūnya ākāram nirākārāḥ śukam dṛṣṭvā vivāsasaḥ tam ājñāya pitā sneha samanvitaḥ uttamām gatim āsthāya pṛṣṭhatas anusasāra ha śukaḥ tu mārutāt ūrdhvam gatim kṛtvā antarikṣa gām darśayitvā prabhāvam svam sarva bhūtaḥ abhavat tadā mahā yoga gatim tu agryām vyāsa utthāya mahā tapāḥ nimeṣa antara mātreṇa śuka abhipatanam yayau sa dadarśa dvidhā kṛtvā parvata agram śukam gatam śaśaṃsuḥ ṛṣayaḥ tasmai karma putrasya tat tadā tatas śuka iti dīrgheṇa śaikṣeṇa ākranditaḥ tadā svayam pitrā svareṇa uccais trīn lokān anunādya vai śukaḥ sarva gataḥ bhūtvā sarva ātmā sarvatomukhaḥ pratyabhāṣata dharma ātmā bhoḥ śabdena anunādayan tatas eka akṣaram nādam bho iti eva samīrayan tatas prabhṛti ca adya api śabdān uccāritān pṛthak giri gahvara pṛṣṭheṣu vyājahāra śukam prati antarhitaḥ prabhāvam tu darśayitvā śukaḥ tadā mahimānam tu tam dṛṣṭvā putrasya amita tejasaḥ tatas mandākinī tīre krīḍantaḥ apsarasām gaṇāḥ āsādya tam ṛṣim sarvāḥ saṃbhrāntāḥ gata cetasaḥ vasanāni ādaduḥ kāḥ cit dṛṣṭvā tam muni sattamam tām mukta tām tu vijñāya muniḥ putrasya vai tadā sakta tām ātmanaḥ ca eva prītaḥ abhūt vrīḍitaḥ ca ha tam deva gandharva vṛtaḥ mahā ṛṣi gaṇa pūjitaḥ pinākahastaḥ bhagavān abhyāgacchata śaṃkaraḥ tam uvāca mahādevaḥ sāntva pūrvam idam vacaḥ putra śoka abhisaṃtaptam kṛṣṇadvaipāyanam tadā vīryeṇa sadṛśaḥ putraḥ tvayā mattaḥ purā vṛtaḥ sa tathā lakṣaṇaḥ jātaḥ tapasā tava saṃbhṛtaḥ sa gatim paramām prāptaḥ duṣprāpām ajita indriyaiḥ yāvat sthāsyanti girayaḥ yāvat sthāsyanti sāgarāḥ tāvat tava akṣayā kīrtiḥ sa putrasya bhaviṣyati chāyām sva putra sadṛśīm sarvatas anapagām sadā chāyām paśyan samāvṛttaḥ sa muniḥ parayā mudā vistareṇa mayā ākhyātam yat mām tvam paripṛcchasi etat ācaṣṭa me rājan deva ṛṣiḥ nāradaḥ purā vyāsaḥ ca eva mahā yogī saṃjalpeṣu pade pade itihāsam imam puṇyam mokṣa dharma artha saṃhitam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca gṛhasthaḥ brahmacārī vā vānaprasthaḥ atha bhikṣukaḥ yaḥ icchet siddhim āsthātum devatām kām yajeta saḥ muktaḥ ca kām gatim gacchet mokṣaḥ ca eva kimātmakaḥ devatānām ca kaḥ devaḥ pitṝṇām ca tathā pitā bhīṣmaḥ uvāca gūḍham mām praśna vid praśnam pṛcchase tvam iha anagha na hi eṣa tarkayā śakyaḥ vaktum varṣa śataiḥ api ṛte deva prasādāt vā rājan jñāna āgamena vā gahanam hi etat ākhyānam vyākhyātavyam tava ari han atrā api udāharanti imam itihāsam purātanam nāradasya ca saṃvādam ṛṣeḥ nārāyaṇasya ca nārāyaṇaḥ hi viśvātmā catur mūrtiḥ sanātanaḥ dharma ātmajaḥ saṃbabhūva pitā evam me abhyabhāṣata kṛte yuge mahā rāja purā svāyaṃbhuve antare naraḥ nārāyaṇaḥ ca eva hariḥ kṛṣṇaḥ tathā eva ca badaryāśramam āsādya śakaṭe kanaka āmaye aṣṭa cakram hi tat yānam bhūta yuktam manoramam mahā meroḥ gireḥ śṛṅgāt pracyutaḥ gandhamādanam nāradaḥ su mahat bhūtam lokān sarvān acīcarat tam deśam agamat rājan badaryāśramam āśu gaḥ tayoḥ āhnika velāyām tasya kautūhalam tu abhūt idam tat āspadam kṛtsnam yasmin lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ sa deva asura gandharvāḥ sa ṛṣi kiṃnara lelihāḥ ekā mūrtiḥ iyam pūrvam jātā bhūyas caturvidhā nara nārāyaṇābhyām ca kṛṣṇena hariṇā tathā tatra kṛṣṇaḥ hariḥ ca eva kasmin cit kāraṇa antare pitarau sarva bhūtānām daivatam ca yaśasvinau kām devatām nu yajataḥ pitṝn vā kān mahāmatī iti saṃcintya manasā bhaktyā nārāyaṇasya ha kṛte daive ca pitrye ca tatas tābhyām nirīkṣitaḥ pūjitaḥ ca eva vidhinā yathā proktena śāstrataḥ tam dṛṣṭvā mahat āścaryam apūrvam vidhi vistaram upopaviṣṭaḥ su prītaḥ nāradaḥ bhagavān ṛṣiḥ nārāyaṇam saṃnirīkṣya prasannena antarātmanā vedeṣu sa purāṇeṣu sa aṅga upāṅgeṣu gīyase tvam ajaḥ śāśvataḥ dhātā mataḥ amṛtam anuttamam catvāraḥ hi āśramāḥ deva sarve gārhasthya mūlakāḥ pitā mātā ca sarvasya jagataḥ śāśvataḥ guruḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca sa hi antarātmā bhūtānām kṣetrajñaḥ ca iti kathyate avyaktā vyakta bhāva sthā yā sā prakṛtiḥ avyayā ātmā hi nau sa vijñeyaḥ tatas tam pūjayāvahe tena eṣā prathitā brahman maryādā loka bhāvinī marīciḥ aṅgirāḥ atriḥ ca pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ parameṣṭhī ca vivasvān somaḥ eva ca ekaviṃśatiḥ utpannāḥ te prajāpatayaḥ smṛtāḥ tasya devasya maryādām pūjayanti sanātanīm ātma prāptāni ca tatas jānanti dvijasattamāḥ te tad prasādāt gacchanti tena ādiṣṭa phalām gatim ye hīnāḥ saptadaśabhiḥ guṇaiḥ karmabhiḥ eva ca kalāḥ pañcadaśa tyaktvā te muktāḥ iti niścayaḥ dṛśyate jñāna yogena āvām ca prasṛtau tatas evam jñātvā tam ātmānam pūjayāvaḥ sanātanam tam vedāḥ ca āśramāḥ ca eva nānā tanu samāsthitāḥ bhaktyā saṃpūjayanti ādyam gatim ca eṣām dadāti saḥ ye tu tad bhāvitāḥ loke ekānti tvam samāsthitāḥ bhaktyā premṇā ca viprarṣe asmad bhaktyā ca te śrutaḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca saḥ evam uktaḥ dvipadām variṣṭhaḥ nārāyaṇena uttama pūruṣeṇa jagāda vākyam dvipadām variṣṭham nārāyaṇam loka hita adhivāsam tat sādhyatām loka hita artham adya gacchāmi draṣṭum prakṛtim tava ādyām vedāḥ su adhītāḥ mama lokanātha taptam tapaḥ na anṛtam ukta pūrvam pūjām gurūṇām satatam karomi parasya guhyam na ca bhinna pūrvam tam ca ādidevam satatam prapanna ekānta bhāvena vṛṇomi ajasram ebhiḥ viśeṣaiḥ pariśuddha sattvaḥ kasmāt na paśyeyam anantam īśam tat pārameṣṭhyasya vacaḥ niśamya nārāyaṇaḥ sātvata dharma goptā tatas visṛṣṭaḥ parameṣṭhi putraḥ saḥ abhyarcayitvā tam ṛṣim purāṇam tatra avatasthe ca muniḥ muhūrtam ekāntam āsādya gireḥ sa śṛṅge kṣīrodadheḥ uttaratas hi dvīpaḥ śvetaḥ sa nāmnā prathitaḥ viśālaḥ meroḥ sahasraiḥ sa hi yojanānām dvātriṃśatā ūrdhvam kavibhiḥ niruktaḥ atīndriyāḥ ca anaśanāḥ ca tatra niṣpanda hīnāḥ su sugandhinaḥ ca śvetāḥ pumāṃsaḥ gata sarva pāpāḥ cakṣuḥ muṣaḥ pāpa kṛtām narāṇām vajra asthikāyāḥ sama māna unmānā divya anvaya rūpāḥ śubha sāra upetāḥ chatra ākṛti śīrṣāḥ megha ogha ninādāḥ sat puṣkara catuṣkāḥ rājīva śata pādāḥ ṣaṣṭyā dantaiḥ yuktāḥ śuklaiḥ aṣṭābhiḥ daṃṣṭrābhiḥ ye bhaktyā devam viśva utpannam yasmāt sarve lokāḥ sūtāḥ vedāḥ dharmāḥ munayaḥ śāntāḥ devāḥ sarve tasya visargāḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca atīndriyāḥ nirāhārāḥ aniṣpandāḥ sugandhinaḥ katham te puruṣāḥ jātāḥ kā teṣām gatiḥ uttamā teṣām lakṣaṇam etat hi yat śvetadvīpa vāsinām tasmāt me saṃśayam chindhi param kautūhalam hi me tvam hi sarva kathā ārāmaḥ tvām ca eva upāśritāḥ vayam bhīṣmaḥ uvāca vistīrṇā eṣā kathā rājan śrutā me pitṛ saṃnidhau sā eṣā tava hi vaktavyā kathāsāraḥ hi sa smṛtaḥ ākhaṇḍala sakhaḥ khyātaḥ bhaktaḥ nārāyaṇam harim sāmrājyam tena saṃprāptam nārāyaṇa varāt purā sātvatam vidhim āsthāya prāk sūrya mukha niḥsṛtam pūjayām āsa deveśam tad śeṣeṇa pitāmahān pitṛ śeṣeṇa viprān ca saṃvibhajya āśritān ca saḥ śeṣa anna bhuj satya paraḥ sarva bhūteṣu ahiṃsakaḥ eka śayyā āsanam śakraḥ dattavān devarāj svayam ātmā rājyam dhanam ca eva kalatram vāhanāni ca kāmya naimittika ajasram yajñiyāḥ parama kriyāḥ sarvāḥ sātvatam āsthāya vidhim cakre samāhitaḥ tasya praśāsataḥ rājyam dharmeṇa amitra ghātinaḥ na anṛtā vāc samabhavat manaḥ duṣṭam na ca abhavat na ca kāyena kṛtavān sa pāpam param aṇu api ye hi te munayaḥ khyātāḥ sapta citraśikhaṇḍinaḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ ca mahā tejāḥ ete citraśikhaṇḍinaḥ sapta prakṛtayaḥ hi etāḥ tathā svāyaṃbhuvaḥ aṣṭamaḥ etābhiḥ dhāryate lokaḥ tābhyaḥ śāstram viniḥsṛtam ekāgra manasaḥ dāntāḥ munayaḥ saṃyame ratāḥ lokān saṃcintya manasā tatas śāstram pracakrire tatra dharma artha kāmāḥ hi mokṣaḥ paścāt ca kīrtitaḥ maryādāḥ vividhāḥ ca eva divi bhūmau ca saṃsthitāḥ ārādhya tapasā devam harim nārāyaṇam prabhum divyam varṣa sahasram vai sarve te ṛṣibhiḥ saha nārāyaṇa anuśāstā hi tadā devī sarasvatī viveśa tān ṛṣīn sarvān lokānām hita kāmyayā ādau eva hi tat śāstram oṃkāra svara bhūṣitam ṛṣibhiḥ bhāvitam tatra yatra kāruṇikaḥ hi asau tatas prasannaḥ bhagavān anirdiṣṭa śarīra gaḥ ṛṣīn uvāca tān sarvān adṛśyaḥ puruṣottamaḥ kṛtam śata sahasram hi ślokānām idam uttamam ṛk yajuḥ sāmabhiḥ juṣṭam atharva āṅgirasaiḥ tathā tathā pramāṇam hi mayā kṛtaḥ brahmā prasāda jaḥ sarve ca nakṣatra gaṇāḥ yat ca bhūta abhiśabditam adhikāreṣu vartante yathāsvam brahma vādinaḥ bhaviṣyati pramāṇam vai etat mad anuśāsanam asmāt pravakṣyate dharmāt manuḥ svāyaṃbhuvaḥ svayam tadā pravakṣyataḥ śāstram yuṣmad matibhiḥ uddhṛtam svāyaṃbhuveṣu dharmeṣu śāstre ca uśanasā kṛte yuṣmad kṛtam idam śāstram prajāpālaḥ vasuḥ tatas bṛhaspati sakāśāt vai prāpsyate dvijasattamāḥ tena śāstreṇa lokeṣu kriyāḥ sarvāḥ kariṣyati etat hi sarva śāstrāṇām śāstram uttama saṃjñitam sa ca rājā śriyā yuktaḥ bhaviṣyati mahān vasuḥ etāvat uktvā vacanam adṛśyaḥ puruṣottamaḥ visṛjya tān ṛṣīn sarvān kām api prasthitaḥ diśam sāṅga upaniṣadam śāstram sthāpayitvā bṛhaspatau jagmuḥ yathā īpsitam deśam tapase kṛta niścayāḥ dhāraṇāt sarva lokānām sarva dharma pravartakāḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca bṛhat brahma mahat ca iti śabdāḥ paryāya vācakāḥ tasya śiṣyaḥ babhūva agryaḥ rājā uparicaraḥ vasuḥ adhītavān tadā śāstram samyak citraśikhaṇḍi jam sa rājā bhāvitaḥ pūrvam daivena vidhinā vasuḥ pālayām āsa pṛthivīm divam ākhaṇḍalaḥ yathā tasya yajñaḥ mahān āsīt aśvamedhaḥ mahātmanaḥ prajāpati sutāḥ ca atra sadasyāḥ tu abhavan trayaḥ dhanuṣākṣaḥ atha raibhyaḥ ca arvāvasu parāvasū ṛṣiḥ medhātithiḥ ca eva tāṇḍyaḥ ca eva mahān ṛṣiḥ ṛṣiḥ śaktiḥ mahābhāgaḥ tathā vedaśirāḥ ca yaḥ kapilaḥ ca ṛṣi śreṣṭhaḥ śālihotra pitāmahaḥ ādyaḥ kaṭhaḥ taittiriḥ ca vaiśaṃpāyana pūrvajaḥ kaṇvaḥ atha devahotraḥ ca ete ṣoḍaśa kīrtitāḥ saṃbhṛtāḥ sarva saṃbhārāḥ tasmin rājan mahā kratau ahiṃsraḥ śuciḥ akṣudraḥ nirāśīḥ karma saṃstutaḥ āraṇyaka pada udgītāḥ bhāgāḥ tatra upakalpitāḥ sākṣāt tam darśayām āsa saḥ adṛśyaḥ anyena kena cit svayam bhāgam upāghrāya puroḍāśam gṛhītavān ākāśam ghnan sruvaḥ pātaiḥ roṣāt aśrūṇi avartayat grāhyaḥ svayam hi devena mad pratyakṣam na saṃśayaḥ udyatāḥ yajña bhāgāḥ hi sākṣāt prāptāḥ suraiḥ iha tatas sa tam samuddhūtam bhūmipālaḥ mahān vasuḥ prasādayām āsa munim sadasyāḥ te ca sarvaśas ūcuḥ ca enam asaṃbhrāntāḥ na roṣam kartum arhasi na eṣa dharmaḥ kṛta yuge yaḥ tvam roṣam acīkṛthāḥ na sa śakyaḥ tvayā draṣṭum asmābhiḥ vā bṛhaspate ekata dvita tritāḥ ūcuḥ vayam hi brahmaṇaḥ putrāḥ mānasāḥ parikīrtitāḥ gatāḥ niḥśreyasa artham hi kadā cit diśam uttarām eka pāda sthitāḥ samyak kāṣṭha bhūtāḥ samāhitāḥ meroḥ uttara bhāge tu kṣīrodasya anukūlataḥ katham paśyemahi vayam devam nārāyaṇam tu iti tatas vratasya avabhṛthe vāc uvāca aśarīriṇī yūyam jijñāsavaḥ bhaktāḥ katham drakṣyatha tam prabhum kṣīrodadheḥ uttaratas śvetadvīpaḥ mahā prabhaḥ tatra nārāyaṇa parāḥ mānavāḥ candra varcasaḥ ekānta bhāva upagatāḥ te bhaktāḥ puruṣottamam te sahasra arciṣam devam praviśanti sanātanam atīndriyāḥ nirāhārāḥ aniṣpandāḥ sugandhinaḥ ekāntinaḥ te puruṣāḥ śvetadvīpa nivāsinaḥ atha śrutvā vayam sarve vācam tām aśarīriṇīm yathā ākhyātena mārgeṇa tam deśam pratipedire prāpya śvetam mahā dvīpam tad cittāḥ tad didṛkṣavaḥ na ca paśyāma puruṣam tad tejaḥ hṛta darśanāḥ na kila a tapta tapasā śakyate draṣṭum añjasā tatas punar varṣa śatam taptvā tātkālikam mahat vrata avasāne su śubhān narān dadṛśire vayam śvetān candra pratīkāśān sarva lakṣaṇa lakṣitān nitya añjali kṛtān brahma japataḥ prāc udak mukhān yā bhavet muni śārdūla bhās sūryasya yuga kṣaye sahasā dṛṣṭavantaḥ sma punar eva bṛhaspate sahitāḥ ca abhyadhāvanta tatas te mānavāḥ drutam kṛta añjali puṭāḥ hṛṣṭāḥ namaḥ iti eva vādinaḥ tatas abhivadatām teṣām aśrauṣma vipulam dhvanim na kim cit api paśyāmaḥ hṛta dṛṣṭi bala indriyāḥ ekaḥ tu śabdaḥ a virataḥ śrutaḥ asmābhiḥ udīritaḥ jitam te puṇḍarīkākṣa namaḥ te viśvabhāvana namaḥ te astu hṛṣīkeśa mahāpuruṣa pūrvaja iti śabdaḥ śrutaḥ asmābhiḥ śikṣā akṣara samīritaḥ divyāni uvāha puṣpāṇi karmaṇyāḥ ca oṣadhīḥ
