tathā taiḥ iṣṭaḥ pañca kāla jñaiḥ hariḥ ekāntibhiḥ naraiḥ nūnam tatra āgataḥ devaḥ yathā taiḥ vāc udīritā vayam tu enam na paśyāmaḥ mohitāḥ tasya māyayā cintā vyākulita ātmānaḥ jātāḥ smaḥ aṅgirasām vara mānavānām sahasreṣu teṣu vai śuddha yoniṣu asmān na kaḥ cit manasā cakṣuṣā vā api apūjayat te api svasthāḥ muni gaṇāḥ eka bhāvam anuvratāḥ na asmāsu dadhire bhāvam brahma bhāvam anuṣṭhitāḥ tatas asmān su pariśrāntān tapasā ca api karśitān uvāca kha stham kim api bhūtam tatra aśarīrakam dṛṣṭāḥ vaḥ puruṣāḥ śvetāḥ sarva indriya vivarjitāḥ dṛṣṭaḥ bhavati deveśaḥ ebhiḥ dṛṣṭaiḥ dvijottamāḥ na sa śakyaḥ a bhaktena draṣṭum devaḥ katham cana kāmam kālena mahatā ekānti tvam samāgataiḥ śakyaḥ draṣṭum sa bhagavān prabhā maṇḍala durdṛśaḥ mahat kāryam tu kartavyam yuṣmābhiḥ dvijasattamāḥ surāṇām kārya siddhi artham sahāyāḥ vai bhaviṣyatha tasya prasādāt prāptāḥ smaḥ deśam īpsitam añjasā devaḥ asmābhiḥ na dṛṣṭaḥ sa katham tvam draṣṭum arhasi nārāyaṇaḥ mahat bhūtam viśvasṛj ghavya kavya bhuj bhīṣmaḥ uvāca anunītaḥ sadasyaiḥ ca bṛhaspatiḥ udāra dhīḥ samānīya tatas yajñam daivatam samapūjayat samāpta yajñaḥ rājā api prajāḥ pālitavān vasuḥ brahma śāpāt divaḥ bhraṣṭaḥ praviveśa mahīm tatas nārāyaṇa paraḥ bhūtvā nārāyaṇa padam jagau mahī talāt gataḥ sthānam brahmaṇaḥ samanantaram parām gatim anuprāptaḥ iti naiṣṭhikam añjasā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca yadā bhaktaḥ bhagavataḥ āsīt rājā mahāvasuḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca atrā api udāharanti imam itihāsam purātanam ṛṣīṇām ca eva saṃvādam tridaśānām ca bhārata ajena yaṣṭavyam iti devāḥ prāhuḥ dvijottamān sa ca chāgaḥ hi ajaḥ jñeyaḥ na anyaḥ paśuḥ iti sthitiḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ bījaiḥ yajñeṣu yaṣṭavyam iti vai vaidikī śrutiḥ aja saṃjñāni bījāni chāgam na ghnantum arhatha na eṣa dharmaḥ satām devāḥ yatra vadhyeta vai paśuḥ idam kṛta yugam śreṣṭham katham vadhyeta vai paśuḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca teṣām saṃvadatām evam ṛṣīṇām vibudhaiḥ saha mārga āgataḥ nṛpa śreṣṭhaḥ tam deśam prāptavān vasuḥ tam dṛṣṭvā sahasā āyāntam vasum te tu antarikṣa gam ūcuḥ dvijātayaḥ devān eṣa chetsyati saṃśayam yajvā dānapatiḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sarva bhūta hita priyaḥ katham svid anyathā brūyāt vākyam eṣa mahān vasuḥ evam te saṃvidam kṛtvā vibudhāḥ ṛṣayaḥ tathā apṛcchan sahasā abhyetya vasum rājānam antikāt etat naḥ saṃśayam chindhi pramāṇam naḥ bhavān mataḥ sa tān kṛtāñjaliḥ bhūtvā paripapraccha vai vasuḥ kasya vaḥ kaḥ mataḥ pakṣaḥ brūta satyam samāgatāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ dhānyaiḥ yaṣṭavyam iti eṣa pakṣaḥ asmākam narādhipa devānām tu paśuḥ pakṣaḥ mataḥ rājan vadasva naḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca devānām tu matam jñātvā vasunā pakṣa saṃśrayāt chāgena ajena yaṣṭavyam evam uktam vacaḥ tadā ūcuḥ vasum vimāna stham deva pakṣa artha vādinam sura pakṣaḥ gṛhītaḥ te yasmāt tasmāt divaḥ pata adya prabhṛti te rājan ākāśe vihatā gatiḥ asmad śāpa abhighātena mahīm bhittvā pravekṣyasi adhas vai saṃbabhūva āśu bhūmeḥ vivara gaḥ nṛpaḥ smṛtiḥ tu enam na prajahau tadā nārāyaṇa ājñayā devāḥ tu sahitāḥ sarve vasoḥ śāpa vimokṣaṇam cintayām āsuḥ avyagrāḥ sukṛtam hi nṛpasya tat anena asmad kṛte rājñā śāpaḥ prāptaḥ mahātmanā iti buddhyā vyavasya āśu gatvā niścayam īśvarāḥ ūcuḥ tam hṛṣṭa manasaḥ rāja upari caram tadā kāmam sa tava tuṣṭa ātmā kuryāt śāpa vimokṣaṇam mānanā tu dvijātīnām kartavyā vai mahātmanām avaśyam tapasā teṣām phalitavyam nṛpa uttama yatas tvam sahasā bhraṣṭaḥ ākāśāt medinī talam yāvat tvam śāpa doṣeṇa kālam āsiṣyase anagha bhūmeḥ vivara gaḥ bhūtvā tāvantam kālam āpsyasi yajñeṣu su hutām vipraiḥ vasoḥ dhārām mahātmabhiḥ prāpsyase asmad anudhyānāt mā ca tvām glāniḥ āspṛśet na kṣudh pipāse rāja indra bhūmeḥ chidre bhaviṣyataḥ vasoḥ dhārā anupīta tvāt tejasā āpyāyitena ca evam dattvā varam rājñe sarve tatra divaukasaḥ gatāḥ sva bhavanam devāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca tapodhanāḥ cakre ca satatam pūjām viṣvaksenāya bhārata tatra api pañcabhiḥ yajñaiḥ pañca kālān ariṃdama tatas asya tuṣṭaḥ bhagavān bhaktyā nārāyaṇaḥ hariḥ samrāj rājā vasuḥ nāma dharma ātmā mām samāśritaḥ brāhmaṇānām prakopena praviṣṭaḥ vasudhā talam bhūmeḥ vivara saṃguptam garuḍa iha mama ājñayā adhas caram nṛpa śreṣṭham khecaram kuru māciram viveśa vivaram bhūmeḥ yatra āste vāgyataḥ vasuḥ tasmin muhūrte saṃjajñe rājā uparicaraḥ punar sa śarīraḥ gataḥ ca eva brahma lokam nṛpa uttamaḥ evam tena api kaunteya vāc doṣāt devatā ājñayā prāptā gatiḥ a yajva arhā dvija śāpāt mahātmanā tatas śīghram jahau śāpam brahma lokam avāpa ca etat te sarvam ākhyātam te bhūtāḥ mānavāḥ yathā nāradaḥ api yathā śvetam dvīpam sa gatavān ṛṣiḥ tat te sarvam pravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣva ekamanāḥ nṛpa bhīṣmaḥ uvāca prāpya śvetam mahā dvīpam nāradaḥ bhagavān ṛṣiḥ dadarśa tān eva narān śvetān candra prabhān śubhān pūjayām āsa śirasā manasā taiḥ ca pūjitaḥ bhūtvā ekāgra manāḥ vipraḥ ūrdhvabāhuḥ mahā muniḥ stotram jagau sa viśvāya nirguṇāya mahātmane nāradaḥ uvāca vedeśaya kuśeśaya brahmeśaya padmeśaya viśveśvara tvam jagat anvayaḥ tvam jagat prakṛtiḥ tava agniḥ āsyam vaḍavāmukhaḥ agniḥ tvam āhutiḥ tvam sārathiḥ tvam vaṣaṭkāraḥ tvam oṃkāraḥ tvam manaḥ tvam candramāḥ tvam cakṣuḥ ādyam tvam sūryaḥ tvam diśām gajaḥ diś bhāno hayaśiraḥ prathamatrisauparṇa pañca agne triṇāciketa ṣaḍaṅga vidhāna prāgjyotiṣa jyeṣṭha sāma ga sāmika vrata dhara atharvaśiraḥ pañcamahākalpa phenapa ācārya vrata āvāsa samudra adhivāsa yaśaḥ vāsa tapaḥ vāsa lakṣmī āvāsa vidyā vāsa kīrti āvāsa śrīvāsa sarva āvāsa vāsudeva chinna saṃśaya sarvatas nivṛtta brāhmaṇa rūpa brāhmaṇapriya viśvamūrte mahā mūrte bāndhava bhakta vatsala brahmaṇyadeva bhaktaḥ aham tvām didṛkṣuḥ ekānta darśanāya namaḥ namaḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca tam munim darśayām āsa nāradam viśva rūpa dhṛk kim cit candra viśuddha ātmā kim cit candrāt viśeṣavān kṛśānu varṇaḥ kim cit ca kim cit dhiṣṇya ākṛtiḥ prabhuḥ śuka patra varṇaḥ kim cit ca kim cit sphaṭika saprabhaḥ pravāla aṅkura varṇaḥ ca śveta varṇaḥ kva cit babhau kva cit suvarṇa varṇa ābhaḥ vaiḍūrya sadṛśaḥ kva cit nīla vaiḍūrya sadṛśaḥ indranīla nibhaḥ kva cit mayūragrīva varṇa ābhaḥ muktā hāra nibhaḥ kva cit etān varṇān bahuvidhān rūpe bibhrat sanātanaḥ sahasra nayanaḥ śrīmān śata śīrṣaḥ sahasrapād oṃkāram udgiran vaktrāt sāvitrīm ca tad anvayām āraṇyakam jagau devaḥ hariḥ nārāyaṇaḥ vaśī vedīm kamaṇḍalum darbhān maṇi rūpān atha upalān ajinam daṇḍa kāṣṭham ca jvalitam ca hutāśanam dhārayām āsa deveśaḥ hastaiḥ yajñapatiḥ tadā tam uvāca natam mūrdhnā devānām ādiḥ avyayaḥ imam deśam anuprāptāḥ mama darśana lālasāḥ na ca mām te dadṛśire na ca drakṣyati kaḥ cana ṛte hi ekāntika śreṣṭhāt tvam ca eva ekāntikaḥ mataḥ mama etāḥ tanavaḥ śreṣṭhāḥ jātāḥ dharma gṛhe dvija prasannaḥ aham tava adyā iha viśvamūrtiḥ iha avyayaḥ nāradaḥ uvāca sadyas phalam avāptam vai dṛṣṭaḥ yat bhagavān mayā varaḥ eṣa mama atyantam dṛṣṭaḥ tvam yat sanātanaḥ bhagavān viśva dṛś siṃhaḥ sarva mūrtiḥ mahā prabhuḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca evam saṃdarśayitvā tu nāradam parameṣṭhi jam ekāgrāḥ cintayeyuḥ mām na eṣām vighnaḥ bhavet iti siddhāḥ ca ete mahābhāgāḥ purā hi ekāntinaḥ abhavan na dṛśyaḥ cakṣuṣā yaḥ asau na spṛśyaḥ sparśanena ca yaḥ ca sarva gataḥ sākṣī lokasya ātmā iti kathyate bhūta grāma śarīreṣu naśyatsu na vinaśyati ajaḥ nityaḥ śāśvataḥ ca nirguṇaḥ niṣkalaḥ tathā dvis dvādaśebhyaḥ tattvebhyaḥ khyātaḥ yaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ puruṣaḥ niṣkriyaḥ ca eva jñāna dṛśyaḥ ca kathyate sa vāsudevaḥ vijñeyaḥ parama ātmā sanātanaḥ paśya devasya māhātmyam mahimānam ca nārada etān guṇān tu kṣetrajñaḥ bhuṅkte na ebhiḥ sa bhujyate nirguṇaḥ guṇabhuj ca eva guṇasraṣṭā guṇa adhikaḥ khe vāyuḥ pralayam yāti manasi ākāśam eva ca na asti tasmāt parataram puruṣāt vai sanātanāt ṛte tam ekam puruṣam vāsudevam sanātanam sarva bhūta ātma bhūtaḥ hi vāsudevaḥ mahā balaḥ pṛthivī vāyuḥ ākāśam āpaḥ jyotiḥ ca pañcamam te sametāḥ mahātmānaḥ śarīram iti saṃjñitam utpannaḥ eva bhavati śarīram ceṣṭayan prabhuḥ na vinā dhātu saṃghātam śarīram bhavati kva cit na ca jīvam vinā brahman dhātavaḥ ceṣṭayanti uta sa jīvaḥ parisaṃkhyātaḥ śeṣaḥ saṃkarṣaṇaḥ prabhuḥ yasmin ca sarva bhūtāni pralayam yānti saṃkṣaye sa manaḥ sarva bhūtānām pradyumnaḥ paripaṭhyate tasmāt prasūtaḥ yaḥ kartā kāryam kāraṇam eva ca saḥ aniruddhaḥ saḥ īśānaḥ vyaktiḥ sā sarva karmasu yaḥ vāsudevaḥ bhagavān kṣetrajñaḥ nirguṇa ātmakaḥ jñeyaḥ saḥ eva bhagavān jīvaḥ saṃkarṣaṇaḥ prabhuḥ saṃkarṣaṇāt ca pradyumnaḥ manaḥ bhūtaḥ saḥ ucyate akṣaram ca kṣaram ca eva sat ca asat ca eva nārada aham hi puruṣaḥ jñeyaḥ niṣkriyaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ etat tvayā na vijñeyam rūpavān iti dṛśyate icchan muhūrtāt naśyeyam īśaḥ aham jagataḥ guruḥ māyā hi eṣā mayā sṛṣṭā yat mām paśyasi nārada sarva bhūta guṇaiḥ yuktam na evam tvam jñātum arhasi siddhāḥ hi ete mahābhāgāḥ narāḥ hi ekāntinaḥ abhavan tamaḥ rajobhyām nirmuktāḥ pravekṣyanti ca mām mune aham kartā ca kāryam ca kāraṇam ca api nārada aham hi jīva saṃjñaḥ vai mayi jīvaḥ samāhitaḥ mā evam te buddhiḥ atrā abhūt dṛṣṭaḥ jīvaḥ mayā iti ca bhūta grāma śarīreṣu naśyatsu na naśāmi aham paśya ekādaśa me rudrān dakṣiṇam pārśvam āsthitān dvādaśa eva tathā ādityān vāmam pārśvam samāsthitān agratas ca eva me paśya vasūn aṣṭau sura uttamān nāsatyam ca eva dasram ca bhiṣajau paśya pṛṣṭhatas sarvān prajāpatīn paśya paśya sapta ṛṣīn api vedān yajñān ca śataśas paśya amṛtam atha auṣadhīḥ tapāṃsi niyamān ca eva yamān api pṛthagvidhān tathā aṣṭaguṇam aiśvaryam ekastham paśya mūrtimat śriyam lakṣmīm ca kīrtim ca pṛthivīm ca kakudminīm vedānām mātaram paśya mad sthām devīm sarasvatīm dhruvam ca jyotiṣām śreṣṭham paśya nārada khecaram ambhodharān samudrān ca sarāṃsi saritaḥ tathā mūrtimantaḥ pitṛ gaṇān caturaḥ paśya sattama trīn ca eva imān guṇān paśya mad sthān mūrti vivarjitān deva kāryāt api mune pitṛ kāryam viśiṣyate devānām ca pitṝṇām ca pitā hi ekaḥ aham āditas mayā sṛṣṭaḥ purā brahmā mad yajñam ayajat svayam ahaṃkāra kṛtam ca eva nāma paryāya vācakam tvayā kṛtām ca maryādām na atikrāmyati kaḥ cana sura asura gaṇānām ca ṛṣīṇām ca tapodhana pitṝṇām ca mahābhāga satatam saṃśita vrata vividhānām ca bhūtānām tvam upāsyaḥ bhaviṣyasi prādurbhāva gataḥ ca aham sura kāryeṣu nityadā etān ca anyān ca rucirān brahmaṇe amita tejase nirvāṇam sarva dharmāṇām nivṛttiḥ paramā smṛtā tasmāt nivṛttim āpannaḥ caret sarva aṅga nirvṛtaḥ vidyā sahāyavantam mām āditya stham sanātanam kapilam prāhuḥ ācāryāḥ sāṃkhya niścita niścayāḥ hiraṇyagarbhaḥ bhagavān eṣa chandasi suṣṭutaḥ eṣaḥ aham vyaktim āgamya tiṣṭhāmi divi śāśvataḥ kṛtvā ātma sthāni bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca ekākī vidyayā sārdham vihariṣye dvijottama tatas bhūyas jagat sarvam kariṣyāmi iha vidyayā asmad mūrtiḥ caturthī yā sā asṛjat śeṣam avyayam sa hi saṃkarṣaṇaḥ proktaḥ pradyumnam saḥ api ajījanat brahmaṇaḥ sarva bhūtāni carāṇi sthāvarāṇi ca etām sṛṣṭim vijānīhi kalpa ādiṣu punar punar naṣṭau punar balāt kālaḥ ānayati amita dyutiḥ tathā balāt aham pṛthvīm sarva bhūta hitāya vai sattvaiḥ ākrānta sarva aṅgām naṣṭām sāgaramekhalām ānayiṣyāmi svam sthānam vārāham rūpam āsthitaḥ hiraṇyākṣam haniṣyāmi daiteyam bala garvitam nārasiṃham vapuḥ kṛtvā hiraṇyakaśipum punar bhaviṣyati sa śakram ca sva rājyāt cyāvayiṣyati adityām dvādaśaḥ putraḥ saṃbhaviṣyāmi kaśyapāt tatas rājyam pradāsyāmi śakrāya amita tejase devatāḥ sthāpayiṣyāmi sveṣu sthāneṣu nārada balim ca eva kariṣyāmi pātāla tala vāsinam tretā yuge bhaviṣyāmi rāmaḥ bhṛgukulodvahaḥ kṣatram ca utsādayiṣyāmi samṛddha bala vāhanam rāmaḥ dāśarathiḥ bhūtvā bhaviṣyāmi jagatpatiḥ prāpsyataḥ vānara tvam hi prajāpati sutau ṛṣī haniṣye rāvaṇam saṃkhye sa gaṇam lokakaṇṭakam prādurbhāvaḥ kaṃsa hetoḥ mathurāyām bhaviṣyati tatra aham dānavān hatvā su bahūn deva kaṇṭakān kuśasthalīm kariṣyāmi nivāsam dvārakām purīm haniṣye narakam bhaumam muram pīṭham ca dānavam kuśasthalīm nayiṣyāmi hatvā vai dānava uttamān śaṃkaram ca mahāsenam bāṇa priya hita eṣiṇam tatas sutam baleḥ jitvā bāṇam bāhu sahasriṇam vināśayiṣyāmi tatas sarvān saubha nivāsinaḥ yaḥ kālayavanaḥ khyātaḥ garga tejobhiḥ saṃvṛtaḥ jarāsaṃdhaḥ ca balavān sarva rāja virodhakaḥ samāgateṣu baliṣu pṛthivyām sarva rājasu evam lokāḥ vadiṣyanti nara nārāyaṇau ṛṣī udyuktau dahataḥ kṣatram loka kārya artham īśvarau kṛtvā bhāra avataraṇam vasudhāyāḥ yathā īpsitam sarva sātvata mukhyānām dvārakāyāḥ ca sattama kariṣye pralayam ghoram ātma jñāti vināśanam kṛtvā lokān gamiṣyāmi svān aham brahma satkṛtān haṃsaḥ hayaśirāḥ ca eva prādurbhāvāḥ dvijottama yadā veda śrutiḥ naṣṭā mayā pratyāhṛtā tadā sa vedāḥ sa śrutīkāḥ ca kṛtāḥ pūrvam kṛte yuge atikrāntāḥ purāṇeṣu śrutāḥ te yadi vā kva cit atikrāntāḥ ca bahavaḥ prādurbhāvāḥ mama uttamāḥ loka kāryāṇi kṛtvā ca punar svām prakṛtim gatāḥ na hi etat brahmaṇā prāptam īdṛśam mama darśanam purāṇam ca bhaviṣyam ca sa rahasyam ca sattama nāradaḥ api mahā tejāḥ prāpya anugraham īpsitam nara nārāyaṇau draṣṭum prādravat badara āśramam sāṃkhya yoga kṛtam tena pañcarātra anuśabditam nārāyaṇa mukha udgītam nāradaḥ aśrāvayat punar brahmaṇaḥ sadane tāta yathā dṛṣṭam yathā śrutam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca etat āścarya bhūtam hi māhātmyam tasya dhīmataḥ kim brahmā na vijānīte yatas śuśrāva nāradāt pitāmahaḥ hi bhagavān tasmāt devāt anantaraḥ katham sa na vijānīyāt prabhāvam amita ojasaḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca mahākalpa sahasrāṇi mahākalpa śatāni ca samatītāni rāja indra sargāḥ ca pralayāḥ ca ha jānāti deva pravaram bhūyas ca atas adhikam nṛpa parama ātmānam īśānam ātmanaḥ prabhavam tathā tebhyaḥ tat śrāvayām āsa purāṇam veda saṃmitam teṣām sakāśāt sūryaḥ ca śrutvā vai bhāvitātmanām ātma anugāminām brahma śrāvayām āsa bhārata ṣaṭṣaṣṭiḥ hi sahasrāṇi ṛṣīṇām bhāvitātmanām sūryasya tapataḥ lokān nirmitāḥ ye puraḥsarāḥ teṣām akathayat sūryaḥ sarveṣām bhāvitātmanām sūrya anugāmibhiḥ tāta ṛṣibhiḥ taiḥ mahātmabhiḥ merau samāgatāḥ devāḥ śrāvitāḥ ca idam uttamam devānām tu sakāśāt vai tatas śrutvā asitaḥ dvijaḥ śrāvayām āsa rāja indra pitṝṇām muni sattamaḥ mama ca api pitā tāta kathayām āsa śaṃtanuḥ suraiḥ vā munibhiḥ vā api purāṇam yaiḥ idam śrutam sarve te paramātmānam pūjayanti punar punar idam ākhyānam ārṣeyam pāraṃparya āgatam nṛpa na a vāsudeva bhaktāya tvayā deyam katham cana mattaḥ anyāni ca te rājan upākhyāna śatāni vai yāni śrutāni dharmyāṇi teṣām sāraḥ ayam uddhṛtaḥ yaḥ ca idam paṭhate nityam yaḥ ca idam śṛṇuyāt naraḥ prāpya śvetam mahā dvīpam bhūtvā candra prabhaḥ naraḥ sa sahasra arciṣam devam praviśet na atra saṃśayaḥ mucyet ārtaḥ tathā rogāt śrutvā imām āditas kathām brahmaṇyadevaḥ bhagavān prīyatām te sanātanaḥ yudhiṣṭhira mahā bāho mahā bāhuḥ janārdanaḥ vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca bhrātaraḥ ca asya te sarve nārāyaṇa parāḥ abhavan nityam japya pare bhūtvā sarasvatīm udīrayan yaḥ hi asmākam guruḥ śreṣṭhaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ muniḥ sa jagau paramam japyam nārāyaṇam udīrayan gatvā antarikṣāt satatam kṣīrodam amṛta āśayam pūjayitvā ca deveśam punar āyāt svam āśramam yajña dhārī ca satatam veda vedāṅga vid tathā nivṛttam ca āsthitaḥ dharmam kṣemī bhāgavata priyaḥ katham pravṛtti dharmeṣu bhāga arhāḥ devatāḥ kṛtāḥ katham nivṛtti dharmāḥ ca kṛtāḥ vyāvṛtta buddhayaḥ etam naḥ saṃśayam vipra chindhi guhyam sanātanam tvayā nārāyaṇa kathā śrutā vai dharma saṃhitā ime sa brahmakāḥ lokāḥ sa sura asura mānavāḥ kriyāsu abhyudaya uktāsu saktāḥ dṛśyanti sarvaśas mokṣaḥ ca uktaḥ tvayā brahman nirvāṇam paramam sukham ye ca muktāḥ bhavanti iha puṇya pāpa vivarjitāḥ te sahasra arciṣam devam praviśanti iti śuśrumaḥ aho hi duranuṣṭheyaḥ mokṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ ākāśam jagatī ca eva ye ca śeṣāḥ divaukasaḥ smṛtvā kāla parīmāṇam pravṛttim ye samāsthitāḥ doṣaḥ kāla parīmāṇe mahān eṣa kriyāvatām etat me saṃśayam vipra hṛdi śalyam iva arpitam chindhi itihāsa kathanāt param kautūhalam hi me katham bhāga harāḥ proktāḥ devatāḥ kratuṣu dvija ye ca bhāgam pragṛhṇanti yajñeṣu dvijasattama vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca aho gūḍhatamaḥ praśnaḥ tvayā pṛṣṭaḥ janeśvara na a tapta tapasā hi eṣa na a veda viduṣā tathā na a purāṇa vidā ca api śakyaḥ vyāhartum añjasā hanta te kathayiṣyāmi yat me pṛṣṭaḥ purā guruḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ vyāsaḥ vedavyāsaḥ mahān ṛṣiḥ aham caturthaḥ śiṣyaḥ vai pañcamaḥ ca śukaḥ smṛtaḥ etān samāgatān sarvān pañca śiṣyān dama anvitān śauca ācāra samāyuktān jita krodhān jita indriyān vedān adhyāpayām āsa mahābhārata pañcamān teṣām abhyasyatām vedān kadā cit saṃśayaḥ abhavat eṣa vai yaḥ tvayā pṛṣṭaḥ tena teṣām prakīrtitaḥ tatas śrutaḥ mayā ca api tava ākhyeyaḥ adya bhārata śiṣyāṇām vacanam śrutvā sarva ajñāna tamonudaḥ parāśara sutaḥ śrīmān vyāsaḥ vākyam uvāca ha bhūtam bhavyam bhaviṣyat ca jānīyām iti sattamāḥ nārāyaṇa prasādena kṣīrodasya anukūlataḥ traikālikam idam jñānam prādurbhūtam yathā īpsitam tat śṛṇudhvam yathājñānam vakṣye saṃśayam uttamam yathā vṛttam hi kalpa ādau dṛṣṭam me jñānacakṣuṣā paramātmā iti yam prāhuḥ sāṃkhya yoga vidaḥ janāḥ mahāpuruṣa saṃjñām sa labhate svena karmaṇā tasmāt prasūtam avyaktam pradhānam tat viduḥ budhāḥ avyaktāt vyaktam utpannam loka sṛṣṭi artham īśvarāt pṛthivī vāyuḥ ākāśam āpaḥ jyotiḥ ca pañcamam ahaṃkāra prasūtāni mahābhūtāni bhārata mahābhūtāni sṛṣṭvā atha tad guṇān nirmame punar bhūtebhyaḥ ca eva niṣpannāḥ mūrtimantaḥ aṣṭa tān śṛṇu marīciḥ aṅgirāḥ ca atriḥ pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ ca mahātmā vai manuḥ svāyaṃbhuvaḥ tathā jñeyāḥ prakṛtayaḥ aṣṭau tāḥ yāsu lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ vedān vedāṅga saṃyuktān yajñān yajña aṅga saṃyutān aṣṭābhyaḥ prakṛtibhyaḥ ca jātam viśvam idam jagat rudraḥ roṣa ātmakaḥ jātaḥ daśa anyān saḥ asṛjat svayam ekādaśā ete rudrāḥ tu vikārāḥ puruṣāḥ smṛtāḥ utpannāḥ loka siddhi artham brahmāṇam samupasthitāḥ vayam hi sṛṣṭāḥ bhagavan tvayā vai prabhaviṣṇunā paripālyaḥ katham tena saḥ adhikāraḥ adhikāriṇā sādhu aham jñāpitaḥ devāḥ yuṣmābhiḥ bhadram astu vaḥ mama api eṣā samutpannā cintā yā bhavatām matā katham bala kṣayaḥ na syāt yuṣmākam hi ātmanaḥ ca me itas sarve api gacchāmaḥ śaraṇam lokasākṣiṇam tatas te brahmaṇā sārdham ṛṣayaḥ vibudhāḥ tathā kṣīrodasya uttaram kūlam jagmuḥ loka hita arthinaḥ sa mahāniyamaḥ nāma tapaḥ caryā su dāruṇā ūrdhvam dṛṣṭiḥ bāhavaḥ ca ekāgram ca manaḥ abhavat eka pāda sthitāḥ samyak kāṣṭha bhūtāḥ samāhitāḥ śuśruvuḥ madhurām vāṇīm veda vedāṅga bhūṣitām bho bhoḥ sa brahmakāḥ devāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca tapodhanāḥ svāgatena arcya vaḥ sarvān śrāvaye vākyam uttamam vijñātam vaḥ mayā kāryam tat ca loka hitam mahat pravṛtti yuktam kartavyam yuṣmad prāṇa upabṛṃhaṇam su taptam vaḥ tapaḥ devāḥ mama ārādhana kāmyayā yūyam ca vibudha śreṣṭhāḥ mām yajadhvam samāhitāḥ sarve bhāgān kalpayadhvam yajñeṣu mama nityaśas tathā śreyaḥ vidhāsyāmi yathā adhīkāram īśvarāḥ śrutvā etat devadevasya vākyam hṛṣṭa tanūruhāḥ veda dṛṣṭena vidhinā vaiṣṇavam kratum āharan te kārtayuga dharmāṇaḥ bhāgāḥ parama satkṛtāḥ prāpuḥ āditya varṇam tam puruṣam tamasaḥ param bṛhantam sarvagam devam īśānam vara dam prabhum aśarīraḥ babhāṣa idam vākyam kha sthaḥ maheśvaraḥ yena yaḥ kalpitaḥ bhāgaḥ sa tathā samupāgataḥ prītaḥ aham pradiśāmi adya phalam āvṛtti lakṣaṇam yūyam yajñaiḥ ijyamānāḥ samāpta vara dakṣiṇaiḥ kalpayiṣyanti vaḥ bhāgān te narāḥ veda kalpitān sa tathā yajña bhāga arhaḥ veda sūtre mayā kṛtaḥ yūyam lokān dhārayadhvam yajña bhāga phala uditāḥ sarva artha cintakāḥ loke yathā adhīkāra nirmitāḥ yāḥ kriyāḥ pracariṣyanti pravṛtti phala satkṛtāḥ tābhiḥ āpyāyita balāḥ lokān vai dhārayiṣyatha yūyam hi bhāvitāḥ loke sarva yajñeṣu mānavaiḥ mām tatas bhāvayiṣyadhvam eṣā vaḥ bhāvanā mama iti artham nirmitāḥ vedāḥ yajñāḥ ca oṣadhibhiḥ saha nirmāṇam etat yuṣmākam pravṛtti guṇa kalpitam mayā kṛtam sura śreṣṭhāḥ yāvat kalpa kṣayāt iti cintayadhvam loka hitam yathā adhīkāram īśvarāḥ marīciḥ aṅgirāḥ ca atriḥ pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ ete veda vidaḥ mukhyāḥ veda ācāryāḥ ca kalpitāḥ pravṛtti dharmiṇaḥ ca eva prājāpatyena kalpitāḥ ayam kriyāvatām panthāḥ vyaktībhūtaḥ sanātanaḥ sanatkumāraḥ kapilaḥ saptamaḥ ca sanātanaḥ sapta ete mānasāḥ proktāḥ ṛṣayaḥ brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ svayam āgata vijñānāḥ nivṛttam dharmam āsthitāḥ ācāryāḥ mokṣa śāstre ca mokṣa dharma pravartakāḥ yatas aham prasṛtaḥ pūrvam avyaktāt triguṇaḥ mahān saḥ aham kriyāvatām panthāḥ punarāvṛtti durlabhaḥ pravṛttau vā nivṛttau vā tad phalam saḥ aśnute avaśaḥ eṣa mātā pitā ca eva yuṣmākam ca pitāmahaḥ mayā anuśiṣṭaḥ bhavitā sarva bhūta vara pradaḥ asya ca eva anujaḥ rudraḥ lalāṭāt yaḥ samutthitaḥ brahma anuśiṣṭaḥ bhavitā sarvatra sa vara pradaḥ gacchadhvam svān adhīkārān cintayadhvam yathāvidhi pravartantām kriyāḥ sarvāḥ sarva lokeṣu māciram pradṛśyantām ca karmāṇi prāṇinām gatayaḥ tathā parinirmita kālāni āyūṃṣi ca sura uttamāḥ idam kṛta yugam nāma kālaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ pravartate tatas vai dvāparam nāma miśraḥ kālaḥ bhaviṣyati devāḥ ūcuḥ śrī bhagavān uvāca yatra vedāḥ ca yajñāḥ ca tapaḥ satyam damaḥ tathā ahiṃsā dharma saṃyuktāḥ pracareyuḥ sura uttamāḥ sa vai deśaḥ sevitavyaḥ mā vaḥ adharmaḥ padā spṛśet vyāsaḥ uvāca te anuśiṣṭāḥ bhagavatā devāḥ sa ṛṣi gaṇāḥ tathā tam devaḥ darśayām āsa kṛtvā haya śiraḥ mahat sa aṅgān āvartayan vedān tatas aśvaśirasam dṛṣṭvā tam devam amita ojasam lokakartā prabhuḥ brahmā lokānām hita kāmyayā mūrdhnā praṇamya vara dam tasthau prāñjaliḥ agratas dhātā tvam sarva bhūtānām tvam prabhuḥ jagataḥ guruḥ tvayi āveśita bhāraḥ aham dhṛtim prāpsyāmi atha añjasā yadā ca sura kāryam te aviṣahyam bhaviṣyati prādurbhāvam gamiṣyāmi tadā ātma jñāna deśikaḥ tena anuśiṣṭaḥ brahmā api svam lokam acirāt gataḥ evam eṣa mahābhāgaḥ padmanābhaḥ sanātanaḥ yajñeṣu agra haraḥ proktaḥ yajña dhārī ca nityadā nivṛttim ca āsthitaḥ dharmam gatim akṣaya dharmiṇām saḥ ādiḥ sa madhyaḥ sa ca antaḥ prajānām tasmai namadhvam devāya nirguṇāya guṇa ātmane ajāya viśvarūpāya dhāmne sarva divaukasām mahābhūta adhipataye rudrāṇām pataye tathā aśvibhyām pataye ca eva marutām pataye tathā śāntaye sarva bhūtānām mokṣa dharma anubhāṣiṇe vācaḥ ca pataye nityam saritām pataye tathā kapardine varāhāya ekaśṛṅgāya dhīmate guhyāya jñāna dṛśyāya akṣarāya kṣarāya ca evam etat purā dṛṣṭam mayā vai jñānacakṣuṣā kathitam tat ca vaḥ sarvam mayā pṛṣṭena tattvataḥ kriyatām mad vacaḥ śiṣyāḥ sevyatām hariḥ īśvaraḥ gīyatām veda śabdaiḥ ca pūjyatām ca yathāvidhi vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca sarve śiṣyāḥ sutaḥ ca asya śukaḥ parama dharma vid sa ca asmākam upādhyāyaḥ saha asmābhiḥ viśām pate etat te sarvam ākhyātam yat mām tvam paripṛcchasi yaḥ ca idam śṛṇuyāt nityam yaḥ ca idam parikīrtayet kāma kāmī labhet kāmam dīrgham āyuḥ avāpnuyāt brāhmaṇaḥ sarva vedī syāt kṣatriyaḥ vijayī bhavet vaiśyaḥ vipula lābhaḥ syāt śūdraḥ sukham avāpnuyāt idam mahā ṛṣeḥ vacanam viniścitam mahātmanaḥ puruṣa varasya kīrtanam samāgamam ca ṛṣi divaukasām imam niśamya bhaktāḥ su sukham labhante astauṣīt yaiḥ imam vyāsaḥ sa śiṣyaḥ madhusūdanam vaktum arhasi śuśrūṣoḥ prajāpati pateḥ hareḥ śrutvā bhaveyam yat pūtaḥ śarad candraḥ iva amalaḥ vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca śṛṇu rājan yathā ācaṣṭa phalgunasya hariḥ vibhuḥ prasanna ātmā ātmanaḥ nāmnām niruktam guṇa karma jam pṛṣṭavān keśavam rājan phalgunaḥ para vīra hā yāni nāmāni te deva kīrtitāni mahā ṛṣibhiḥ vedeṣu sa purāṇeṣu yāni guhyāni karmabhiḥ teṣām niruktam tvattaḥ aham śrotum icchāmi keśava śrī bhagavān uvāca bahūni mama nāmāni kīrtitāni mahā ṛṣibhiḥ gauṇāni tatra nāmāni karma jāni ca kāni cit niruktam karma jānām ca śṛṇuṣva prayataḥ anagha kathyamānam mayā tāta tvam hi me ardham smṛtaḥ purā nārāyaṇāya viśvāya nirguṇāya guṇa ātmane aṣṭādaśaguṇam yat tat sattvam sattvavatām vara prakṛtiḥ sā parā mahyam rodasī yoga dhāriṇī ṛtā satyā amarā ajayyā lokānām ātma saṃjñitā tatas yajñaḥ ca yaṣṭā ca purāṇaḥ puruṣaḥ virāj ahnaḥ kṣaye lalāṭāt ca sutaḥ devasya vai tathā krodha āviṣṭasya saṃjajñe rudraḥ saṃhāra kārakaḥ tad ādeśita panthānau sṛṣṭi saṃhāra kārakau nārāyaṇa ātmakaḥ jñeyaḥ pāṇḍaveya yuge yuge saṃpūjitaḥ bhavet pārtha devaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ aham ātmā hi lokānām viśvānām pāṇḍu nandana tasmāt ātmānam eva agre rudram saṃpūjayāmi aham yadi aham na arcayeyam vai īśānam vara dam śivam ātmānam na arcayet kaḥ cit iti me bhāvitam manaḥ mayā pramāṇam hi kṛtam lokaḥ samanuvartate pramāṇāni hi pūjyāni tatas tam pūjayāmi aham rudraḥ nārāyaṇaḥ ca eva sattvam ekam dvidhākṛtam iti saṃcintya manasā purāṇam viśvam īśvaram putra artham ārādhitavān ātmānam aham ātmanā sa brahmakāḥ sa rudrāḥ ca sa indrāḥ devāḥ saha ṛṣibhiḥ arcayanti suraśreṣṭham devam nārāyaṇam harim bhaviṣyatām vartatām ca bhūtānām ca eva bhārata sarveṣām agraṇīḥ viṣṇuḥ sevyaḥ pūjyaḥ ca nityaśas namasva havya dam viṣṇum tathā śaraṇa dam nama teṣām ekāntinaḥ śreṣṭhāḥ te ca eva an anya devatāḥ aham eva gatiḥ teṣām nirāśīḥ karma kāriṇām ye ca śiṣṭāḥ trayaḥ bhaktāḥ phala kāmāḥ hi te matāḥ sarve cyavana dharmāṇaḥ pratibuddhaḥ tu śreṣṭha bhāj brahmāṇam śitikaṇṭham ca yāḥ ca anyāḥ devatāḥ smṛtāḥ bhaktam prati viśeṣaḥ te eṣa pārtha anukīrtitaḥ tvam ca eva aham ca kaunteya nara nārāyaṇau smṛtau bhāra avataraṇa artham hi praviṣṭau mānuṣīm tanum jānāmi adhyātma yogān ca yaḥ aham yasmāt ca bhārata narāṇām ayanam khyātam aham ekaḥ sanātanaḥ āpaḥ nārāḥ iti proktāḥ āpaḥ vai nara sūnavaḥ chādayāmi jagat viśvam bhūtvā sūryaḥ iva aṃśubhiḥ gatiḥ ca sarva bhūtānām prajānām ca api bhārata vyāptā me rodasī pārtha kāntiḥ ca abhyadhikā mama adhibhūtāni ca ante aham tat icchan ca asmi bhārata kramaṇāt ca api aham pārtha viṣṇuḥ iti abhisaṃjñitaḥ damāt siddhim parīpsantaḥ mām janāḥ kāmayanti hi pṛśniḥ iti ucyate ca annam vedāḥ āpaḥ amṛtam tathā ṛṣayaḥ prāhuḥ evam mām tritakūpa abhipātitam pṛśni garbha tritam pāhi iti ekata dvita pātitam tatas sa brahmaṇaḥ putraḥ ādyaḥ ṛṣi varaḥ tritaḥ uttatāra udapānāt vai pṛśnigarbha anukīrtanāt aṃśavaḥ ye prakāśante mama te keśa saṃjñitāḥ sarva jñāḥ keśavam tasmāt mām āhuḥ dvijasattamāḥ bṛhaspatiḥ atha avindat tām patnīm tasya bhārata tatas vai tam ṛṣi śreṣṭham maithuna upagatam tathā pūrva āgataḥ aham vara da na arhasi ambām prabādhitum etat bṛhaspatiḥ śrutvā cukrodha ca śaśāpa ca tasmāt andhaḥ jāsyasi tvam mad śāpāt na atra saṃśayaḥ sa śāpāt ṛṣi mukhyasya dīrgham tamaḥ upeyivān sa hi dīrghatamāḥ nāma nāmnā hi āsīt ṛṣiḥ purā vedān avāpya caturaḥ sa aṅga upāṅgān sanātanān ānupūrvyeṇa vidhinā keśava iti punar punar devānām atha sarveṣām ṛṣīṇām ca mahātmanām agnīṣoma ātmakam tasmāt jagat kṛtsnam carācaram eka yoni ātmakau agnīṣomau devāḥ ca agni mukhāḥ iti eṣa me saṃśayaḥ jātaḥ tam chindhi madhusūdana śrī bhagavān uvāca hanta te vartayiṣyāmi purāṇam pāṇḍu nandana ātma teja udbhavam pārtha śṛṇuṣva ekamanāḥ mama tamaḥ iti eva abhibhūte asaṃjñake advitīye pratiṣṭhite etasyām avasthāyām nārāyaṇa guṇa āśrayāt akṣayāt ajarāt anindriyāt agrāhyāt asaṃbhavāt satyāt ahiṃsrāt lalāmāt vividha pravṛtti viśeṣāt akṣayāt ajara amarāt amūrtitaḥ sarva vyāpinaḥ sarva kartuḥ śāśvatāt tamasaḥ puruṣaḥ prādurbhūtaḥ hariḥ avyayaḥ na āsīt ahaḥ na rātriḥ āsīt na sat āsīt na asat āsīt sā viśvasya jananī iti evam asya arthaḥ anubhāṣyate tasya idānīm tamaḥ saṃbhavasya puruṣasya padmayoneḥ brahmaṇaḥ prādurbhāve sa puruṣaḥ prajāḥ sisṛkṣamāṇaḥ netrābhyām agnīṣomau sasarja tatas bhūta sarge pravṛtte prajā krama vaśāt brahma kṣatram upātiṣṭhat brāhmaṇebhyaḥ param bhūtam na utpanna pūrvam dīpyamāne agnau juhoti iti kṛtvā bravīmi bhūta sargaḥ kṛtaḥ brahmaṇā bhūtāni ca pratiṣṭhāpya trailokyam dhāryate iti tvam agne yajñānām hotā viśveṣām viśveṣām agne yajñānām hotā iti agniḥ hi yajñānām hotā kartā na vinā puruṣam tapaḥ saṃbhavati haviḥ mantrāṇām saṃpūjā vidyate deva manuṣyāṇām anena tvam hotā iti niyuktaḥ ye ca mānuṣāḥ hotrā adhikārāḥ te ca brāhmaṇasya hi yājanam vidhīyate na kṣatra vaiśyayoḥ dvijātyoḥ tasmāt brāhmaṇāḥ hi agni bhūtāḥ yajñān udvahanti yajñāḥ devān tarpayanti devāḥ pṛthivīm bhāvayanti evam api agni bhūtāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ vidvāṃsaḥ agnim bhāvayanti agniḥ viṣṇuḥ sarva bhūtāni anupraviśya prāṇān dhārayati api ca atra sanatkumāra gītāḥ ślokāḥ bhavanti viśvam brahmā asṛjat pūrvam sarva ādiḥ niravaskaram brāhmaṇānām matiḥ vākyam karma śraddhā tapāṃsi ca dhārayanti mahīm dyām ca śaityāt vāri amṛtam yathā na asti satyāt paraḥ dharmaḥ na asti mātṛ samaḥ guruḥ na eṣām ukṣā vardhate na uta vāhā apadhvastāḥ dasyu bhūtāḥ bhavanti yeṣām rāṣṭre brāhmaṇāḥ vṛtti hīnāḥ veda purāṇa itihāsa prāmāṇyāt nārāyaṇa mukha udgatāḥ sarva ātmānaḥ sarva kartāraḥ sarva bhāvanāḥ ca brāhmaṇāḥ vāc sama kālam hi tasya devasya vara pradasya brāhmaṇāḥ prathamam prādurbhūtāḥ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ ca śeṣāḥ varṇāḥ prādurbhūtāḥ ittham ca sura asura viśiṣṭāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ yadā mayā brahma bhūtena purā svayam eva utpāditāḥ sura asura mahā ṛṣayaḥ bhūta viśeṣāḥ sthāpitāḥ nigṛhītāḥ ca ahalyā dharṣaṇa nimittam hi gautamāt hari śmaśru tām indraḥ prāptaḥ kauśika nimittam ca indraḥ muṣka viyogam meṣa vṛṣaṇa tvam ca avāpa kratu vadha prāpta manyunā ca dakṣeṇa bhūyas tapasā ca ātmānam saṃyojya netra ākṛtiḥ anyā lalāṭe rudrasya utpāditā tripura vadha artham dīkṣām abhyupagatasya rudrasya uśanasā śirasaḥ jaṭāḥ utkṛtya prayuktāḥ tatas prādurbhūtāḥ bhujagāḥ taiḥ asya bhujagaiḥ pīḍyamānaḥ kaṇṭhaḥ nīla tām upanītaḥ pūrve ca manvantare svāyaṃbhuve nārāyaṇa hasta bandha grahaṇāt nīlakaṇṭha tvam eva vā amṛta utpādane puraścaraṇa tām upagatasya aṅgirasaḥ bṛhaspateḥ upaspṛśataḥ na prasādam gatavatyaḥ kila apaḥ yasmāt mama upaspṛśataḥ kaluṣībhūtāḥ na prasādam upagatāḥ tasmāt adya prabhṛti jhaṣa makara matsya kacchapa jantu saṃkīrṇāḥ kaluṣībhavata iti tadā prabhṛti āpaḥ yādobhiḥ saṃkīrṇāḥ saṃvṛttāḥ viśvarūpaḥ vai tvāṣṭraḥ purohitaḥ devānām āsīt svasrīyaḥ asurāṇām atha hiraṇyakaśipum puraskṛtya viśvarūpa mātaram svasāram asurāḥ varam ayācanta he svasar ayam te putraḥ tvāṣṭraḥ viśvarūpaḥ triśirāḥ devānām purohitaḥ pratyakṣam devebhyaḥ bhāgam adadat parokṣam asmākam tatas devāḥ vardhante vayam kṣīyāmaḥ putra kim para pakṣa vardhanaḥ tvam mātula pakṣam nāśayasi sa viśvarūpaḥ mātuḥ vākyam an atikramaṇīyam iti matvā saṃpūjya hiraṇyakaśipum agāt hairaṇyagarbhāt ca vasiṣṭhāt hiraṇyakaśipuḥ śāpam prāptavān yasmāt tvayā anyaḥ vṛtaḥ hotā tasmāt a samāpta yajñaḥ tvam apūrvāt sattva jātāt vadham prāpsyasi iti tad śāpa dānāt hiraṇyakaśipuḥ prāptavān vadham tāḥ ca dṛṣṭvā manaḥ kṣubhitam tasya abhavat tāsu ca apsaraḥsu nacirāt eva saktaḥ abhavat saktam ca enam jñātvā apsarasaḥ ūcuḥ gacchāmahe vayam yathāgatam iti tāḥ tvāṣṭraḥ uvāca kva gamiṣyathaḥ āsyatām tāvat mayā saha śreyaḥ bhaviṣyati iti vayam deva striyaḥ apsarasaḥ indram vara dam purā prabhaviṣṇum vṛṇīmahe iti atha tāḥ viśvarūpaḥ abravīt adya eva sa indrāḥ devāḥ na bhaviṣyanti iti tatas mantrān jajāpa taiḥ mantraiḥ prāvardhata triśirāḥ athā indraḥ tam vivardhamānam soma pāna āpyāyita sarva gātram dṛṣṭvā cintām āpede devāḥ ca te saha indreṇa brahmāṇam abhijagmuḥ ūcuḥ ca viśvarūpeṇa sarva yajñeṣu su hutaḥ somaḥ pīyate vayam a bhāgāḥ saṃvṛttāḥ asura pakṣaḥ vardhate vayam kṣīyāmaḥ tān brahmā uvāca ṛṣiḥ bhārgavaḥ tapaḥ tapyate dadhīcaḥ sa yācyatām varam yathā kalevaram jahyāt tān dadhīcaḥ uvāca svāgatam bhavadbhyaḥ kim kriyatām yat vakṣyatha tat kariṣyāmi iti atha dadhīcaḥ tathā eva avimanāḥ sukha duḥkha samaḥ mahā yogī ātmānam samādhāya śarīra parityāgam cakāra tena vajreṇa abhedyena apradhṛṣyeṇa brahma asthi saṃbhūtena viṣṇu praviṣṭena indraḥ viśvarūpam jaghāna śirasām ca asya chedanam akarot tasmāt anantaram viśvarūpa gātra mathana saṃbhavam tvaṣṭrā utpāditam eva arim vṛtram indraḥ jaghāna tasyām dvaidhībhūtāyām brahma vadhyāyām bhayāt indraḥ deva rājyam parityajya apsu śītalām mānasa saraḥ gatām nalinīm prapede devān rajaḥ tamaḥ ca āviveśa mantrāḥ na prāvartanta mahā ṛṣīṇām rakṣāṃsi prādurabhavan an indrāḥ ca abalāḥ lokāḥ su pradhṛṣyāḥ babhūvuḥ atha devāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca āyuṣaḥ putram nahuṣam nāma deva rāja tve abhiṣiṣicuḥ nahuṣaḥ pañcabhiḥ śataiḥ jyotiṣām lalāṭe jvaladbhiḥ sarva tejaḥ haraiḥ triviṣṭapam pālayām babhūva atha lokāḥ prakṛtim āpedire svasthāḥ ca babhūvuḥ atha uvāca nahuṣaḥ sarvam mām śakra upabhuktam upasthitam ṛte śacīm iti saḥ evam uktvā śacī samīpam agamat uvāca ca enām tam śacī pratyuvāca prakṛtyā tvam dharma vatsalaḥ soma vaṃśa udbhavaḥ ca tām atha uvāca nahuṣaḥ sā tam uvāca atha śacī duḥkha śoka ārtā bhartṛ darśana lālasā nahuṣa bhaya gṛhītā bṛhaspatim upāgacchat sa ca tām abhigatām dṛṣṭvā eva dhyānam praviśya bhartṛ kārya tatparām jñātvā bṛhaspatiḥ uvāca sā tava indram darśayiṣyati iti sā atha mahāniyamam āsthitā devīm vara dām upaśrutim mantraiḥ āhvayat sā upaśrutiḥ śacī samīpam agāt kim te priyam karavāṇi iti tām mūrdhnā praṇamya uvāca śacī bhagavati arhasi me bhartāram darśayitum tvam satyā matā ca iti sā enām mānasam saraḥ anayat tām indraḥ patnīm kṛśām glānām ca dṛṣṭvā babhūva naṣṭam hi mām iyam anviṣya upāgamat duḥkha ārtā iti sā tam uvāca nahuṣaḥ mām āhvayati kālaḥ ca asya mayā kṛtaḥ iti tām indraḥ uvāca nahuṣaḥ tvayā vācyaḥ apūrveṇa mām ṛṣi yuktena yānena tvam adhirūḍhaḥ udvahasva indrasya hi mahānti vāhanāni manasaḥ priyāṇi adhirūḍhāni mayā sā evam uktā hṛṣṭā jagāma atha indrāṇīm abhyāgatām dṛṣṭvā uvāca nahuṣaḥ pūrṇaḥ sa kālaḥ iti sa mahā ṛṣi yuktam vāhanam adhirūḍhaḥ śacī samīpam upāgacchat atha maitrāvaruṇiḥ kumbhayoniḥ agastyaḥ mahā ṛṣīn vikriyamāṇān tān nahuṣeṇa apaśyat padbhyām ca tena aspṛśyata sa mahā ṛṣi vākya sama kālam eva tasmāt yānāt avāpatat tatas devāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca bhagavantam viṣṇum śaraṇam indra arthe abhijagmuḥ ūcuḥ ca enam bhagavan indram brahma vadhyā abhibhūtam trātum arhasi iti tatas sa vara daḥ tān abravīt aśvamedham yajñam vaiṣṇavam śakraḥ abhiyajatu tatas svam sthānam prāpsyati iti tatas devāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca indram na apaśyan yadā tadā śacīm ūcuḥ gaccha subhage indram ānayasva iti bṛhaspatiḥ ca aśvamedham mahā kratum śakrāya aharat tatas kṛṣṇasāraṅgam medhyam aśvam utsṛjya vāhanam tam eva kṛtvā indram marutpatim bṛhaspatiḥ sva sthānam prāpayām āsa tatas sa devarāj devaiḥ ṛṣibhiḥ stūyamānaḥ triviṣṭapa sthaḥ niṣkalmaṣaḥ babhūva evam indraḥ brahma tejaḥ prabhāva upabṛṃhitaḥ śatru vadham kṛtvā sva sthānam prāpitaḥ ākāśagaṅgā gataḥ ca purā bharadvājaḥ mahā ṛṣiḥ upāspṛśan trīn kramān kramatā viṣṇunā abhyāsāditaḥ sa bharadvājena sa salilena pāṇinā urasi tāḍitaḥ sa lakṣaṇa uraskaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ bhṛguṇā mahā ṛṣiṇā śaptaḥ agniḥ sarva bhakṣa tvam upanītaḥ aditim ca avocat bhikṣām dehi iti tatra devaiḥ pūrvam etat prāśyam na anyena iti aditiḥ bhikṣām na adāt atha bhikṣā pratyākhyāna ruṣitena budhena brahma bhūtena vivasvataḥ dvitīye janmani aṇḍa saṃjñitasya aṇḍam māritam adityāḥ sa mārtaṇḍaḥ vivasvān abhavat śrāddhadevaḥ dakṣasya vai duhitaraḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ āsan tābhyaḥ kaśyapāya trayodaśa prādāt daśa dharmāya daśa manave saptaviṃśatim indave tāsu tulyāsu nakṣatra ākhyām gatāsu somaḥ rohiṇyām abhyadhikām prītim akarot tatas tāḥ śeṣāḥ patnyaḥ īrṣyāvatyaḥ pituḥ samīpam gatvā imam artham śaśaṃsuḥ saḥ abravīt yakṣmā enam āvekṣyati iti dakṣa śāpāt somam rājānam yakṣmā āviveśa sa yakṣmaṇā āviṣṭaḥ dakṣam agamat tatra ṛṣayaḥ somam abruvan kṣīyase yakṣmaṇā snātvā ca ātmānam pāpmanaḥ mokṣayām āsa tatra ca avabhāsitaḥ tīrthe yadā somaḥ tadā prabhṛti tīrtham tat prabhāsam iti nāmnā khyātam babhūva tad śāpāt adya api kṣīyate somaḥ amāvāsyā antara sthaḥ tasya tapaḥ tapyamānasya sarva gandha vahaḥ śuciḥ vāyuḥ vivāyamānaḥ śarīram aspṛśat sa tapasā tāpita śarīraḥ kṛśaḥ vāyunā upavījyamānaḥ hṛdaya paritoṣam agamat nārāyaṇaḥ loka hita artham vaḍavāmukhaḥ nāma mahā ṛṣiḥ purā bhavat tena amarṣitena ātma gātra ūṣmaṇā samudraḥ stimita jalaḥ kṛtaḥ sveda prasyandana sadṛśaḥ ca asya lavaṇa bhāvaḥ janitaḥ etat ca te toyam vaḍavāmukha saṃjñitena pīyamānam madhuram bhaviṣyati tat etat adya api vaḍavāmukha saṃjñitena anuvartinā toyam sāmudram pīyate bhṛguḥ api ca mahā ṛṣiḥ himavantam āgamya abravīt kanyām umām me dehi iti tam abravīt bhṛguḥ yasmāt tvayā aham kanyā varaṇa kṛta bhāvaḥ pratyākhyātaḥ tasmāt na ratnānām bhavān bhājanam bhaviṣyati iti tat evaṃvidham māhātmyam brāhmaṇānām kṣatram api śāśvatīm avyayām pṛthivīm patnīm abhigamya bubhuje tat etat brahma agnīṣomīyam śrī bhagavān uvāca sūryācandramasau śaśvat keśaiḥ me aṃśu saṃjñitaiḥ bodhayan tāpayan ca eva jagat uttiṣṭhataḥ pṛthak bodhanāt tāpanāt ca eva jagataḥ harṣaṇam bhavet agnīṣoma kṛtaiḥ ebhiḥ karmabhiḥ pāṇḍu nandana hṛṣīkeśaḥ aham īśānaḥ vara daḥ loka bhāvanaḥ varṇaḥ ca me hari śreṣṭhaḥ tasmāt hariḥ aham smṛtaḥ dhāma sāraḥ hi lokānām ṛtam ca eva vicāritam ṛtadhāmā tatas vipraiḥ satyaḥ ca aham prakīrtitaḥ naṣṭām ca dharaṇīm pūrvam avindam vai guhā gatām govindaḥ iti mām devāḥ vāgbhiḥ samabhituṣṭuvuḥ śipiviṣṭa iti ca ākhyāyām hīna romā ca yaḥ bhavet tena āviṣṭam hi yat kim cit śipiviṣṭam hi tat smṛtam yāskaḥ mām ṛṣiḥ avyagraḥ na eka yajñeṣu gītavān stutvā mām śipiviṣṭa iti yāskaḥ ṛṣiḥ udāra dhīḥ kṣetrajñaḥ sarva bhūtānām tasmāt aham ajaḥ smṛtaḥ na ukta pūrvam mayā kṣudram aślīlam vā kadā cana ṛtā brahma sutā sā me satyā devī sarasvatī pauṣkare brahma sadane satyam mām ṛṣayaḥ viduḥ nirāśīḥ karma saṃyuktam sātvatam mām prakalpaya sātvata jñāna dṛṣṭaḥ aham sātvataḥ sātvatām patiḥ kṛṣāmi medinīm pārtha bhūtvā kārṣṇāyasaḥ mahān kṛṣṇaḥ varṇaḥ ca me yasmāt tasmāt kṛṣṇaḥ aham arjuna mayā saṃśleṣitā bhūmiḥ adbhiḥ vyoma ca vāyunā vāyuḥ ca tejasā sārdham vaikuṇṭha tvam tatas mama tayoḥ saṃdhāraṇa artham hi mām adhokṣajam añjasā niruktam veda viduṣaḥ ye ca śabda artha cintakāḥ te mām gāyanti prāc vaṃśe adhokṣajaḥ iti sthitiḥ śabdaḥ eka mataiḥ eṣa vyāhṛtaḥ parama ṛṣibhiḥ na anyaḥ hi adhokṣajaḥ loke ṛte nārāyaṇam prabhum ghṛtam mama arciṣaḥ loke jantūnām prāṇa dhāraṇam trayaḥ hi dhātavaḥ khyātāḥ karma jāḥ iti ca smṛtāḥ pittam śleṣmā ca vāyuḥ ca eṣa saṃghātaḥ ucyate etaiḥ ca dhāryate jantuḥ etaiḥ kṣīṇaiḥ ca kṣīyate āyurveda vidaḥ tasmāt tridhātum mām pracakṣate vṛṣaḥ hi bhagavān dharmaḥ khyātaḥ lokeṣu bhārata naighaṇṭuka pada ākhyātam viddhi mām vṛṣam uttamam kapiḥ varāhaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ ca dharmaḥ ca vṛṣaḥ ucyate tasmāt vṛṣākapim prāha kaśyapaḥ mām prajāpatiḥ na ca ādim na madhyam tathā na eva ca antam kadā cit surāḥ ca asurāḥ ca anādyaḥ hi amadhyaḥ tathā ca api anantaḥ pragītaḥ aham īśaḥ vibhuḥ lokasākṣī śucīni śravaṇīyāni śṛṇomi iha dhanaṃjaya na ca pāpāni gṛhṇāmi tatas aham vai śuciśravāḥ eka śṛṅgaḥ purā bhūtvā varāhaḥ divya darśanaḥ imām uddhṛtavān bhūmim ekaśṛṅgaḥ tatas hi aham tathā eva āsam tri kakudaḥ vārāham rūpam āsthitaḥ trikakud tena vikhyātaḥ śarīrasya tu māpanāt viriñcaḥ iti yaḥ proktaḥ kapila jñāna cintakaiḥ vidyā sahāyavantam mām āditya stham sanātanam kapilam prāhuḥ ācāryāḥ sāṃkhyāḥ niścita niścayāḥ yogaiḥ saṃpūjyate nityam saḥ eva aham vibhuḥ smṛtaḥ ekaviṃśati śākham ca ṛgvedam mām pracakṣate sahasra śākham yat sāma ye vai veda vidaḥ janāḥ gāyanti āraṇyake viprāḥ mad bhaktāḥ te api durlabhāḥ ṣaṭpañcāśatam aṣṭau ca saptatriṃśatam iti uta yasmin śākhāḥ yajurvede saḥ aham ādhvaryave smṛtaḥ pañca kalpam atharvāṇam kṛtyābhiḥ paribṛṃhitam kalpayanti hi mām viprāḥ atharvāṇa vidaḥ tathā śākhā bhedāḥ ca ye ke cit yāḥ ca śākhāsu gītayaḥ svara varṇa samuccārāḥ sarvān tān viddhi mad kṛtān rāma ādeśita mārgeṇa mad prasādāt mahātmanā pāñcālena kramaḥ prāptaḥ tasmāt bhūtāt sanātanāt nārāyaṇāt varam labdhvā prāpya yogam anuttamam kramam praṇīya śikṣām ca praṇayitvā sa gālavaḥ kaṇḍarīkaḥ atha rājā ca brahmadattaḥ pratāpavān jātī maraṇa jam duḥkham smṛtvā smṛtvā punar punar sapta jātiṣu mukhya tvāt yogānām saṃpadam gataḥ purā aham ātmajaḥ pārtha prathitaḥ kāraṇa antare dharmasya kuru śārdūla tatas aham dharmajaḥ smṛtaḥ dharma yānam samārūḍhau parvate gandhamādane tat śūlam bhasmasāt kṛtvā dakṣa yajñam sa vistaram āvayoḥ sahasā agacchat badaryāśramam antikāt tatas sva tejasā āviṣṭāḥ keśāḥ nārāyaṇasya ha babhūvuḥ muñja varṇāḥ tu tatas aham muñja keśavān tat ca śūlam vinirdhūtam huṃkāreṇa mahātmanā jagāma śaṃkara karam nārāyaṇa samāhatam atha rudraḥ upādhāvat tau ṛṣī tapasā anvitau tatas enam samuddhūtam kaṇṭhe jagrāha pāṇinā nārāyaṇaḥ sa viśvātmā tena asya śitikaṇṭha tā atha rudra vighāta artham iṣīkām jagṛhe naraḥ kṣiptaḥ ca sahasā rudre khaṇḍanam prāptavān tadā tatas aham khaṇḍaparaśuḥ smṛtaḥ paraśu khaṇḍanāt jayam kaḥ prāptavān tatra śaṃsa etat me janārdana śrī bhagavān uvāca tayoḥ saṃlagnayoḥ yuddhe rudra nārāyaṇa ātmanoḥ udvignāḥ sahasā kṛtsnāḥ lokāḥ sarve abhavan tadā na agṛhṇāt pāvakaḥ śubhram makheṣu su hutam haviḥ vedāḥ na pratibhānti smaḥ ṛṣīṇām bhāvitātmanām niṣprabhāṇi ca tejāṃsi brahmā ca eva āsanāt cyutaḥ agāt śoṣam samudraḥ ca himavān ca vyaśīryata brahmā vṛtaḥ deva gaṇaiḥ ṛṣibhiḥ ca mahātmabhiḥ ājagāma āśu tam deśam yatra yuddham avartata uvāca vacanam rudram lokānām astu vai śivam nyasya āyudhāni viśveśa jagataḥ hita kāmyayā yat akṣaram atha avyaktam īśam lokasya bhāvanam kūṭastham kartṛ nirdvaṃdvam akartā iti ca yam viduḥ vyakti bhāva gatasya asya ekā mūrtiḥ iyam śivā tapasā mahatā yuktau deva śreṣṭhau mahā vratau aham prasāda jaḥ tasya kasmin cit kāraṇa antare mayā ca sārdham vara dam vibudhaiḥ ca mahā ṛṣibhiḥ prasādaya āśu lokānām śāntiḥ bhavatu māciram prasādayām āsa tatas devam nārāyaṇam prabhum śaraṇam ca jagāma ādyam vareṇyam vara dam harim ṛṣibhiḥ brahmaṇā ca eva vibudhaiḥ ca su pūjitaḥ uvāca devam īśānam īśaḥ sa jagataḥ hariḥ yaḥ tvām vetti sa mām vetti yaḥ tvām anu sa mām anu adya prabhṛti śrīvatsaḥ śūla aṅkaḥ ayam bhavatu ayam mama pāṇi aṅkitaḥ ca api śrīkaṇṭhaḥ tvam bhaviṣyasi evam lakṣaṇam utpādya paraspara kṛtam tadā sakhyam ca eva atulam kṛtvā rudreṇa sahitau ṛṣī eṣa te kathitaḥ pārtha nārāyaṇa jayaḥ mṛdhe ṛṣibhiḥ kathitāni iha yāni saṃkīrtitāni te evam bahuvidhaiḥ rūpaiḥ carāmi iha vasuṃdharām mayā tvam rakṣitaḥ yuddhe mahāntam prāptavān jayam nihatān tena vai pūrvam hatavān asi vai ripūn idam śata sahasrāt hi bhārata ākhyāna vistarāt navanītam yathā dadhnaḥ malayāt candanam yathā āraṇyakam ca vedebhyaḥ oṣadhibhyaḥ amṛtam yathā tapaḥ nidhe tvayā uktam hi nārāyaṇa kathā āśrayam sa hi īśaḥ bhagavān devaḥ sarva bhūta ātma bhāvanaḥ aho nārāyaṇam tejaḥ durdarśam dvijasattama yatra āviśanti kalpa ante sarve brahma ādayaḥ surāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca sa gandharvāḥ yat ca kim cit carācaram sarva āśrama abhigamanam sarva tīrtha avagāhanam na tathā phala dam ca api nārāyaṇa kathā yathā sarvathā pāvitāḥ sma iha śrutvā imām āditas kathām hareḥ viśveśvarasya iha sarva pāpa praṇāśanīm na citram kṛtavān tatra yat āryaḥ me dhanaṃjayaḥ vāsudeva sahāyaḥ yaḥ prāptavān jayam uttamam na ca asya kim cit a prāpyam manye lokeṣu api triṣu trailokya nāthaḥ viṣṇuḥ sa yasya āsīt sāhya kṛt sakhā dhanyāḥ ca sarve eva āsan brahman te mama pūrvakāḥ hitāya śreyase ca eva yeṣām āsīt janārdanaḥ tapasā api na dṛśyaḥ hi bhagavān loka pūjitaḥ yam dṛṣṭavantaḥ te sākṣāt śrīvatsa aṅka vibhūṣaṇam śvetadvīpam samāsādya yena dṛṣṭaḥ svayam hariḥ badarīm āśramam yat tu nāradaḥ prādravat punar nara nārāyaṇau draṣṭum kim nu tad kāraṇam mune śvetadvīpāt nivṛttaḥ ca nāradaḥ parameṣṭhi jaḥ badarīm āśramam prāpya samāgamya ca tau ṛṣī kiyantam kālam avasat kāḥ kathāḥ pṛṣṭavān ca saḥ śvetadvīpāt upāvṛtte tasmin vā su mahātmani kim abrūtām mahātmānau nara nārāyaṇau ṛṣī vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca yasya prasādāt vakṣyāmi nārāyaṇa kathām imām prāpya śvetam mahā dvīpam dṛṣṭvā ca harim avyayam nivṛttaḥ nāradaḥ rājan tarasā merum āgamat hṛdayena udvahan bhāram yat uktam parama ātmanā paścāt asya abhavat rājan ātmanaḥ sādhvasam mahat yat gatvā dūram adhvānam kṣemī punar iha āgataḥ nipapāta ca khāt tūrṇam viśālām badarīm anu tatas sa dadṛśe devau purāṇau ṛṣi sattamau śrīvatsa lakṣaṇau pūjyau jaṭā maṇḍala dhāriṇau jāla pāda bhujau tau tu pādayoḥ cakra lakṣaṇau vyūḍha uraskau dīrgha bhujau tathā muṣka catuṣkiṇau ṣaṣṭi dantau aṣṭa daṃṣṭrau megha ogha sadṛśa svanau su āsyau pṛthu lalāṭau ca su hanū subhru nāsikau ātapatreṇa sadṛśe śirasī devayoḥ tayoḥ evam lakṣaṇa saṃpannau mahāpuruṣa saṃjñitau tau dṛṣṭvā nāradaḥ hṛṣṭaḥ tābhyām ca pratipūjitaḥ svāgatena abhibhāṣya atha pṛṣṭaḥ ca anāmayam tadā śvetadvīpe mayā dṛṣṭāḥ tādṛśau ṛṣi sattamau iti saṃcintya manasā kṛtvā ca abhipradakṣiṇam tatas tau tapasām vāsau yaśasām tejasām api ṛṣī śama dama upetau kṛtvā pūrvāhṇikam vidhim paścāt nāradam avyagrau pādya arghyābhyām prapūjya ca pīṭhayoḥ ca upaviṣṭau tau kṛta atithi āhnikau nṛpa teṣu tatra upaviṣṭeṣu sa deśaḥ abhivyarājata ājya āhuti mahā jvālaiḥ yajña vāṭaḥ agnibhiḥ yathā atha nārāyaṇaḥ tatra nāradam vākyam abravīt sukha upaviṣṭam viśrāntam kṛta ātithyam sukha sthitam api idānīm sa bhagavān parama ātmā sanātanaḥ śvetadvīpe tvayā dṛṣṭaḥ āvayoḥ prakṛtiḥ parā nāradaḥ uvāca dṛṣṭaḥ me puruṣaḥ śrīmān viśva rūpa dharaḥ avyayaḥ sarve hi lokāḥ tatra sthāḥ tathā devāḥ saha ṛṣibhiḥ adya api ca enam paśyāmi yuvām paśyan sanātanau dṛṣṭau mayā yuvām tatra tasya devasya pārśvatas iha ca eva āgataḥ asmi adya visṛṣṭaḥ parama ātmanā kaḥ hi nāma bhavet tasya tejasā yaśasā śriyā sadṛśaḥ triṣu lokeṣu ṛte dharma ātmajau yuvām tena me kathitam pūrvam nāma kṣetrajña saṃjñitam prādurbhāvāḥ ca kathitāḥ bhaviṣyanti hi ye yathā tatra ye puruṣāḥ śvetāḥ pañca indriya vivarjitāḥ sa kartā kāraṇam ca eva kāryam ca ati bala dyutiḥ tapasā yojya saḥ ātmānam śvetadvīpāt param hi yat śāntiḥ sā triṣu lokeṣu siddhānām bhāvitātmanām etayā śubhayā buddhyā naiṣṭhikam vratam āsthitaḥ vedīm aṣṭa tala utsedhām bhūmau āsthāya viśvabhuj sa aṅgān āvartayan vedān tapaḥ tepe su duścaram yat brahmāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca eva svayam paśupatiḥ ca yat śeṣāḥ ca vibudha śreṣṭhāḥ daitya dānava rākṣasāḥ nāgāḥ suparṇāḥ gandharvāḥ siddhāḥ rājarṣayaḥ ca ye kṛtsnam tat tasya devasya caraṇau upatiṣṭhati yāḥ kriyāḥ saṃprayuktāḥ tu ekānta gata buddhibhiḥ tāḥ sarvāḥ śirasā devaḥ pratigṛhṇāti vai svayam iha ca eva āgataḥ tena visṛṣṭaḥ parama ātmanā evam me bhagavān devaḥ svayam ākhyātavān hariḥ āsiṣye tad paraḥ bhūtvā yuvābhyām saha nityaśas nara nārāyaṇau ūcatuḥ dhanyaḥ asi anugṛhītaḥ asi yat te dṛṣṭaḥ svayam prabhuḥ na hi tam dṛṣṭavān kaḥ cit padmayoniḥ api svayam tatas svayam darśitavān svam ātmānam dvijottama na tat saṃprāpnute kaḥ cit ṛte hi āvām dvijottama tasmāt uttiṣṭhate vipra devāt viśvabhuvaḥ pateḥ kṣamā kṣamāvatām śreṣṭha yayā bhūmiḥ tu yujyate tasmāt eva samudbhūtam tejaḥ rūpa guṇa ātmakam tasmāt devāt samudbhūtaḥ sparśaḥ tu puruṣottamāt tasmāt ca uttiṣṭhate śabdaḥ sarva loka īśvarāt prabhoḥ ākāśam yujyate yena tatas tiṣṭhati a saṃvṛtam tasmāt ca uttiṣṭhate devāt sarva bhūta gatam manaḥ candramāḥ yena saṃyuktaḥ prakāśa guṇa dhāraṇaḥ ṣaṣ bhūta utpādakam nāma tat sthānam veda saṃjñitam ye hi niṣkalmaṣāḥ loke puṇya pāpa vivarjitāḥ teṣām vai kṣemam adhvānam gacchatām dvijasattama āditya dagdha sarva aṅgāḥ adṛśyāḥ kena cit kva cit paramāṇu bhūtāḥ bhūtvā tu tam devam praviśanti uta pradyumnāt ca api nirmuktāḥ jīvam saṃkarṣaṇam tathā viśanti vipra pravarāḥ sāṃkhyāḥ bhāgavataiḥ saha tatas traiguṇya hīnāḥ te parama ātmānam añjasā praviśanti dvijaśreṣṭha kṣetrajñam nirguṇa ātmakam sarva āvāsam vāsudevam kṣetrajñam viddhi tattvataḥ samāhita manaskāḥ ca niyatāḥ saṃyata indriyāḥ ekānta bhāva upagatāḥ vāsudevam viśanti te ramyām viśālām āśritya tapaḥ ugram samāsthitau vidhinā svena yuktābhyām yathāpūrvam dvijottama āvābhyām api dṛṣṭaḥ tvam śvetadvīpe tapodhana samāgataḥ bhagavatā saṃjalpam kṛtavān yathā yat bhaviṣyati vṛttam vā vartate vā śubha aśubham vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca nāradaḥ prāñjaliḥ bhūtvā nārāyaṇa parāyaṇaḥ jajāpa vidhivat mantrān nārāyaṇa gatān bahūn divyam varṣa sahasram hi nara nārāyaṇa āśrame avasat sa mahā tejāḥ nāradaḥ bhagavān ṛṣiḥ vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca daivam kṛtvā yathānyāyam pitryam cakre tatas param tatas tam vacanam prāha jyeṣṭhaḥ dharma ātmajaḥ prabhuḥ tvayā matimatām śreṣṭha tat me śaṃsa yathāgamam nāradaḥ uvāca daivatam ca paraḥ yajñaḥ parama ātmā sanātanaḥ tasmāt ca prasṛtaḥ pūrvam brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ yajāmi aham pitṝn sādho nārāyaṇa vidhau kṛte evam saḥ eva bhagavān pitā mātā pitāmahaḥ ijyate pitṛ yajñeṣu mayā nityam jagatpatiḥ veda śrutiḥ praṇaṣṭā ca punar adhyāpitā sutaiḥ nūnam purā etat viditam yuvayoḥ bhāvitātmanoḥ trīn piṇḍān nyasya vai pṛthvyām pūrvam dattvā kuśān iti katham tu piṇḍa saṃjñām te pitaraḥ lebhire purā nara nārāyaṇau ūcatuḥ imām hi dharaṇīm pūrvam naṣṭām sāgara mekhalām govindaḥ ujjahāra āśu vārāham rūpam āśritaḥ sthāpayitvā tu dharaṇīm sve sthāne puruṣottamaḥ daṃṣṭrā vilagnān mṛd piṇḍān vidhūya sahasā prabhuḥ sthāpayām āsa vai pṛthvyām kuśān āstīrya nārada saṃkalpayitvā trīn piṇḍān svena eva vidhinā prabhuḥ prokṣya apavargam deveśaḥ prāc mukhaḥ kṛtavān svayam maryādā sthāpana artham ca tatas vacanam uktavān daṃṣṭrābhyām pravinirdhūtāḥ mama ete dakṣiṇām diśam āśritāḥ dharaṇīm piṇḍāḥ tasmāt pitaraḥ eva te trayaḥ mūrti vihīnāḥ vai piṇḍa mūrti dharāḥ tu ime bhavantu pitaraḥ loke mayā sṛṣṭāḥ sanātanāḥ aham eva atra vijñeyaḥ triṣu piṇḍeṣu saṃsthitaḥ iti evam uktvā vacanam devadevaḥ vṛṣākapiḥ varāhaparvate vipra dattvā piṇḍān sa vistarān ātmānam pūjayitvā eva tatra eva adarśanam gataḥ etad artham śubha mate pitaraḥ piṇḍa saṃjñitāḥ labhante satatam pūjām vṛṣākapi vacaḥ yathā ye yajanti pitṝn devān gurūn ca eva atithīn tathā gāḥ ca eva dvijamukhyān ca pṛthivīm mātaram tathā karmaṇā manasā vācā viṣṇum eva yajanti te samaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu īśvaraḥ sukha duḥkhayoḥ mahān mahātmā sarva ātmā nārāyaṇaḥ iti śrutaḥ vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca śrutvā etat nāradaḥ vākyam nara nārāyaṇa īritam proṣya varṣa sahasram tu nara nārāyaṇa āśrame śrutvā bhagavat ākhyānam dṛṣṭvā ca harim avyayam himavantam jagāma āśu yatra asya svakaḥ āśramaḥ tau api khyāta tapasau nara nārāyaṇau ṛṣī tvam api amita vikrāntaḥ pāṇḍavānām kula udvahaḥ pāvita ātmā adya saṃvṛttaḥ śrutvā imām āditas kathām karmaṇā manasā vācā yaḥ dviṣyāt viṣṇum avyayam majjanti pitaraḥ tasya narake śāśvatīḥ samāḥ yaḥ dviṣyāt vibudha śreṣṭham devam nārāyaṇam harim ātmā hi puruṣa vyāghra jñeyaḥ viṣṇuḥ iti sthitiḥ yaḥ eṣa guruḥ asmākam ṛṣiḥ gandhavatī sutaḥ tena etat kathitam tāta māhātmyam parama ātmanaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanam vyāsam viddhi nārāyaṇam prabhum dharmān nānāvidhān ca eva kaḥ brūyāt tam ṛte prabhum vartatām te mahā yajñaḥ yathā saṃkalpitaḥ tvayā saṃkalpita aśvamedhaḥ tvam śruta dharmaḥ ca tattvataḥ etat tu mahat ākhyānam śrutvā pārikṣitaḥ nṛpaḥ tatas yajña samāpti artham kriyāḥ sarvāḥ samārabhat nārāyaṇīyam ākhyānam etat te kathitam mayā ṛṣīṇām pāṇḍavānām ca śṛṇvatoḥ kṛṣṇa bhīṣmayoḥ tapasām nidhiḥ su mahatām mahataḥ yaśasaḥ ca bhājanam ariṣṭaka hā ekāntinām śaraṇa daḥ abhaya daḥ gati daḥ astu vaḥ sa makha bhāga haraḥ triguṇa atigaḥ catuṣpañca dharaḥ pūrta iṣṭayoḥ ca phala bhāga haraḥ vidadhāti nityam ajitaḥ atibalaḥ gatim ātma gām sukṛtinām ṛṣiṇām tam lokasākṣiṇam ajam puruṣam ravi varṇam īśvara gatim bahuśas sa hi loka yoniḥ amṛtasya padam sūkṣmam purāṇam acalam paramam śrutam bhagavataḥ tasya māhātmyam parama ātmanaḥ mahāvarāha sṛṣṭā ca piṇḍa utpattiḥ purātanī tat ca dṛṣṭam bhagavatā brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā kim tat utpāditam pūrvam hariṇā loka dhāriṇā rūpam prabhāva mahatām apūrvam dhīmatām vara dṛṣṭvā hi vibudha śreṣṭham apūrvam amita ojasam tat aśvaśirasam puṇyam brahmā kim akarot mune etat naḥ saṃśayam brahman purāṇa jñāna saṃbhavam pāvitāḥ sma tvayā brahman puṇyām kathayatā kathām vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca kathayiṣyāmi te sarvam purāṇam veda saṃmitam śrutvā aśvaśirasaḥ mūrtim devasya harimedhasaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca vyāsaḥ uvāca sarvam pañcabhiḥ āviṣṭam bhūtaiḥ īśvara buddhi jaiḥ īśvaraḥ hi jagatsraṣṭā prabhuḥ nārāyaṇaḥ virāj bhūta antarātmā vara daḥ sa guṇaḥ nirguṇaḥ api ca bhūta pralayam avyaktam śṛṇuṣva nṛpa sattama dharaṇyām atha līnāyām apsu ca ekārṇave purā vāyau ca ākāśa saṃlīne ākāśe ca manonuge tamaḥ eva abhavat sarvam na prājñāyata kim cana tamasaḥ brahma saṃbhūtam tamaḥ mūlam ṛta ātmakam tat viśva bhāva saṃjñā antam pauruṣīm tanum āsthitam jagataḥ cintayan sṛṣṭim citrām bahu guṇa udbhavām tasya cintayataḥ sṛṣṭim mahān ātma guṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ahaṃkāraḥ tatas jātaḥ brahmā śubha caturmukhaḥ padme aniruddhāt saṃbhūtaḥ tadā padma nibha īkṣaṇaḥ sahasra patre dyutimān upaviṣṭaḥ sanātanaḥ dadṛśe adbhuta saṃkāśe lokān āpaḥ mayān prabhuḥ sattva sthaḥ parameṣṭhī sa tatas bhūta gaṇān sṛjat nārāyaṇa kṛtau bindū apām āstām guṇa uttarau sa tāmasaḥ madhuḥ jātaḥ tadā nārāyaṇa ājñayā tau abhyadhāvatām śreṣṭhau tamaḥ raja guṇa anvitau sṛjantam prathamam vedān caturaḥ cāru vigrahān sahasā jagṛhatuḥ vedān brahmaṇaḥ paśyataḥ tadā atha tau dānava śreṣṭhau vedān gṛhya sanātanān rasām viviśatuḥ tūrṇam udak pūrve mahā udadhau tatas hṛteṣu vedeṣu brahmā kaśmalam āviśat tatas vacanam īśānam prāha vedaiḥ vinākṛtaḥ mama vedāḥ hṛtāḥ sarve dānavābhyām balāt itas andhakārāḥ hi me lokāḥ jātāḥ vedaiḥ vinākṛtāḥ vedān ṛte hi kim kuryām lokān vai sraṣṭum udyataḥ prāptam dunoti hṛdayam tīvra śokāya randhayan vedān tān ānayet naṣṭān kasya ca aham priyaḥ bhave iti evam bhāṣamāṇasya brahmaṇaḥ nṛpa sattama cākṣuṣam vai dvitīyam me janma ca āsīt purātanam tvad prasādāt ca me janma tṛtīyam vācikam mahat aṇḍa jam ca api me janma tvattaḥ ṣaṣṭham vinirmitam prathitaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣa pradhāna guṇa kalpitaḥ tvam īśvara svabhāvaḥ ca svayaṃbhūḥ puruṣottamaḥ te me vedāḥ hṛtāḥ cakṣuḥ andhaḥ jātaḥ asmi jāgṛhi evam stutaḥ sa bhagavān puruṣaḥ sarvatomukhaḥ aiśvareṇa prayogeṇa dvitīyām tanum āsthitaḥ kṛtvā hayaśiraḥ śubhram vedānām ālayam prabhuḥ keśāḥ ca asya abhavan dīrghāḥ raveḥ aṃśu sama prabhāḥ karṇau ākāśa pātāle lalāṭam bhūta dhāriṇī gaṅgā sarasvatī puṇyā bhruvau āstām mahā nadī cakṣuṣī soma sūryau te nāsā saṃdhyā punar smṛtā dantāḥ ca pitaraḥ rājan somapāḥ iti viśrutāḥ golokaḥ brahma lokaḥ ca oṣṭhau āstām mahātmanaḥ grīvā ca asya abhavat rājan kālarātriḥ guṇa uttarā etat hayaśiraḥ kṛtvā nānā mūrtibhiḥ āvṛtam antardadhe sa viśveśaḥ viveśa ca rasām prabhuḥ rasām punar praviṣṭaḥ ca yogam paramam āsthitaḥ śaikṣam svaram samāsthāya om iti prāsṛjat svaram babhūva antar mahī bhūtaḥ sarva bhūta guṇa uditaḥ jagrāha vedān akhilān rasātala gatān hariḥ prādāt ca brahmaṇe bhūyas tatas svām prakṛtim gataḥ vedānām ālayaḥ ca api babhūva aśvaśirāḥ tatas yatra vedāḥ vinikṣiptāḥ tat sthānam śūnyam eva ca punar uttasthatuḥ śīghram rasānām ālayāt tadā dadṛśāte ca puruṣam tam eva ādikaram prabhum śayane nāga bhoga āḍhye jvālā mālā samāvṛte tam dṛṣṭvā dānava indrau tau mahā hāsam amuñcatām ūcatuḥ ca samāviṣṭau rajasā tamasā ca tau ayam sa puruṣaḥ śvetaḥ śete nidrām upāgataḥ anena nūnam vedānām kṛtam āharaṇam rasāt brahmaṇā upacitim kurvan jaghāna madhusūdanaḥ śoka apanayanam cakre brahmaṇaḥ puruṣottamaḥ tatas parivṛtaḥ brahmā hata ariḥ veda satkṛtaḥ nirmame sa tadā lokān kṛtsnān sthāvara jaṅgamān dattvā pitāmahāya agryām buddhim loka visargikīm evam eṣa mahābhāgaḥ babhūva aśvaśirāḥ hariḥ paurāṇam etat ākhyātam rūpam vara dam aiśvaram yaḥ hi etat brāhmaṇaḥ nityam śṛṇuyāt dhārayeta vā pāñcālena kramaḥ prāptaḥ rāmeṇa pathi deśite etat haya śiraḥ rājan ākhyānam tava kīrtitam purāṇam veda samitam yat mām tvam paripṛcchasi yām yām icchet tanum devaḥ kartum kārya vidhau kva cit tām tām kuryāt vikurvāṇaḥ svayam ātmānam ātmanā eṣa veda nidhiḥ śrīmān eṣa vai tapasaḥ nidhiḥ eṣa yogaḥ ca sāṃkhyam ca brahma ca agryam hariḥ vibhuḥ nārāyaṇa parāḥ vedāḥ yajñāḥ nārāyaṇa ātmakāḥ tapaḥ nārāyaṇa param nārāyaṇa parā gatiḥ nārāyaṇa param satyam ṛtam nārāyaṇa ātmakam nārāyaṇa paraḥ dharmaḥ punarāvṛtti durlabhaḥ pravṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ ca eva dharmaḥ nārāyaṇa ātmakaḥ nārāyaṇa ātmakaḥ gandhaḥ bhūmau śreṣṭhatamaḥ smṛtaḥ apām ca eva guṇaḥ rājan rasaḥ nārāyaṇa ātmakaḥ jyotiṣām ca guṇaḥ rūpam smṛtam nārāyaṇa ātmakam nārāyaṇa ātmakaḥ ca api sparśaḥ vāyu guṇaḥ smṛtaḥ nārāyaṇa ātmakaḥ ca api śabdaḥ ākāśa saṃbhavaḥ manaḥ ca api tatas bhūtam avyakta guṇa lakṣaṇam nārāyaṇa paraḥ kālaḥ jyotiṣām ayanam ca yat nārāyaṇa parā kīrtiḥ śrīḥ ca lakṣmīḥ ca devatāḥ nārāyaṇa param sāṃkhyam yogaḥ nārāyaṇa ātmakaḥ kāraṇam puruṣaḥ yeṣām pradhānam ca api kāraṇam svabhāvaḥ ca eva karmāṇi daivam yeṣām ca kāraṇam pañca kāraṇa saṃkhyātaḥ niṣṭhā sarvatra vai hariḥ tattvam jijñāsamānānām hetubhiḥ sarvatomukhaiḥ tattvam ekaḥ mahā yogī hariḥ nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ sa brahmakānām lokānām ṛṣīṇām ca mahātmanām sāṃkhyānām yoginām ca api yatīnām ātma vedinām manīṣitam vijānāti keśavaḥ na tu tasya te sarveṣām āśrayaḥ viṣṇuḥ aiśvaram vidhim āsthitaḥ ayam hi nityaḥ paramaḥ mahā ṛṣiḥ mahā vibhūtiḥ guṇavān nirguṇa ākhyaḥ guṇaiḥ ca saṃyogam upaiti śīghram kālaḥ yathā ṛtau ṛtu saṃprayuktaḥ jñāna ātmakāḥ saṃyaminaḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ paśyanti nityam puruṣam guṇa adhikam aho hi ekāntinaḥ sarvān prīṇāti bhagavān hariḥ vidhi prayuktām pūjām ca gṛhṇāti bhagavān svayam teṣām tvayā abhinirdiṣṭā pāraṃparya āgatā gatiḥ nūnam ekānta dharmaḥ ayam śreṣṭhaḥ nārāyaṇa priyaḥ saha upaniṣadān vedān ye viprāḥ samyak āsthitāḥ paṭhanti vidhim āsthāya ye ca api yati dharmiṇaḥ tebhyaḥ viśiṣṭām jānāmi gatim ekāntinām nṛṇām kena eṣa dharmaḥ kathitaḥ devena ṛṣiṇā api vā ekāntinām ca kā caryā kadā ca utpāditā vibho etat me saṃśayam chindhi param kautūhalam hi me vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca samupoḍheṣu anīkeṣu kuru pāṇḍavayoḥ mṛdhe āgatiḥ ca gatiḥ ca eva pūrvam te kathitā mayā saṃmitaḥ sāmavedena purā eva ādi yuge kṛtaḥ dhāryate svayam īśena rājan nārāyaṇena ha etam artham mahā rāja pṛṣṭaḥ pārthena nāradaḥ ṛṣi madhye mahābhāgaḥ śṛṇvatoḥ kṛṣṇa bhīṣmayoḥ yathā tu kathitaḥ tatra nāradena tathā śṛṇu yadā āsīt mānasam janma nārāyaṇa mukha udgatam brahmaṇaḥ pṛthivīpāla tadā nārāyaṇaḥ svayam phenapāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca eva tam dharmam pratipedire yadā āsīt cākṣuṣam janma dvitīyam brahmaṇaḥ nṛpa tadā pitāmahāt somāt etam dharmam ajānata nārāyaṇa ātmakam rājan rudrāya pradadau ca saḥ vālakhilyān ṛṣīn sarvān dharmam etam apāṭhayat tṛtīyam brahmaṇaḥ janma yadā āsīt vācikam mahat tatra eṣa dharmaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ svayam nārāyaṇāt nṛpa suparṇaḥ nāma tam ṛṣiḥ prāptavān puruṣottamāt ṛgveda pāṭha paṭhitam vratam etat hi duścaram suparṇāt ca api adhigataḥ dharmaḥ eṣa sanātanaḥ vāyunā dvipadām śreṣṭha prathitaḥ jagadāyuṣā vāyoḥ sakāśāt prāptaḥ ca ṛṣibhiḥ vighasa āśibhiḥ tatas saḥ antardadhe bhūyas nārāyaṇa samāhitaḥ yadā bhūyas śravaṇa jā sṛṣṭiḥ āsīt mahātmanaḥ brahmaṇaḥ puruṣa vyāghra tatra kīrtayataḥ śṛṇu jagat sraṣṭu manāḥ devaḥ hariḥ nārāyaṇaḥ svayam cintayām āsa puruṣam jagat sarga karam prabhuḥ atha cintayataḥ tasya karṇābhyām puruṣaḥ sṛtaḥ sṛja prajāḥ putra sarvāḥ mukhataḥ pādataḥ tathā dharmam ca mattaḥ gṛhṇīṣva sātvatam nāma nāmataḥ āraṇyakena sahitam nārāyaṇa mukha udgatam tam kārtayuga dharmāṇam nirāśīḥkarma saṃjñitam asṛjat sa tadā lokān kṛtsnān sthāvara jaṅgamān tatas prāvartata tadā ādau kṛta yugam śubham pūjayām āsa deveśam harim nārāyaṇam prabhum dharma pratiṣṭhā hetoḥ ca manum svārociṣam tatas adhyāpayām āsa tadā lokānām hita kāmyayā tatas svārociṣaḥ putram svayam śaṅkhapadam nṛpa tatas śaṅkhapadaḥ ca api putram ātmajam aurasam diśāpālam sudharmāṇam adhyāpayata bhārata dharmam etam svayam devaḥ hariḥ nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ujjagāra aravinda akṣaḥ brahmaṇaḥ paśyataḥ tadā sanatkumāraḥ bhagavān tatas prādhītavān nṛpa sanatkumārāt api ca vīraṇaḥ vai prajāpatiḥ kṛta ādau kuru śārdūla dharmam etam adhītavān vīraṇaḥ ca api adhītya enam raucyāya manave dadau kukṣi nāmne atha pradadau diśām pālāya dharmiṇe tatas saḥ antardadhe bhūyas nārāyaṇa mukha udgataḥ eṣa dharmaḥ samudbhūtaḥ nārāyaṇa mukhāt punar gṛhītaḥ brahmaṇā rājan prayuktaḥ ca yathāvidhi adhyāpitāḥ ca munayaḥ nāmnā barhiṣadaḥ nṛpa barhiṣadbhyaḥ ca saṃkrāntaḥ sāmaveda antagam dvijam jyeṣṭham nāmnā abhivikhyātam jyeṣṭhasāma vrataḥ hariḥ jyeṣṭhāt ca api anusaṃkrāntaḥ rājānam avikampanam tatra eṣa dharmaḥ kathitaḥ svayam nārāyaṇena hi pitāmahāya śuddhāya yuga ādau loka dhāriṇe pitāmahaḥ ca dakṣāya dharmam etam purā dadau āditye savituḥ jyeṣṭhe vivasvān jagṛhe tatas ikṣvākuṇā ca kathitaḥ vyāpya lokān avasthitaḥ gamiṣyati kṣaya ante ca punar nārāyaṇam nṛpa vratinām ca api yaḥ dharmaḥ sa te pūrvam nṛpa uttama nāradena tu saṃprāptaḥ sa rahasyaḥ sa saṃgrahaḥ eṣa dharmaḥ jagannāthāt sākṣāt nārāyaṇāt nṛpa evam eṣa mahān dharmaḥ ādyaḥ rājan sanātanaḥ ahiṃsā dharma yuktena prīyate hariḥ īśvaraḥ eka vyūha vibhāgaḥ vā kva cit dvi vyūha saṃjñitaḥ tri vyūhaḥ ca api saṃkhyātaḥ catur vyūhaḥ ca dṛśyate jīvaḥ ca sarva bhūteṣu pañca bhūta guṇa atigaḥ akartā ca eva kartā ca kāryam kāraṇam eva ca yathā icchati tathā rājan krīḍate puruṣaḥ avyayaḥ mayā guru prasādena durvijñeyaḥ akṛtātmabhiḥ bhavet kṛta yuga prāptiḥ āśīḥ karma vivarjitaiḥ evam sa bhagavān vyāsaḥ guruḥ mama viśām pate ṛṣīṇām saṃnidhau rājan śṛṇvatoḥ kṛṣṇa bhīṣmayoḥ tasya api akathayat pūrvam nāradaḥ su mahā tapāḥ yatra ca ekāntinaḥ yānti nārāyaṇa parāyaṇāḥ vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca tisraḥ prakṛtayaḥ rājan deha bandheṣu nirmitāḥ sāttvikī rājasī ca eva tāmasī ca iti bhārata deha bandheṣu puruṣaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ kuru kula udvaha sāttvikaḥ puruṣa vyāghra bhavet mokṣa artha niścitaḥ nārāyaṇa paraḥ mokṣaḥ tatas vai sāttvikaḥ smṛtaḥ ekānta bhaktiḥ satatam nārāyaṇa parāyaṇaḥ manīṣiṇaḥ hi ye ke cit yatayaḥ mokṣa kāṅkṣiṇaḥ teṣām vai chinna tṛṣṇānām yogakṣema vahaḥ hariḥ jāyamānam hi puruṣam yam paśyet madhusūdanaḥ nārāyaṇa ātmake mokṣe tatas yānti parām gatim nārāyaṇena dṛṣṭaḥ ca pratibuddhaḥ bhavet pumān rājasī tāmasī ca eva vyāmiśre prakṛtī smṛte tad ātmakam hi puruṣam jāyamānam viśām pate pravṛtti lakṣaṇaiḥ yuktam na avekṣati hariḥ svayam paśyati enam jāyamānam brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ kāmam devāḥ ca ṛṣayaḥ sattva sthāḥ nṛpa sattama hīnāḥ sattvena sūkṣmeṇa tatas vaikārikāḥ smṛtāḥ vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca su sūkṣma sattva saṃyuktam saṃyuktam tribhiḥ akṣaraiḥ puruṣaḥ puruṣam gacchet niṣkriyaḥ pañcaviṃśakam evam ekam sāṃkhya yogam veda āraṇyakam eva ca paraspara aṅgāni etāni pañcarātram ca kathyate eṣaḥ ekāntinām dharmaḥ nārāyaṇa para ātmakaḥ yathā samudrāt prasṛtāḥ jala oghāḥ tam eva rājan punar āviśanti ime tathā jñāna mahā jala oghāḥ nārāyaṇam vai punar āviśanti kuruṣva enam yathānyāyam yadi śaknoṣi bhārata śvetānām yatinām āha ekānta gatim avyayām vyāsaḥ ca akathayat prītyā dharmaputrāya dhīmate saḥ eva ayam mayā tubhyam ākhyātaḥ prasṛtaḥ guroḥ kṛṣṇaḥ eva hi lokānām bhāvanaḥ mohanaḥ tathā saṃhāra kārakaḥ ca eva kāraṇam ca viśām pate sāṃkhyam yogam pañcarātram veda āraṇyakam eva ca jñānāni etāni brahmarṣe lokeṣu pracaranti ha kim etāni eka niṣṭhāni pṛthak niṣṭhāni vā mune prabrūhi vai mayā pṛṣṭaḥ pravṛttim ca yathākramam vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca parāśarāt gandhavatī mahā ṛṣim tasmai namaḥ ajñāna tamaḥ nudāya pitāmaha ādyam pravadanti ṣaṣṭham mahā ṛṣim ārṣeya vibhūti yuktam nārāyaṇasya aṃśa jam eka putram dvaipāyanam veda mahā nidhānam tam ādi kāleṣu mahā vibhūtiḥ nārāyaṇaḥ brahma mahā nidhānam sasarja putra artham udāra tejāḥ vyāsam mahātmānam ajaḥ purāṇaḥ vasiṣṭhasya sutaḥ śaktiḥ śakteḥ putraḥ parāśaraḥ parāśarasya dāyādaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ muniḥ bhūyas nārāyaṇa sutam tvam eva enam prabhāṣase kim atas pūrvajam janma vyāsasya amita tejasaḥ vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca guroḥ me jñāna niṣṭhasya himavatpāde āsataḥ kṛtvā bhāratam ākhyānam tapaḥ śrāntasya dhīmataḥ śuśrūṣām tad parāḥ rājan kṛtavantaḥ vayam tadā aham caturthaḥ śiṣyaḥ vai śukaḥ vyāsa ātmajaḥ tathā ebhiḥ parivṛtaḥ vyāsaḥ śiṣyaiḥ pañcabhiḥ uttamaiḥ śuśubhe himavat pāde bhūtaiḥ bhūtapatiḥ yathā vedān āvartayan sa aṅgān bhārata arthān ca sarvaśas kathā antare atha kasmin cit pṛṣṭaḥ asmābhiḥ dvijottamaḥ veda arthān bhārata arthān ca janma nārāyaṇāt tathā sa pūrvam uktvā veda arthān bhārata arthān ca tattva vid nārāyaṇāt idam janma vyāhartum upacakrame śṛṇudhvam ākhyāna varam etat ārṣeyam uttamam ādi kāla udbhavam viprāḥ tapasā adhigatam mayā mama tvam na abhitas jātaḥ prajā sarga karaḥ prabhuḥ sṛja prajāḥ tvam vividhāḥ brahman sa jaḍa paṇḍitāḥ kā śaktiḥ mama deveśa prajāḥ sraṣṭum namaḥ astu te cintayām āsa deveśaḥ buddhim buddhimatām varaḥ sa tām aiśvarya yoga sthām buddhim śaktimatīm satīm brahmāṇam praviśasva iti loka sṛṣṭi artha siddhaye tatas tam īśvara ādiṣṭā buddhiḥ kṣipram viveśa sā athā enam buddhi saṃyuktam punar sa dadṛśe hariḥ bhūyas ca enam vacaḥ prāha sṛja imāḥ vividhāḥ prajāḥ tām ca eva prakṛtim prāpya ekībhāva gataḥ abhavat sṛṣṭāḥ imāḥ prajāḥ sarvāḥ brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā daitya dānava gandharva rakṣaḥ gaṇa samākulāḥ jātā hi iyam vasumatī bhāra ākrāntā tapasvinī bahavaḥ balinaḥ pṛthvyām daitya dānava rākṣasāḥ bādhitavyāḥ sura gaṇāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca tapodhanāḥ tatra nyāyyam idam kartum bhāra avataraṇam mayā atha nānā samudbhūtaiḥ vasudhāyām yathākramam nigraheṇa ca pāpānām sādhūnām pragraheṇa ca imām tapasvinīm satyām dhārayiṣyāmi medinīm mayā hi eṣā hi dhriyate pātāla sthena bhoginā tasmāt pṛthvyāḥ paritrāṇam kariṣye saṃbhavam gataḥ rūpāṇi anekāni asṛjat prādurbhāva bhavāya saḥ vārāham nārasiṃham ca vāmanam mānuṣam tathā ebhiḥ mayā nihantavyāḥ durvinītāḥ surārayaḥ atha bhūyas jagatsraṣṭā bhoḥ śabdena anunādayan apāntaratamāḥ nāma sutaḥ vāc saṃbhavaḥ vibhoḥ bhūta bhavya bhaviṣya jñaḥ satya vādī dṛḍha vrataḥ tam uvāca natam mūrdhnā devānām ādiḥ avyayaḥ veda ākhyāne śrutiḥ kāryā tvayā matimatām vara tena bhinnāḥ tadā vedāḥ manoḥ svāyaṃbhuve antare śrī bhagavān uvāca punar tiṣye ca saṃprāpte kuravaḥ nāma bhāratāḥ bhaviṣyanti mahātmānaḥ rājānaḥ prathitāḥ bhuvi teṣām tvattaḥ prasūtānām kula bhedaḥ bhaviṣyati paraspara vināśa artham tvām ṛte dvijasattama kṛṣṇe yuge ca saṃprāpte kṛṣṇa varṇaḥ bhaviṣyasi dharmāṇām vividhānām ca kartā jñāna karaḥ tathā vīta rāgaḥ ca putraḥ te paramātmā bhaviṣyati vasiṣṭham agryam tapasaḥ nidhānam yaḥ ca api sūryam vyatiricya bhāti tasya anvaye ca api tatas mahā ṛṣiḥ parāśaraḥ nāma mahā prabhāvaḥ kānīna garbhaḥ pitṛ kanyakāyām tasmāt ṛṣeḥ tvam bhavitā ca putraḥ bhūta bhavya bhaviṣyāṇām chinna sarva artha saṃśayaḥ ye hi atikrāntakāḥ pūrvam sahasra yuga paryayāḥ tān ca sarvān mayā uddiṣṭān drakṣyase tapasā anvitaḥ tvam eva bhavitā vatsa mad prasādāt na saṃśayaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca evam sārasvatam ṛṣim apāntaratamam tadā uktvā vacanam īśānaḥ sādhayasva iti atha abravīt apāntaratamāḥ nāma tatas jātaḥ hareḥ punar ca jātaḥ vikhyātaḥ vasiṣṭha kula nandanaḥ nārāyaṇa prasādena tathā nārāyaṇa aṃśa jam purā matimatām śreṣṭhāḥ parameṇa samādhinā etat vaḥ kathitam sarvam yat mām pṛcchatha putrakāḥ pūrva janma bhaviṣyam ca bhaktānām snehataḥ mayā vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca eṣa te kathitaḥ pūrvam saṃbhavaḥ asmad guroḥ nṛpa vyāsasya akliṣṭa manasaḥ yathā pṛṣṭaḥ punar śṛṇu sāṃkhyam yogam pañcarātram vedāḥ pāśupatam tathā jñānāni etāni rājarṣe viddhi nānā matāni vai sāṃkhyasya vaktā kapilaḥ parama ṛṣiḥ saḥ ucyate hiraṇyagarbhaḥ yogasya vettā nā anyaḥ purātanaḥ apāntaratamāḥ ca eva veda ācāryaḥ saḥ ucyate prācīnagarbham tam ṛṣim pravadanti iha ke cana uktavān idam avyagraḥ jñānam pāśupatam śivaḥ sarveṣu ca nṛpa śreṣṭha jñāneṣu eteṣu dṛśyate yathāgamam yathājñānam niṣṭhā nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ na ca enam evam jānanti tamaḥ bhūtāḥ viśām pate tam eva śāstra kartāram pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ niṣṭhām nārāyaṇam ṛṣim na anyaḥ asti iti ca vādinaḥ niḥsaṃśayeṣu sarveṣu nityam vasati vai hariḥ sa saṃśayān hetu balāt na adhyāvasati mādhavaḥ sarvaiḥ samastaiḥ ṛṣibhiḥ niruktaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ viśvam idam purāṇam kaḥ hi atra puruṣaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ kaḥ vā yoniḥ iha ucyate vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca bahavaḥ puruṣāḥ loke sāṃkhya yoga vicāriṇām bahūnām puruṣāṇām ca yathā ekā yoniḥ ucyate tathā tam puruṣam viśvam vyākhyāsyāmi guṇa adhikam idam puruṣasūktam hi sarva vedeṣu pārthiva ṛtam satyam ca vikhyātam ṛṣi siṃhena cintitam utsargeṇa apavādena ṛṣibhiḥ kapila ādibhiḥ adhyātma cintām āśritya śāstrāṇi uktāni bhārata tat te aham saṃpravakṣyāmi prasādāt amita ojasaḥ atrā api udāharanti imam itihāsam purātanam brahmaṇā saha saṃvādam tryambakasya viśām pate lalāṭa prabhavaḥ putraḥ śivaḥ āgāt yadṛcchayā ākāśena eva yogi īśaḥ purā trinayanaḥ prabhuḥ tatas khāt nipapāta āśu dharaṇīdhara mūrdhani agratas ca abhavat prītaḥ vavande ca api pādayoḥ tam pādayoḥ nipatitam dṛṣṭvā savyena pāṇinā utthāpayām āsa tadā prabhuḥ ekaḥ prajāpatiḥ uvāca ca enam bhagavān cirasya āgatam ātmajam svāgatam te mahā bāho diṣṭyā prāptaḥ asi me antikam kaccit te kuśalam putra svādhyāya tapasoḥ sadā cira dṛṣṭaḥ hi bhagavān vairāja sadane mayā kim nu tat sadanam śreṣṭham kṣudh pipāsā vivarjitam sura asuraiḥ adhyuṣitam ṛṣibhiḥ ca amita prabhaiḥ utsṛjya imam giri varam ekākī prāptavān asi atra ekāgreṇa manasā puruṣaḥ cintyate virāj bahavaḥ puruṣāḥ brahman tvayā sṛṣṭāḥ svayaṃbhuvā sṛjyante ca apare brahman sa ca ekaḥ puruṣaḥ virāj etat me saṃśayam brūhi mahat kautūhalam hi me bahavaḥ puruṣāḥ putra ye tvayā samudāhṛtāḥ ādhāram tu pravakṣyāmi ekasya puruṣasya te bahūnām puruṣāṇām sa yathā ekā yoniḥ ucyate tathā tam puruṣam viśvam paramam su mahattamam nirguṇam nirguṇāḥ bhūtvā praviśanti sanātanam śṛṇu putra yathā hi eṣa puruṣaḥ śāśvataḥ avyayaḥ na sa śakyaḥ tvayā draṣṭum mayā anyaiḥ vā api sattama sa guṇaḥ nirguṇaḥ viśvaḥ jñāna dṛśyaḥ hi asau smṛtaḥ aśarīraḥ śarīreṣu sarveṣu nivasati asau mama antarātmā tava ca ye ca anye deha saṃjñitāḥ sarveṣām sākṣi bhūtaḥ asau na grāhyaḥ kena cit kva cit ekaḥ carati kṣetreṣu svaira cārī yathāsukham kṣetrāṇi hi śarīrāṇi bījāni ca śubha aśubhe tāni vetti sa yoga ātmā tatas kṣetrajñaḥ ucyate yathājñānam tu vakṣyāmi puruṣam tam sanātanam tasya eka tvam mahā tvam hi sa ca ekaḥ puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ mahāpuruṣa śabdam sa bibharti ekaḥ sanātanaḥ ekaḥ hutāśaḥ bahudhā samidhyate ekaḥ sūryaḥ tapasām yoniḥ ekā ekaḥ vāyuḥ bahudhā vāti loke mahā udadhiḥ ca ambhasām yoniḥ ekaḥ puruṣaḥ ca ekaḥ nirguṇaḥ viśva rūpaḥ tam nirguṇam puruṣam ca āviśanti hitvā guṇa mayam sarvam karma hitvā śubha aśubham ubhe satya anṛte tyaktvā evam bhavati nirguṇaḥ acintyam ca api tam jñātvā bhāva sūkṣmam catuṣṭayam evam hi parama ātmānam ke cid icchanti paṇḍitāḥ eka ātmānam tathā ātmānam apare adhyātma cintakāḥ tatra yaḥ parama ātmā hi sa nityam nirguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ sa hi nārāyaṇaḥ jñeyaḥ sarva ātmā puruṣaḥ hi saḥ sa saptadaśakena api rāśinā yujyate hi saḥ mantā mantavyam prāśitā prāśitavyam ghrātā ghreyam sparśitā sparśanīyam draṣṭā draṣṭavyam śrāvitā śrāvaṇīyam jñātā jñeyam sa guṇam nirguṇam ca yat vai proktam guṇa sāmyam pradhānam nityam ca etat śāśvatam ca avyayam ca devāḥ sarve munayaḥ sādhu dāntāḥ tam prāk yajñaiḥ yajñabhāgam yajante aham brahmā ādyaḥ īśaḥ prajānām tasmāt jātaḥ tvam ca mattaḥ prasūtaḥ evam saḥ eva bhagavān jñānena pratibodhitaḥ sāṃkhya jñāne tathā yoge yathāvat anuvarṇitam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca dharmāḥ pitāmahena uktāḥ mokṣa dharma āśritāḥ śubhāḥ dharmam āśramiṇām śreṣṭham vaktum arhati me bhavān bhīṣmaḥ uvāca purā śakrasya kathitām nāradena sura ṛṣiṇā sa kadā cit mahā iṣvāsa devarāja ālayam gataḥ tam kṛtakṣaṇam āsīnam paryapṛcchat śacīpatiḥ brahmarṣe kim cit āścaryam asti dṛṣṭam tvayā anagha jāta kautūhalaḥ nityam siddhaḥ carasi sākṣi vat śrutam vā api anubhūtam vā dṛṣṭam vā kathayasva me tasmai rājan sura indrāya nāradaḥ vadatām varaḥ āsīnāya upapannāya proktavān vipulām kathām kathām kathitavān pṛṣṭaḥ tathā tvam api me śṛṇu bhīṣmaḥ uvāca āsīt kila kuruśreṣṭha mahāpadme pura uttame gaṅgāyāḥ dakṣiṇe tīre kaḥ cit vipraḥ samāhitaḥ saumyaḥ soma anvaye vede gatādhvā chinna saṃśayaḥ ahiṃsā nirataḥ nityam satyaḥ sat jana saṃmataḥ nyāya prāptena vittena svena śīlena ca anvitaḥ jñāti saṃbandhi vipule mitra apāśraya saṃmate kule mahati vikhyāte viśiṣṭām vṛttim āsthitaḥ sa putrān bahulān dṛṣṭvā vipule karmaṇi sthitaḥ śiṣṭa ācīrṇam ca dharmam ca trividham cintya cetasā kim nu me syāt śubham kṛtvā kim kṣamam kim parāyaṇam kadā cit atithiḥ prāptaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ su samāhitaḥ viśrāntam ca enam āsīnam idam vacanam abravīt brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca mitra tām abhipannaḥ tvām kim cit vakṣyāmi tat śṛṇu kartum kāṅkṣāmi na icchāmi baddhaḥ sādhāraṇaiḥ guṇaiḥ yāvat eva anatītam me vayaḥ putra phala āśritam tāvat icchāmi pātheyam ādātum pāralaukikam asmin hi loka saṃtāne param pāram abhīpsataḥ samuhyamānāni niśamya loke niryātyamānāni ca sāttvikāni dṛṣṭvā ca dharma dhvaja ketu mālām prakīryamāṇām upari prajānām tena atithe buddhi bala āśrayeṇa dharma artha tattve viniyuṅkṣva mām tvam bhīṣmaḥ uvāca saḥ atithiḥ vacanam tasya śrutvā dharma abhilāṣiṇaḥ provāca vacanam ślakṣṇam prājñaḥ madhurayā girā na ca saṃniścayam yāmi bahu dvāre triviṣṭape ke cit mokṣam praśaṃsanti ke cit yajña phalam dvijāḥ vānaprastha āśramam ke cit gārhasthyam ke cit āśritāḥ rāja dharma āśrayam ke cit ke cit ātma phala āśrayam guru caryā āśrayam ke cid ke cid vākyam yam āśrayam mātaram pitaram ke cit śuśrūṣantaḥ divam gatāḥ āhave abhimukhāḥ ke cit nihatāḥ svid divam gatāḥ ke cid uñcha vrataiḥ siddhāḥ svarga mārga samāśritāḥ ke cit adhyayane yuktāḥ veda vrata parāḥ śubhāḥ buddhimantaḥ gatāḥ svargam tuṣṭa ātmānaḥ jita indriyāḥ ārjavena apare yuktāḥ nihata anārjavaiḥ janaiḥ ṛjavaḥ nāka pṛṣṭhe vai śuddha ātmānaḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ guruṇā me yathā ākhyātam arthataḥ tat ca me śṛṇu naimiṣe gomatī tīre tatra nāgāhvayam puram yatra indra atikramam cakre māndhātā rāja sattamaḥ kṛta adhivāsaḥ dharma ātmā tatra cakṣuḥśravāḥ mahān padmanābhaḥ mahābhāgaḥ padmaḥ iti eva viśrutaḥ sa vācā karmaṇā ca eva manasā ca dvijarṣabha viṣama stham janam svam ca cakṣuḥ dhyānena rakṣati sa hi sarva atithiḥ nāgaḥ buddhi śāstra viśāradaḥ tapaḥ damābhyām saṃyuktaḥ vṛttena an avareṇa ca yajvā dāna ruciḥ kṣāntaḥ vṛtte ca parame sthitaḥ satya vāc anasūyuḥ ca śīlavān abhisaṃśritaḥ śeṣa anna bhoktā vacana anukūlaḥ hita ārjava utkṛṣṭa kṛtākṛta jñaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca para āśvāsa karam vākyam idam me bhavataḥ śrutam tṛṣitasya ca pānīyam kṣudhā ārtasya ca bhojanam eṣitasya ātmanaḥ kāle vṛddhasya iva sutaḥ yathā prahrādayati mām vākyam bhavatā yat udīritam datta cakṣuḥ iva ākāśe paśyāmi vimṛśāmi ca prajñāna vacanāt yaḥ ayam upadeśaḥ hi me kṛtaḥ bāḍham evam kariṣyāmi yathā mām bhāṣate bhavān iha imām rajanīm sādho nivasasva mayā saha prabhāte yāsyati bhavān paryāśvastaḥ sukha uṣitaḥ asau hi bhagavān sūryaḥ manda raśmiḥ avāṅmukhaḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca tatas tena kṛta ātithyaḥ saḥ atithiḥ śatru sūdana vyatītā sā niśā kṛtsnā sukhena divasa upamā brāhmaṇena yathāśaktyā sva kāryam abhikāṅkṣatā yathā upadiṣṭam bhujaga indra saṃśrayam jagāma kāle sukṛta eka niścayaḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca sa vanāni vicitrāṇi tīrthāni ca sarāṃsi ca tam sa tena yathā uddiṣṭam nāgam vipreṇa brāhmaṇaḥ paryapṛcchat yathānyāyam śrutvā eva ca jagāma saḥ proktavān aham asmi iti bhoḥ śabda alaṃkṛtam vacaḥ tatas tasya vacaḥ śrutvā rūpiṇī dharma vatsalā darśayām āsa tam vipram nāga patnī pativratā sā tasmai vidhivat pūjām cakre dharma parāyaṇā svāgatena āgatam kṛtvā kim karomi iti ca abravīt brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca viśrāntaḥ abhyarcitaḥ ca asmi bhavatyā ślakṣṇayā girā nāga bhāryā uvāca ārya sūrya ratham voḍhum gataḥ asau māsacārikaḥ sapta aṣṭabhiḥ dinaiḥ vipra darśayiṣyati asaṃśayam brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca anena niścayena aham sādhvi saṃprāptavān iha mama abhigamanam prāptaḥ vācyaḥ ca vacanam tvayā kālam parimita āhāraḥ yathoktam paripālayan bhīṣmaḥ uvāca tatas sa vipraḥ tām nāgīm samādhāya punar punar tat eva pulinam nadyāḥ prayayau brāhmaṇa ṛṣabhaḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca atha tena nara śreṣṭha brāhmaṇena tapasvinā nirāhāreṇa vasatā duḥkhitāḥ te bhujaṃgamāḥ sarve saṃbhūya sahitāḥ tasya nāgasya bāndhavāḥ bhrātaraḥ tanayāḥ bhāryāḥ yayuḥ tam brāhmaṇam prati samāsīnam nirāhāram dvijam japya parāyaṇam ūcuḥ vākyam asaṃdigdham ātitheyasya bāndhavāḥ na ca abhilaṣase kim cit āhāram dharma vatsala asmān abhigataḥ ca asi vayam ca tvām upasthitāḥ kāryam ca ātithyam asmābhiḥ vayam sarve kuṭumbinaḥ mūlam phalam vā parṇam vā payaḥ vā dvijasattama āhāra hetoḥ annam vā bhoktum arhasi brāhmaṇa tyakta āhāreṇa bhavatā vane nivasatā satā bāla vṛddham idam sarvam pīḍyate dharma saṃkaṭāt na hi naḥ bhrūṇa hā kaḥ cit rājā apathyaḥ anṛtaḥ api vā pūrva āśī vā kule hi asmin devatā atithi bandhuṣu brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca upadeśena yuṣmākam āhāraḥ ayam mayā vṛtaḥ dvis ūnam daśa rātram vai nāgasya āgamanam prati yadi aṣṭa rātre niryāte na āgamiṣyati pannagaḥ tad āhāram kariṣyāmi tad nimittam idam vratam bhīṣmaḥ uvāca tena te samanujñātāḥ brāhmaṇena bhujaṃgamāḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca atha kāle bahutithe pūrṇe prāptaḥ bhujaṃgamaḥ datta abhyanujñaḥ svam veśma kṛta karmā vivasvataḥ tam bhāryā samabhikrāmat pāda śauca ādibhiḥ guṇaiḥ upapannām ca tām sādhvīm pannagaḥ paryapṛcchata na khalu asi akṛtārthena strī buddhyā mārdavīkṛtā nāga bhāryā uvāca śiṣyāṇām guru śuśrūṣā viprāṇām veda pāraṇam bhṛtyānām svāmi vacanam rājñām loka anupālanam vaiśyānām yajña saṃvṛttiḥ ātitheya samanvitā vipra kṣatriya vaiśyānām śuśrūṣā śūdra karma tat niyata āhāra tā nityam vrata caryā yathākramam dharmaḥ hi dharma saṃbandhāt indriyāṇām viśeṣaṇam pativratā tvam bhāryāyāḥ paramaḥ dharmaḥ ucyate devatānām mahābhāga dharma caryā na hīyate atithīnām ca satkāre nitya yuktā asmi atandritā sa ca kāryam na me khyāti darśanam tava kāṅkṣati āsīnaḥ brahma brāhmaṇaḥ saṃśita vrataḥ aham tu anena nāga indra sāma pūrvam samāhitā prasthāpyaḥ mad sakāśam sa saṃprāptaḥ bhujaga uttamaḥ dātum arhasi vā tasya darśanam darśana śravaḥ nāgaḥ uvāca atha brāhmaṇa rūpeṇa kam tam samanupaśyasi mānuṣam kevalam vipram devam vā atha śuci smite kaḥ hi mām mānuṣaḥ śaktaḥ draṣṭu kāmaḥ yaśasvini saṃdarśana ruciḥ vākyam ājñā pūrvam vadiṣyati sura asura gaṇānām ca devarṣīṇām ca bhāmini nanu nāgāḥ mahā vīryāḥ sauraseyāḥ tarasvinaḥ vandanīyāḥ ca vara dāḥ vayam api anuyāyinaḥ manuṣyāṇām viśeṣeṇa dhana adhyakṣāḥ iti śrutiḥ nāga bhāryā uvāca ārjavena abhijānāmi na asau devaḥ anilāśana ekam tu asya vijānāmi bhaktimān ati roṣaṇaḥ sa hi kārya antara akāṅkṣī jala īpsuḥ stokakaḥ yathā varṣam varṣapriyaḥ pakṣī darśanam tava kāṅkṣati tat roṣam sahajam tyaktvā tvam enam draṣṭum arhasi āśā chedena tasya adya nā ātmānam dagdhum arhasi āśayā tu abhipannānām a kṛtvā aśru pramārjanam rājā vā rāja putraḥ vā bhrūṇa hatyā eva yujyate maunāt jñāna phala avāptiḥ dānena ca yaśaḥ mahat bhūmi pradānena gatim labhati āśrama saṃmitām naṣṭasya arthasya saṃprāptim kṛtvā phalam upāśnute abhipretām asaṃkliṣṭām kṛtvā akāmavatīm kriyām nāgaḥ uvāca abhimānena mānaḥ me jāti doṣeṇa vai mahān roṣaḥ saṃkalpa jaḥ sādhvi dagdhaḥ vācā agninā tvayā na ca roṣāt aham sādhvi paśyeyam adhikam tamaḥ yasya vaktavya tām yānti viśeṣeṇa bhujaṃgamāḥ doṣasya hi vaśam gatvā daśagrīvaḥ pratāpavān tathā śakra pratispardhī hataḥ rāmeṇa saṃyuge antaḥpura gatam vatsam śrutvā rāmeṇa nirhṛtam dharṣaṇāt roṣa saṃvignāḥ kārtavīrya sutāḥ hatāḥ saṃyuge nihataḥ roṣāt kārtavīryaḥ mahā balaḥ tat eṣa tapasām śatruḥ śreyasaḥ ca nipātanaḥ nigṛhītaḥ mayā roṣaḥ śrutvā eva vacanam tava ātmānam ca viśeṣeṇa praśaṃsāmi anapāyini yasya me tvam viśāla akṣi bhāryā sarva guṇa anvitā sarvathā ca uktavān vākyam na akṛtārthaḥ prayāsyati bhīṣmaḥ uvāca tam eva manasā dhyāyan kāryavat tām vicārayan provāca madhuram vākyam prakṛtyāḥ dharma vatsalaḥ bho bho kṣāmya abhibhāṣe tvām na roṣam kartum arhasi vivikte gomatī tīre kim vā tvam paryupāsase brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca dharmāraṇyam hi mām viddhi nāgam draṣṭum iha āgatam padmanābham dvijaśreṣṭham tatra me kāryam āhitam tasya ca aham asāṃnidhyam śrutavān asmi tam gatam sva janam tam pratīkṣāmi parjanyam iva karṣakaḥ tasya ca akleśa karaṇam svastikāra samāhitam nāgaḥ uvāca aho kalyāṇa vṛttaḥ tvam sādhu sat jana vatsalaḥ śrava āḍhyaḥ tvam mahābhāga param snehena paśyasi aham sa nāgaḥ viprarṣe yathā mām vindate bhavān ājñāpaya yathā svairam kim karomi priyam tava bhavantam sva janāt asmi saṃprāptam śrutavān iha atas tvām svayam eva aham draṣṭum abhyāgataḥ dvija saṃprāptaḥ ca bhavān adya kṛtārthaḥ pratiyāsyati vayam hi bhavatā sarve guṇa krītāḥ viśeṣataḥ brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca āgataḥ aham mahābhāga tava darśana lālasaḥ kam cit artham an artha jñaḥ praṣṭu kāmaḥ bhujaṃgama aham ātmānam ātma sthaḥ mārgamāṇaḥ hitam vāsa arthinam mahā prājña balavantam upāsmi ha śaśāṅka kara saṃsparśaiḥ hṛdyaiḥ ātma prakāśitaiḥ paścāt kāryam vadiṣyāmi śrotum arhati me bhavān brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca āścarya bhūtam yadi tatra kim cit dṛṣṭam tvayā śaṃsitum arhasi tvam nāgaḥ uvāca yasya raśmi sahasreṣu śākhāsu iva vihaṃgamāḥ yatas vāyuḥ viniḥsṛtya sūrya raśmi āśritaḥ mahān śukraḥ nāma asitaḥ pādaḥ yasya vāridharaḥ ambare toyam sṛjati varṣāsu kim āścaryam atas param yaḥ aṣṭa māsān tu śucinā kiraṇena ujjhitam payaḥ paryādatte punar kāle kim āścaryam atas param yasya tejaḥ viśeṣeṣu nityam ātmā pratiṣṭhitaḥ yatas bījam mahī ca iyam dhāryate sacarācaram yatra devaḥ mahā bāhuḥ śāśvataḥ paramaḥ akṣaraḥ āścaryāṇām iva āścaryam idam ekam tu me śṛṇu vimale yat mayā dṛṣṭam ambare sūrya saṃśrayāt prati āditya pratīkāśaḥ sarvatas pratyadṛśyata sa lokān tejasā sarvān sva bhāsā nirvibhāsayan anirdeśyena rūpeṇa dvitīyaḥ iva bhāskaraḥ ekībhūtam ca tat tejaḥ kṣaṇena āditya tām gatam tatra naḥ saṃśayaḥ jātaḥ tayoḥ tejaḥ samāgame te vayam jāta saṃdehāḥ paryapṛcchāmahe ravim kaḥ eṣa divam ākramya gataḥ sūryaḥ iva aparaḥ sūryaḥ uvāca eṣa mūla phala āhāraḥ śīrṇa parṇa aśanaḥ tathā abbhakṣaḥ vāyubhakṣaḥ ca āsīt vipraḥ samāhitaḥ ṛcaḥ ca anena vipreṇa saṃhitā antar abhiṣṭutāḥ nityam uñcha śila aśanaḥ na hi devāḥ na gandharvāḥ na asurāḥ na ca pannagāḥ prabhavanti iha bhūtānām prāptānām paramām gatim nāgaḥ uvāca etat evaṃvidham dṛṣṭam āścaryam tatra me dvija saṃsiddhaḥ mānuṣaḥ kāyaḥ yaḥ asau siddha gatim gataḥ brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca āścaryam na atra saṃdehaḥ su prītaḥ asmi bhujaṃgama anvartha upagataiḥ vākyaiḥ panthānam ca asmi darśitaḥ smaraṇīyaḥ asmi bhavatā saṃpreṣaṇa niyojanaiḥ nāgaḥ uvāca an uktvā mad gatam kāryam kva idānīm prasthitaḥ bhavān ucyatām dvija yat kāryam yad artham tvam iha āgataḥ ukta anukte kṛte kārye mām āmantrya dvijarṣabha na hi mām kevalam dṛṣṭvā tyaktvā praṇayavān iha tvayi ca aham dvijaśreṣṭha bhavān mayi na saṃśayaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca evam etat mahā prājña vijñāta artha bhujaṃgama aham bhavān ca bhūtāni sarve sarvatragāḥ sadā āsīt tu me bhoga pate saṃśayaḥ puṇya saṃcaye eṣa me niścayaḥ sādho kṛtaḥ kāraṇavattaraḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca sa ca āmantrya uraga śreṣṭham brāhmaṇaḥ kṛta niścayaḥ dīkṣā ākāṅkṣī tadā rājan cyavanam bhārgavam śritaḥ tathā eva ca kathām etām rājan kathitavān tadā kathā eṣā kathitā puṇyā nāradāya mahātmane kathitā bharata śreṣṭha pṛṣṭena akliṣṭa karmaṇā devarājena ca purā kathā eṣā kathitā śubhā yadā ca mama rāmeṇa yuddham āsīt su dāruṇam pṛcchamānāya tattvena mayā tubhyam viśām pate kathā iyam kathitā puṇyā dharmyā dharma bhṛtām vara a sanna dhīḥ an ākāṅkṣī dharma artha karaṇe nṛpa yama niyama samāhitaḥ vanāntam parigaṇita uñcha śila aśanaḥ praviṣṭaḥ
